\bibbook{the\\\bibtitlemain{book of psalms}}{psalms}{Psalms}{Psa}
\vs Psa 1:1 Blessed \bibemph{is} the man that walketh not in the counsel of the ungodly, nor standeth in the way of sinners, nor sitteth in the seat of the scornful.
\fn{ungodly: or, wicked.}
\vs Psa 1:2 But his delight \bibemph{is} in the law of the \textsc{Lord}; and in his law doth he meditate day and night.
\vs Psa 1:3 And he shall be like a tree planted by the rivers of water, that bringeth forth his fruit in his season; his leaf also shall not wither; and whatsoever he doeth shall prosper.
\fn{wither: Heb. fade.}
\vs Psa 1:4 The ungodly \bibemph{are} not so: but \bibemph{are} like the chaff which the wind driveth away.
\vs Psa 1:5 Therefore the ungodly shall not stand in the judgment, nor sinners in the congregation of the righteous.
\vs Psa 1:6 For the \textsc{Lord} knoweth the way of the righteous: but the way of the ungodly shall perish.
\vs Psa 2:1 Why do the heathen rage, and the people imagine a vain thing?
\fn{rage: or, tumultuously assemble. imagine: Heb. meditate.}
\vs Psa 2:2 The kings of the earth set themselves, and the rulers take counsel together, against the \textsc{Lord}, and against his anointed, \bibemph{saying},
\vs Psa 2:3 Let us break their bands asunder, and cast away their cords from us.
\vs Psa 2:4 He that sitteth in the heavens shall laugh: the Lord shall have them in derision.
\vs Psa 2:5 Then shall he speak unto them in his wrath, and vex them in his sore displeasure.
\fn{vex: or, trouble.}
\vs Psa 2:6 Yet have I set my king upon my holy hill of Zion.
\fn{set: Heb. anointed. upon...: Heb. upon Zion, the hill of my holiness.}
\vs Psa 2:7 I will declare the decree: the \textsc{Lord} hath said unto me, Thou \bibemph{art} my Son; this day have I begotten thee.
\fn{the decree: or, for a decree.}
\vs Psa 2:8 Ask of me, and I shall give \bibemph{thee} the heathen \bibemph{for} thine inheritance, and the uttermost parts of the earth \bibemph{for} thy possession.
\vs Psa 2:9 Thou shalt break them with a rod of iron; thou shalt dash them in pieces like a potter's vessel.
\vs Psa 2:10 Be wise now therefore, O ye kings: be instructed, ye judges of the earth.
\vs Psa 2:11 Serve the \textsc{Lord} with fear, and rejoice with trembling.
\vs Psa 2:12 Kiss the Son, lest he be angry, and ye perish \bibemph{from} the way, when his wrath is kindled but a little. Blessed \bibemph{are} all they that put their trust in him.
\vs Psa 3:1 A Psalm of David, when he fled from Absalom his son. \textsc{Lord}, how are they increased that trouble me! many \bibemph{are} they that rise up against me.
\vs Psa 3:2 Many \bibemph{there be} which say of my soul, \bibemph{There is} no help for him in God. Selah.
\vs Psa 3:3 But thou, O \textsc{Lord}, \bibemph{art} a shield for me; my glory, and the lifter up of mine head.
\fn{for: or, about.}
\vs Psa 3:4 I cried unto the \textsc{Lord} with my voice, and he heard me out of his holy hill. Selah.
\vs Psa 3:5 I laid me down and slept; I awaked; for the \textsc{Lord} sustained me.
\vs Psa 3:6 I will not be afraid of ten thousands of people, that have set \bibemph{themselves} against me round about.
\vs Psa 3:7 Arise, O \textsc{Lord}; save me, O my God: for thou hast smitten all mine enemies \bibemph{upon} the cheek bone; thou hast broken the teeth of the ungodly.
\vs Psa 3:8 Salvation \bibemph{belongeth} unto the \textsc{Lord}: thy blessing \bibemph{is} upon thy people. Selah.
\vs Psa 4:1 To the chief Musician on Neginoth, A Psalm of David. Hear me when I call, O God of my righteousness: thou hast enlarged me \bibemph{when I was} in distress; have mercy upon me, and hear my prayer.
\fn{chief...: or, overseer. have...: or, be gracious unto me.}
\vs Psa 4:2 O ye sons of men, how long \bibemph{will ye turn} my glory into shame? \bibemph{how long} will ye love vanity, \bibemph{and} seek after leasing? Selah.
\vs Psa 4:3 But know that the \textsc{Lord} hath set apart him that is godly for himself: the \textsc{Lord} will hear when I call unto him.
\vs Psa 4:4 Stand in awe, and sin not: commune with your own heart upon your bed, and be still. Selah.
\vs Psa 4:5 Offer the sacrifices of righteousness, and put your trust in the \textsc{Lord}.
\vs Psa 4:6 \bibemph{There be} many that say, Who will shew us \bibemph{any} good? \textsc{Lord}, lift thou up the light of thy countenance upon us.
\vs Psa 4:7 Thou hast put gladness in my heart, more than in the time \bibemph{that} their corn and their wine increased.
\vs Psa 4:8 I will both lay me down in peace, and sleep: for thou, \textsc{Lord}, only makest me dwell in safety.
\vs Psa 5:1 To the chief Musician upon Nehiloth, A Psalm of David. Give ear to my words, O \textsc{Lord}, consider my meditation.
\vs Psa 5:2 Hearken unto the voice of my cry, my King, and my God: for unto thee will I pray.
\vs Psa 5:3 My voice shalt thou hear in the morning, O \textsc{Lord}; in the morning will I direct \bibemph{my prayer} unto thee, and will look up.
\vs Psa 5:4 For thou \bibemph{art} not a God that hath pleasure in wickedness: neither shall evil dwell with thee.
\vs Psa 5:5 The foolish shall not stand in thy sight: thou hatest all workers of iniquity.
\fn{in...: Heb. before thine eyes.}
\vs Psa 5:6 Thou shalt destroy them that speak leasing: the \textsc{Lord} will abhor the bloody and deceitful man.
\fn{bloody...: Heb. man of bloods and deceit.}
\vs Psa 5:7 But as for me, I will come \bibemph{into} thy house in the multitude of thy mercy: \bibemph{and} in thy fear will I worship toward thy holy temple.
\fn{thy holy...: Heb. the temple of thy holiness.}
\vs Psa 5:8 Lead me, O \textsc{Lord}, in thy righteousness because of mine enemies; make thy way straight before my face.
\fn{mine...: Heb. those which observe me.}
\vs Psa 5:9 For \bibemph{there is} no faithfulness in their mouth; their inward part \bibemph{is} very wickedness; their throat \bibemph{is} an open sepulchre; they flatter with their tongue.
\fn{faithfulness: or, stedfastness. very...: Heb. wickednesses. their mouth: Heb. his mouth, that is, the mouth of any of them.}
\vs Psa 5:10 Destroy thou them, O God; let them fall by their own counsels; cast them out in the multitude of their transgressions; for they have rebelled against thee.
\fn{Destroy...: or, Make them guilty. by...: or, from their counsels.}
\vs Psa 5:11 But let all those that put their trust in thee rejoice: let them ever shout for joy, because thou defendest them: let them also that love thy name be joyful in thee.
\fn{defendest...: Heb. coverest over, or, protectest them.}
\vs Psa 5:12 For thou, \textsc{Lord}, wilt bless the righteous; with favour wilt thou compass him as \bibemph{with} a shield.
\fn{compass: Heb. crown.}
\vs Psa 6:1 To the chief Musician on Neginoth upon Sheminith, A Psalm of David. O \textsc{Lord}, rebuke me not in thine anger, neither chasten me in thy hot displeasure.
\fn{Sheminith: or, the eighth.}
\vs Psa 6:2 Have mercy upon me, O \textsc{Lord}; for I \bibemph{am} weak: O \textsc{Lord}, heal me; for my bones are vexed.
\vs Psa 6:3 My soul is also sore vexed: but thou, O \textsc{Lord}, how long?
\vs Psa 6:4 Return, O \textsc{Lord}, deliver my soul: oh save me for thy mercies' sake.
\vs Psa 6:5 For in death \bibemph{there is} no remembrance of thee: in the grave who shall give thee thanks?
\vs Psa 6:6 I am weary with my groaning; all the night make I my bed to swim; I water my couch with my tears.
\fn{all...: or, every night.}
\vs Psa 6:7 Mine eye is consumed because of grief; it waxeth old because of all mine enemies.
\vs Psa 6:8 Depart from me, all ye workers of iniquity; for the \textsc{Lord} hath heard the voice of my weeping.
\vs Psa 6:9 The \textsc{Lord} hath heard my supplication; the \textsc{Lord} will receive my prayer.
\vs Psa 6:10 Let all mine enemies be ashamed and sore vexed: let them return \bibemph{and} be ashamed suddenly.
\vs Psa 7:1 Shiggaion of David, which he sang unto the \textsc{Lord}, concerning the words of Cush the Benjamite. O \textsc{Lord} my God, in thee do I put my trust: save me from all them that persecute me, and deliver me:
\fn{words: or, business.}
\vs Psa 7:2 Lest he tear my soul like a lion, rending \bibemph{it} in pieces, while \bibemph{there is} none to deliver.
\fn{none...: Heb. not a deliverer.}
\vs Psa 7:3 O \textsc{Lord} my God, if I have done this; if there be iniquity in my hands;
\vs Psa 7:4 If I have rewarded evil unto him that was at peace with me; (yea, I have delivered him that without cause is mine enemy:)
\vs Psa 7:5 Let the enemy persecute my soul, and take \bibemph{it}; yea, let him tread down my life upon the earth, and lay mine honour in the dust. Selah.
\vs Psa 7:6 Arise, O \textsc{Lord}, in thine anger, lift up thyself because of the rage of mine enemies: and awake for me \bibemph{to} the judgment \bibemph{that} thou hast commanded.
\vs Psa 7:7 So shall the congregation of the people compass thee about: for their sakes therefore return thou on high.
\vs Psa 7:8 The \textsc{Lord} shall judge the people: judge me, O \textsc{Lord}, according to my righteousness, and according to mine integrity \bibemph{that is} in me.
\vs Psa 7:9 Oh let the wickedness of the wicked come to an end; but establish the just: for the righteous God trieth the hearts and reins.
\vs Psa 7:10 My defence \bibemph{is} of God, which saveth the upright in heart.
\fn{My...: Heb. My buckler is upon God.}
\vs Psa 7:11 God judgeth the righteous, and God is angry \bibemph{with the wicked} every day.
\fn{judgeth...: or, is a righteous judge.}
\vs Psa 7:12 If he turn not, he will whet his sword; he hath bent his bow, and made it ready.
\vs Psa 7:13 He hath also prepared for him the instruments of death; he ordaineth his arrows against the persecutors.
\vs Psa 7:14 Behold, he travaileth with iniquity, and hath conceived mischief, and brought forth falsehood.
\vs Psa 7:15 He made a pit, and digged it, and is fallen into the ditch \bibemph{which} he made.
\fn{He made a pit: Heb. He hath digged a pit.}
\vs Psa 7:16 His mischief shall return upon his own head, and his violent dealing shall come down upon his own pate.
\vs Psa 7:17 I will praise the \textsc{Lord} according to his righteousness: and will sing praise to the name of the \textsc{Lord} most high.
\vs Psa 8:1 To the chief Musician upon Gittith, A Psalm of David. O \textsc{Lord} our Lord, how excellent \bibemph{is} thy name in all the earth! who hast set thy glory above the heavens.
\vs Psa 8:2 Out of the mouth of babes and sucklings hast thou ordained strength because of thine enemies, that thou mightest still the enemy and the avenger.
\fn{ordained: Heb. founded.}
\vs Psa 8:3 When I consider thy heavens, the work of thy fingers, the moon and the stars, which thou hast ordained;
\vs Psa 8:4 What is man, that thou art mindful of him? and the son of man, that thou visitest him?
\vs Psa 8:5 For thou hast made him a little lower than the angels, and hast crowned him with glory and honour.
\vs Psa 8:6 Thou madest him to have dominion over the works of thy hands; thou hast put all \bibemph{things} under his feet:
\vs Psa 8:7 All sheep and oxen, yea, and the beasts of the field;
\fn{All...: Heb. Flocks and oxen all of them.}
\vs Psa 8:8 The fowl of the air, and the fish of the sea, \bibemph{and whatsoever} passeth through the paths of the seas.
\vs Psa 8:9 O \textsc{Lord} our Lord, how excellent \bibemph{is} thy name in all the earth!
\vs Psa 9:1 To the chief Musician upon Muthlabben, A Psalm of David. I will praise \bibemph{thee}, O \textsc{Lord}, with my whole heart; I will shew forth all thy marvellous works.
\vs Psa 9:2 I will be glad and rejoice in thee: I will sing praise to thy name, O thou most High.
\vs Psa 9:3 When mine enemies are turned back, they shall fall and perish at thy presence.
\vs Psa 9:4 For thou hast maintained my right and my cause; thou satest in the throne judging right.
\fn{maintained...: Heb. made my judgment. judging right: Heb. judging in righteousness.}
\vs Psa 9:5 Thou hast rebuked the heathen, thou hast destroyed the wicked, thou hast put out their name for ever and ever.
\vs Psa 9:6 O thou enemy, destructions are come to a perpetual end: and thou hast destroyed cities; their memorial is perished with them.
\fn{O thou...: or, The destructions of the enemy are come to a perpetual end: and their cities hast thou destroyed, etc.}
\vs Psa 9:7 But the \textsc{Lord} shall endure for ever: he hath prepared his throne for judgment.
\vs Psa 9:8 And he shall judge the world in righteousness, he shall minister judgment to the people in uprightness.
\vs Psa 9:9 The \textsc{Lord} also will be a refuge for the oppressed, a refuge in times of trouble.
\fn{a refuge: Heb. an high place.}
\vs Psa 9:10 And they that know thy name will put their trust in thee: for thou, \textsc{Lord}, hast not forsaken them that seek thee.
\vs Psa 9:11 Sing praises to the \textsc{Lord}, which dwelleth in Zion: declare among the people his doings.
\vs Psa 9:12 When he maketh inquisition for blood, he remembereth them: he forgetteth not the cry of the humble.
\fn{humble: or, afflicted.}
\vs Psa 9:13 Have mercy upon me, O \textsc{Lord}; consider my trouble \bibemph{which I suffer} of them that hate me, thou that liftest me up from the gates of death:
\vs Psa 9:14 That I may shew forth all thy praise in the gates of the daughter of Zion: I will rejoice in thy salvation.
\vs Psa 9:15 The heathen are sunk down in the pit \bibemph{that} they made: in the net which they hid is their own foot taken.
\vs Psa 9:16 The \textsc{Lord} is known \bibemph{by} the judgment \bibemph{which} he executeth: the wicked is snared in the work of his own hands. Higgaion. Selah.
\fn{Higgaion: that is, Meditation.}
\vs Psa 9:17 The wicked shall be turned into hell, \bibemph{and} all the nations that forget God.
\vs Psa 9:18 For the needy shall not alway be forgotten: the expectation of the poor shall \bibemph{not} perish for ever.
\vs Psa 9:19 Arise, O \textsc{Lord}; let not man prevail: let the heathen be judged in thy sight.
\vs Psa 9:20 Put them in fear, O \textsc{Lord}: \bibemph{that} the nations may know themselves \bibemph{to be but} men. Selah.
\vs Psa 10:1 Why standest thou afar off, O \textsc{Lord}? \bibemph{why} hidest thou \bibemph{thyself} in times of trouble?
\vs Psa 10:2 The wicked in \bibemph{his} pride doth persecute the poor: let them be taken in the devices that they have imagined.
\fn{The wicked...: Heb. In the pride of the wicked he doth persecute.}
\vs Psa 10:3 For the wicked boasteth of his heart's desire, and blesseth the covetous, \bibemph{whom} the \textsc{Lord} abhorreth.
\fn{heart's: Heb. soul's. blesseth...: or, the covetous blesseth himself, he abhorreth the \textsc{Lord}.}
\vs Psa 10:4 The wicked, through the pride of his countenance, will not seek \bibemph{after God}: God \bibemph{is} not in all his thoughts.
\fn{God is...: or, all his thoughts are, There is no God.}
\vs Psa 10:5 His ways are always grievous; thy judgments \bibemph{are} far above out of his sight: \bibemph{as for} all his enemies, he puffeth at them.
\vs Psa 10:6 He hath said in his heart, I shall not be moved: for \bibemph{I shall} never \bibemph{be} in adversity.
\fn{never: Heb. unto generation and generation.}
\vs Psa 10:7 His mouth is full of cursing and deceit and fraud: under his tongue \bibemph{is} mischief and vanity.
\fn{deceit: Heb. deceits. vanity: or, iniquity.}
\vs Psa 10:8 He sitteth in the lurking places of the villages: in the secret places doth he murder the innocent: his eyes are privily set against the poor.
\fn{are...: Heb. hide themselves.}
\vs Psa 10:9 He lieth in wait secretly as a lion in his den: he lieth in wait to catch the poor: he doth catch the poor, when he draweth him into his net.
\fn{secretly: Heb. in the secret places.}
\vs Psa 10:10 He croucheth, \bibemph{and} humbleth himself, that the poor may fall by his strong ones.
\fn{He...: Heb. He breaketh himself. by...: or, into his strong parts.}
\vs Psa 10:11 He hath said in his heart, God hath forgotten: he hideth his face; he will never see \bibemph{it}.
\vs Psa 10:12 Arise, O \textsc{Lord}; O God, lift up thine hand: forget not the humble.
\fn{humble: or, afflicted.}
\vs Psa 10:13 Wherefore doth the wicked contemn God? he hath said in his heart, Thou wilt not require \bibemph{it}.
\vs Psa 10:14 Thou hast seen \bibemph{it}; for thou beholdest mischief and spite, to requite \bibemph{it} with thy hand: the poor committeth himself unto thee; thou art the helper of the fatherless.
\fn{committeth: Heb. leaveth.}
\vs Psa 10:15 Break thou the arm of the wicked and the evil \bibemph{man}: seek out his wickedness \bibemph{till} thou find none.
\vs Psa 10:16 The \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} King for ever and ever: the heathen are perished out of his land.
\vs Psa 10:17 \textsc{Lord}, thou hast heard the desire of the humble: thou wilt prepare their heart, thou wilt cause thine ear to hear:
\fn{prepare: or, establish.}
\vs Psa 10:18 To judge the fatherless and the oppressed, that the man of the earth may no more oppress.
\fn{oppress: or, terrify.}
\vs Psa 11:1 To the chief Musician, \bibemph{A Psalm} of David. In the \textsc{Lord} put I my trust: how say ye to my soul, Flee \bibemph{as} a bird to your mountain?
\vs Psa 11:2 For, lo, the wicked bend \bibemph{their} bow, they make ready their arrow upon the string, that they may privily shoot at the upright in heart.
\fn{privily: Heb. in darkness.}
\vs Psa 11:3 If the foundations be destroyed, what can the righteous do?
\vs Psa 11:4 The \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} in his holy temple, the \textsc{Lord's} throne \bibemph{is} in heaven: his eyes behold, his eyelids try, the children of men.
\vs Psa 11:5 The \textsc{Lord} trieth the righteous: but the wicked and him that loveth violence his soul hateth.
\vs Psa 11:6 Upon the wicked he shall rain snares, fire and brimstone, and an horrible tempest: \bibemph{this shall be} the portion of their cup.
\fn{an horrible...: or, a burning tempest.}
\vs Psa 11:7 For the righteous \textsc{Lord} loveth righteousness; his countenance doth behold the upright.
\vs Psa 12:1 To the chief Musician upon Sheminith, A Psalm of David. Help, \textsc{Lord}; for the godly man ceaseth; for the faithful fail from among the children of men.
\fn{upon...: or, upon the eighth. Help: or, Save.}
\vs Psa 12:2 They speak vanity every one with his neighbour: \bibemph{with} flattering lips \bibemph{and} with a double heart do they speak.
\fn{a double...: Heb. an heart and an heart.}
\vs Psa 12:3 The \textsc{Lord} shall cut off all flattering lips, \bibemph{and} the tongue that speaketh proud things:
\fn{proud: Heb. great.}
\vs Psa 12:4 Who have said, With our tongue will we prevail; our lips \bibemph{are} our own: who \bibemph{is} lord over us?
\fn{are...: Heb. are with us.}
\vs Psa 12:5 For the oppression of the poor, for the sighing of the needy, now will I arise, saith the \textsc{Lord}; I will set \bibemph{him} in safety \bibemph{from him that} puffeth at him.
\fn{puffeth...: or, would ensnare him.}
\vs Psa 12:6 The words of the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{are} pure words: \bibemph{as} silver tried in a furnace of earth, purified seven times.
\vs Psa 12:7 Thou shalt keep them, O \textsc{Lord}, thou shalt preserve them from this generation for ever.
\fn{them from: Heb. him, etc: that is, every one of them, etc.}
\vs Psa 12:8 The wicked walk on every side, when the vilest men are exalted.
\fn{men: Heb. of the sons of the men.}
\vs Psa 13:1 To the chief Musician, A Psalm of David. How long wilt thou forget me, O \textsc{Lord}? for ever? how long wilt thou hide thy face from me?
\fn{chief...: or, overseer.}
\vs Psa 13:2 How long shall I take counsel in my soul, \bibemph{having} sorrow in my heart daily? how long shall mine enemy be exalted over me?
\vs Psa 13:3 Consider \bibemph{and} hear me, O \textsc{Lord} my God: lighten mine eyes, lest I sleep the \bibemph{sleep of} death;
\vs Psa 13:4 Lest mine enemy say, I have prevailed against him; \bibemph{and} those that trouble me rejoice when I am moved.
\vs Psa 13:5 But I have trusted in thy mercy; my heart shall rejoice in thy salvation.
\vs Psa 13:6 I will sing unto the \textsc{Lord}, because he hath dealt bountifully with me.
\vs Psa 14:1 To the chief Musician, \bibemph{A Psalm} of David. The fool hath said in his heart, \bibemph{There is} no God. They are corrupt, they have done abominable works, \bibemph{there is} none that doeth good.
\vs Psa 14:2 The \textsc{Lord} looked down from heaven upon the children of men, to see if there were any that did understand, \bibemph{and} seek God.
\vs Psa 14:3 They are all gone aside, they are \bibemph{all} together become filthy: \bibemph{there is} none that doeth good, no, not one.
\fn{filthy: Heb. stinking.}
\vs Psa 14:4 Have all the workers of iniquity no knowledge? who eat up my people \bibemph{as} they eat bread, and call not upon the \textsc{Lord}.
\vs Psa 14:5 There were they in great fear: for God \bibemph{is} in the generation of the righteous.
\fn{were...: Heb. they feared a fear.}
\vs Psa 14:6 Ye have shamed the counsel of the poor, because the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} his refuge.
\vs Psa 14:7 Oh that the salvation of Israel \bibemph{were come} out of Zion! when the \textsc{Lord} bringeth back the captivity of his people, Jacob shall rejoice, \bibemph{and} Israel shall be glad.
\fn{Oh...: Heb. Who will give.}
\vs Psa 15:1 A Psalm of David. \textsc{Lord}, who shall abide in thy tabernacle? who shall dwell in thy holy hill?
\fn{abide: Heb. sojourn.}
\vs Psa 15:2 He that walketh uprightly, and worketh righteousness, and speaketh the truth in his heart.
\vs Psa 15:3 \bibemph{He that} backbiteth not with his tongue, nor doeth evil to his neighbour, nor taketh up a reproach against his neighbour.
\fn{taketh...: or, receiveth, or, endureth.}
\vs Psa 15:4 In whose eyes a vile person is contemned; but he honoureth them that fear the \textsc{Lord}. \bibemph{He that} sweareth to \bibemph{his own} hurt, and changeth not.
\vs Psa 15:5 \bibemph{He that} putteth not out his money to usury, nor taketh reward against the innocent. He that doeth these \bibemph{things} shall never be moved.
\vs Psa 16:1 Michtam of David. Preserve me, O God: for in thee do I put my trust.
\fn{Michtam: or, A golden Psalm.}
\vs Psa 16:2 \bibemph{O my soul}, thou hast said unto the \textsc{Lord}, Thou \bibemph{art} my Lord: my goodness \bibemph{extendeth} not to thee;
\vs Psa 16:3 \bibemph{But} to the saints that \bibemph{are} in the earth, and \bibemph{to} the excellent, in whom \bibemph{is} all my delight.
\vs Psa 16:4 Their sorrows shall be multiplied \bibemph{that} hasten \bibemph{after} another \bibemph{god}: their drink offerings of blood will I not offer, nor take up their names into my lips.
\fn{hasten...: or, give gifts to another.}
\vs Psa 16:5 The \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} the portion of mine inheritance and of my cup: thou maintainest my lot.
\fn{of mine...: Heb. of my part.}
\vs Psa 16:6 The lines are fallen unto me in pleasant \bibemph{places}; yea, I have a goodly heritage.
\vs Psa 16:7 I will bless the \textsc{Lord}, who hath given me counsel: my reins also instruct me in the night seasons.
\vs Psa 16:8 I have set the \textsc{Lord} always before me: because \bibemph{he is} at my right hand, I shall not be moved.
\vs Psa 16:9 Therefore my heart is glad, and my glory rejoiceth: my flesh also shall rest in hope.
\fn{rest...: Heb. dwell confidently.}
\vs Psa 16:10 For thou wilt not leave my soul in hell; neither wilt thou suffer thine Holy One to see corruption.
\vs Psa 16:11 Thou wilt shew me the path of life: in thy presence \bibemph{is} fulness of joy; at thy right hand \bibemph{there are} pleasures for evermore.
\vs Psa 17:1 A Prayer of David. Hear the right, O \textsc{Lord}, attend unto my cry, give ear unto my prayer, \bibemph{that goeth} not out of feigned lips.
\fn{the right: Heb. justice. not...: Heb. without lips of deceit.}
\vs Psa 17:2 Let my sentence come forth from thy presence; let thine eyes behold the things that are equal.
\vs Psa 17:3 Thou hast proved mine heart; thou hast visited \bibemph{me} in the night; thou hast tried me, \bibemph{and} shalt find nothing; I am purposed \bibemph{that} my mouth shall not transgress.
\vs Psa 17:4 Concerning the works of men, by the word of thy lips I have kept \bibemph{me from} the paths of the destroyer.
\vs Psa 17:5 Hold up my goings in thy paths, \bibemph{that} my footsteps slip not.
\fn{slip...: Heb. be not moved.}
\vs Psa 17:6 I have called upon thee, for thou wilt hear me, O God: incline thine ear unto me, \bibemph{and hear} my speech.
\vs Psa 17:7 Shew thy marvellous lovingkindness, O thou that savest by thy right hand them which put their trust \bibemph{in thee} from those that rise up \bibemph{against them}.
\fn{by thy...: or, them which trust in thee from those that rise up against thy right hand.}
\vs Psa 17:8 Keep me as the apple of the eye, hide me under the shadow of thy wings,
\vs Psa 17:9 From the wicked that oppress me, \bibemph{from} my deadly enemies, \bibemph{who} compass me about.
\fn{oppress: Heb. waste. my...: Heb. my enemies against the soul.}
\vs Psa 17:10 They are inclosed in their own fat: with their mouth they speak proudly.
\vs Psa 17:11 They have now compassed us in our steps: they have set their eyes bowing down to the earth;
\vs Psa 17:12 Like as a lion \bibemph{that} is greedy of his prey, and as it were a young lion lurking in secret places.
\fn{Like...: Heb. The likeness of him (that is, of every one of them) is as a lion that desireth to ravin. lurking: Heb. sitting.}
\vs Psa 17:13 Arise, O \textsc{Lord}, disappoint him, cast him down: deliver my soul from the wicked, \bibemph{which is} thy sword:
\fn{disappoint...: Heb. prevent his face. which is: or, by.}
\vs Psa 17:14 From men \bibemph{which are} thy hand, O \textsc{Lord}, from men of the world, \bibemph{which have} their portion in \bibemph{this} life, and whose belly thou fillest with thy hid \bibemph{treasure}: they are full of children, and leave the rest of their \bibemph{substance} to their babes.
\fn{which are: or, by. they...: or, their children are full.}
\vs Psa 17:15 As for me, I will behold thy face in righteousness: I shall be satisfied, when I awake, with thy likeness.
\vs Psa 18:1 To the chief Musician, \bibemph{A Psalm} of David, the servant of the \textsc{Lord}, who spake unto the \textsc{Lord} the words of this song in the day \bibemph{that} the \textsc{Lord} delivered him from the hand of all his enemies, and from the hand of Saul: And he said, I will love thee, O \textsc{Lord}, my strength.
\vs Psa 18:2 The \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} my rock, and my fortress, and my deliverer; my God, my strength, in whom I will trust; my buckler, and the horn of my salvation, \bibemph{and} my high tower.
\fn{my strength: Heb. my rock.}
\vs Psa 18:3 I will call upon the \textsc{Lord}, \bibemph{who is worthy} to be praised: so shall I be saved from mine enemies.
\vs Psa 18:4 The sorrows of death compassed me, and the floods of ungodly men made me afraid.
\fn{ungodly men: Heb. Belial.}
\vs Psa 18:5 The sorrows of hell compassed me about: the snares of death prevented me.
\fn{sorrows: or, cords.}
\vs Psa 18:6 In my distress I called upon the \textsc{Lord}, and cried unto my God: he heard my voice out of his temple, and my cry came before him, \bibemph{even} into his ears.
\vs Psa 18:7 Then the earth shook and trembled; the foundations also of the hills moved and were shaken, because he was wroth.
\vs Psa 18:8 There went up a smoke out of his nostrils, and fire out of his mouth devoured: coals were kindled by it.
\fn{out of his nostrils: Heb. by his, etc.}
\vs Psa 18:9 He bowed the heavens also, and came down: and darkness \bibemph{was} under his feet.
\vs Psa 18:10 And he rode upon a cherub, and did fly: yea, he did fly upon the wings of the wind.
\vs Psa 18:11 He made darkness his secret place; his pavilion round about him \bibemph{were} dark waters \bibemph{and} thick clouds of the skies.
\vs Psa 18:12 At the brightness \bibemph{that was} before him his thick clouds passed, hail \bibemph{stones} and coals of fire.
\vs Psa 18:13 The \textsc{Lord} also thundered in the heavens, and the Highest gave his voice; hail \bibemph{stones} and coals of fire.
\vs Psa 18:14 Yea, he sent out his arrows, and scattered them; and he shot out lightnings, and discomfited them.
\vs Psa 18:15 Then the channels of waters were seen, and the foundations of the world were discovered at thy rebuke, O \textsc{Lord}, at the blast of the breath of thy nostrils.
\vs Psa 18:16 He sent from above, he took me, he drew me out of many waters.
\fn{many: or, great.}
\vs Psa 18:17 He delivered me from my strong enemy, and from them which hated me: for they were too strong for me.
\vs Psa 18:18 They prevented me in the day of my calamity: but the \textsc{Lord} was my stay.
\vs Psa 18:19 He brought me forth also into a large place; he delivered me, because he delighted in me.
\vs Psa 18:20 The \textsc{Lord} rewarded me according to my righteousness; according to the cleanness of my hands hath he recompensed me.
\vs Psa 18:21 For I have kept the ways of the \textsc{Lord}, and have not wickedly departed from my God.
\vs Psa 18:22 For all his judgments \bibemph{were} before me, and I did not put away his statutes from me.
\vs Psa 18:23 I was also upright before him, and I kept myself from mine iniquity.
\fn{before: Heb. with.}
\vs Psa 18:24 Therefore hath the \textsc{Lord} recompensed me according to my righteousness, according to the cleanness of my hands in his eyesight.
\fn{in...: Heb. before his eyes.}
\vs Psa 18:25 With the merciful thou wilt shew thyself merciful; with an upright man thou wilt shew thyself upright;
\vs Psa 18:26 With the pure thou wilt shew thyself pure; and with the froward thou wilt shew thyself froward.
\fn{shew thyself froward: or, wrestle.}
\vs Psa 18:27 For thou wilt save the afflicted people; but wilt bring down high looks.
\vs Psa 18:28 For thou wilt light my candle: the \textsc{Lord} my God will enlighten my darkness.
\fn{candle: or, lamp.}
\vs Psa 18:29 For by thee I have run through a troop; and by my God have I leaped over a wall.
\fn{run...: or, broken.}
\vs Psa 18:30 \bibemph{As for} God, his way \bibemph{is} perfect: the word of the \textsc{Lord} is tried: he \bibemph{is} a buckler to all those that trust in him.
\fn{tried: or, refined.}
\vs Psa 18:31 For who \bibemph{is} God save the \textsc{Lord}? or who \bibemph{is} a rock save our God?
\vs Psa 18:32 \bibemph{It is} God that girdeth me with strength, and maketh my way perfect.
\vs Psa 18:33 He maketh my feet like hinds' \bibemph{feet}, and setteth me upon my high places.
\vs Psa 18:34 He teacheth my hands to war, so that a bow of steel is broken by mine arms.
\vs Psa 18:35 Thou hast also given me the shield of thy salvation: and thy right hand hath holden me up, and thy gentleness hath made me great.
\fn{thy gentleness...: or, with thy meekness thou hast multiplied me.}
\vs Psa 18:36 Thou hast enlarged my steps under me, that my feet did not slip.
\fn{my feet: Heb. mine ankles.}
\vs Psa 18:37 I have pursued mine enemies, and overtaken them: neither did I turn again till they were consumed.
\vs Psa 18:38 I have wounded them that they were not able to rise: they are fallen under my feet.
\vs Psa 18:39 For thou hast girded me with strength unto the battle: thou hast subdued under me those that rose up against me.
\fn{subdued: Heb. caused to bow.}
\vs Psa 18:40 Thou hast also given me the necks of mine enemies; that I might destroy them that hate me.
\vs Psa 18:41 They cried, but \bibemph{there was} none to save \bibemph{them: even} unto the \textsc{Lord}, but he answered them not.
\vs Psa 18:42 Then did I beat them small as the dust before the wind: I did cast them out as the dirt in the streets.
\vs Psa 18:43 Thou hast delivered me from the strivings of the people; \bibemph{and} thou hast made me the head of the heathen: a people \bibemph{whom} I have not known shall serve me.
\vs Psa 18:44 As soon as they hear of me, they shall obey me: the strangers shall submit themselves unto me.
\fn{As soon...: Heb. At the hearing of the ear. submit...: or, yield feigned obedience. strangers: Heb. sons of the stranger.}
\vs Psa 18:45 The strangers shall fade away, and be afraid out of their close places.
\fn{strangers: Heb. sons of the stranger.}
\vs Psa 18:46 The \textsc{Lord} liveth; and blessed \bibemph{be} my rock; and let the God of my salvation be exalted.
\vs Psa 18:47 \bibemph{It is} God that avengeth me, and subdueth the people under me.
\fn{avengeth: Heb. giveth avengements for. subdueth: or, destroyeth.}
\vs Psa 18:48 He delivereth me from mine enemies: yea, thou liftest me up above those that rise up against me: thou hast delivered me from the violent man.
\fn{violent...: Heb. man of violence.}
\vs Psa 18:49 Therefore will I give thanks unto thee, O \textsc{Lord}, among the heathen, and sing praises unto thy name.
\fn{give...: or, confess.}
\vs Psa 18:50 Great deliverance giveth he to his king; and sheweth mercy to his anointed, to David, and to his seed for evermore.
\vs Psa 19:1 To the chief Musician, A Psalm of David. The heavens declare the glory of God; and the firmament sheweth his handywork.
\vs Psa 19:2 Day unto day uttereth speech, and night unto night sheweth knowledge.
\vs Psa 19:3 \bibemph{There is} no speech nor language, \bibemph{where} their voice is not heard.
\fn{where...: or, without these their voice is heard: Heb. without their voice heard.}
\vs Psa 19:4 Their line is gone out through all the earth, and their words to the end of the world. In them hath he set a tabernacle for the sun,
\fn{line: or, rule, or, direction.}
\vs Psa 19:5 Which \bibemph{is} as a bridegroom coming out of his chamber, \bibemph{and} rejoiceth as a strong man to run a race.
\vs Psa 19:6 His going forth \bibemph{is} from the end of the heaven, and his circuit unto the ends of it: and there is nothing hid from the heat thereof.
\vs Psa 19:7 The law of the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} perfect, converting the soul: the testimony of the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} sure, making wise the simple.
\fn{law: or, doctrine. converting: or, restoring.}
\vs Psa 19:8 The statutes of the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{are} right, rejoicing the heart: the commandment of the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} pure, enlightening the eyes.
\vs Psa 19:9 The fear of the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} clean, enduring for ever: the judgments of the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{are} true \bibemph{and} righteous altogether.
\fn{true: Heb. truth.}
\vs Psa 19:10 More to be desired \bibemph{are they} than gold, yea, than much fine gold: sweeter also than honey and the honeycomb.
\fn{the honeycomb: Heb. the dropping of honeycomb.}
\vs Psa 19:11 Moreover by them is thy servant warned: \bibemph{and} in keeping of them \bibemph{there is} great reward.
\vs Psa 19:12 Who can understand \bibemph{his} errors? cleanse thou me from secret \bibemph{faults}.
\vs Psa 19:13 Keep back thy servant also from presumptuous \bibemph{sins}; let them not have dominion over me: then shall I be upright, and I shall be innocent from the great transgression.
\fn{the great: or, much.}
\vs Psa 19:14 Let the words of my mouth, and the meditation of my heart, be acceptable in thy sight, O \textsc{Lord}, my strength, and my redeemer.
\fn{strength: Heb. rock.}
\vs Psa 20:1 To the chief Musician, A Psalm of David. The \textsc{Lord} hear thee in the day of trouble; the name of the God of Jacob defend thee;
\fn{defend...: Heb. set thee on an high place.}
\vs Psa 20:2 Send thee help from the sanctuary, and strengthen thee out of Zion;
\fn{thee help: Heb. thy help. strengthen: Heb. support.}
\vs Psa 20:3 Remember all thy offerings, and accept thy burnt sacrifice; Selah.
\fn{accept: Heb. turn to ashes: or, make fat.}
\vs Psa 20:4 Grant thee according to thine own heart, and fulfil all thy counsel.
\vs Psa 20:5 We will rejoice in thy salvation, and in the name of our God we will set up \bibemph{our} banners: the \textsc{Lord} fulfil all thy petitions.
\vs Psa 20:6 Now know I that the \textsc{Lord} saveth his anointed; he will hear him from his holy heaven with the saving strength of his right hand.
\fn{his holy...: Heb. the heaven of his holiness. with...: Heb. by the strength of the salvation of.}
\vs Psa 20:7 Some \bibemph{trust} in chariots, and some in horses: but we will remember the name of the \textsc{Lord} our God.
\vs Psa 20:8 They are brought down and fallen: but we are risen, and stand upright.
\vs Psa 20:9 Save, \textsc{Lord}: let the king hear us when we call.
\vs Psa 21:1 To the chief Musician, A Psalm of David. The king shall joy in thy strength, O \textsc{Lord}; and in thy salvation how greatly shall he rejoice!
\vs Psa 21:2 Thou hast given him his heart's desire, and hast not withholden the request of his lips. Selah.
\vs Psa 21:3 For thou preventest him with the blessings of goodness: thou settest a crown of pure gold on his head.
\vs Psa 21:4 He asked life of thee, \bibemph{and} thou gavest \bibemph{it} him, \bibemph{even} length of days for ever and ever.
\vs Psa 21:5 His glory \bibemph{is} great in thy salvation: honour and majesty hast thou laid upon him.
\vs Psa 21:6 For thou hast made him most blessed for ever: thou hast made him exceeding glad with thy countenance.
\fn{made him most...: Heb. set him to be blessings. made him exceeding...: Heb. make him glad with joy.}
\vs Psa 21:7 For the king trusteth in the \textsc{Lord}, and through the mercy of the most High he shall not be moved.
\vs Psa 21:8 Thine hand shall find out all thine enemies: thy right hand shall find out those that hate thee.
\vs Psa 21:9 Thou shalt make them as a fiery oven in the time of thine anger: the \textsc{Lord} shall swallow them up in his wrath, and the fire shall devour them.
\vs Psa 21:10 Their fruit shalt thou destroy from the earth, and their seed from among the children of men.
\vs Psa 21:11 For they intended evil against thee: they imagined a mischievous device, \bibemph{which} they are not able \bibemph{to perform}.
\vs Psa 21:12 Therefore shalt thou make them turn their back, \bibemph{when} thou shalt make ready \bibemph{thine arrows} upon thy strings against the face of them.
\fn{shalt thou...: or, thou shalt set them as a butt. back: Heb. shoulder.}
\vs Psa 21:13 Be thou exalted, \textsc{Lord}, in thine own strength: \bibemph{so} will we sing and praise thy power.
\vs Psa 22:1 To the chief Musician upon Aijeleth Shahar, A Psalm of David. My God, my God, why hast thou forsaken me? \bibemph{why art thou so} far from helping me, \bibemph{and from} the words of my roaring?
\fn{Aijeleth...: or, the hind of the morning. helping...: Heb. my salvation.}
\vs Psa 22:2 O my God, I cry in the daytime, but thou hearest not; and in the night season, and am not silent.
\fn{am...: Heb. there is no silence to me.}
\vs Psa 22:3 But thou \bibemph{art} holy, \bibemph{O thou} that inhabitest the praises of Israel.
\vs Psa 22:4 Our fathers trusted in thee: they trusted, and thou didst deliver them.
\vs Psa 22:5 They cried unto thee, and were delivered: they trusted in thee, and were not confounded.
\vs Psa 22:6 But I \bibemph{am} a worm, and no man; a reproach of men, and despised of the people.
\vs Psa 22:7 All they that see me laugh me to scorn: they shoot out the lip, they shake the head, \bibemph{saying},
\fn{shoot...: Heb. open.}
\vs Psa 22:8 He trusted on the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{that} he would deliver him: let him deliver him, seeing he delighted in him.
\fn{He trusted...: Heb. He rolled himself on. seeing...: or, if he delight in.}
\vs Psa 22:9 But thou \bibemph{art} he that took me out of the womb: thou didst make me hope \bibemph{when I was} upon my mother's breasts.
\fn{didst...: or, kept me in safety.}
\vs Psa 22:10 I was cast upon thee from the womb: thou \bibemph{art} my God from my mother's belly.
\vs Psa 22:11 Be not far from me; for trouble \bibemph{is} near; for \bibemph{there is} none to help.
\fn{none...: Heb. not a helper.}
\vs Psa 22:12 Many bulls have compassed me: strong \bibemph{bulls} of Bashan have beset me round.
\vs Psa 22:13 They gaped upon me \bibemph{with} their mouths, \bibemph{as} a ravening and a roaring lion.
\fn{gaped...: Heb. opened their mouths against me.}
\vs Psa 22:14 I am poured out like water, and all my bones are out of joint: my heart is like wax; it is melted in the midst of my bowels.
\fn{out of...: or, sundered.}
\vs Psa 22:15 My strength is dried up like a potsherd; and my tongue cleaveth to my jaws; and thou hast brought me into the dust of death.
\vs Psa 22:16 For dogs have compassed me: the assembly of the wicked have inclosed me: they pierced my hands and my feet.
\vs Psa 22:17 I may tell all my bones: they look \bibemph{and} stare upon me.
\vs Psa 22:18 They part my garments among them, and cast lots upon my vesture.
\vs Psa 22:19 But be not thou far from me, O \textsc{Lord}: O my strength, haste thee to help me.
\vs Psa 22:20 Deliver my soul from the sword; my darling from the power of the dog.
\fn{my darling: Heb. my only one. power: Heb. hand.}
\vs Psa 22:21 Save me from the lion's mouth: for thou hast heard me from the horns of the unicorns.
\vs Psa 22:22 I will declare thy name unto my brethren: in the midst of the congregation will I praise thee.
\vs Psa 22:23 Ye that fear the \textsc{Lord}, praise him; all ye the seed of Jacob, glorify him; and fear him, all ye the seed of Israel.
\vs Psa 22:24 For he hath not despised nor abhorred the affliction of the afflicted; neither hath he hid his face from him; but when he cried unto him, he heard.
\vs Psa 22:25 My praise \bibemph{shall be} of thee in the great congregation: I will pay my vows before them that fear him.
\vs Psa 22:26 The meek shall eat and be satisfied: they shall praise the \textsc{Lord} that seek him: your heart shall live for ever.
\vs Psa 22:27 All the ends of the world shall remember and turn unto the \textsc{Lord}: and all the kindreds of the nations shall worship before thee.
\vs Psa 22:28 For the kingdom \bibemph{is} the \textsc{Lord's}: and he \bibemph{is} the governor among the nations.
\vs Psa 22:29 All \bibemph{they that be} fat upon earth shall eat and worship: all they that go down to the dust shall bow before him: and none can keep alive his own soul.
\vs Psa 22:30 A seed shall serve him; it shall be accounted to the Lord for a generation.
\vs Psa 22:31 They shall come, and shall declare his righteousness unto a people that shall be born, that he hath done \bibemph{this}.
\vs Psa 23:1 A Psalm of David. The \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} my shepherd; I shall not want.
\vs Psa 23:2 He maketh me to lie down in green pastures: he leadeth me beside the still waters.
\fn{green...: Heb. pastures of tender grass. still...: Heb. waters of quietness.}
\vs Psa 23:3 He restoreth my soul: he leadeth me in the paths of righteousness for his name's sake.
\vs Psa 23:4 Yea, though I walk through the valley of the shadow of death, I will fear no evil: for thou \bibemph{art} with me; thy rod and thy staff they comfort me.
\vs Psa 23:5 Thou preparest a table before me in the presence of mine enemies: thou anointest my head with oil; my cup runneth over.
\fn{anointest: Heb. makest fat.}
\vs Psa 23:6 Surely goodness and mercy shall follow me all the days of my life: and I will dwell in the house of the \textsc{Lord} for ever.
\fn{for ever: Heb. to length of days.}
\vs Psa 24:1 A Psalm of David. The earth \bibemph{is} the \textsc{Lord's}, and the fulness thereof; the world, and they that dwell therein.
\vs Psa 24:2 For he hath founded it upon the seas, and established it upon the floods.
\vs Psa 24:3 Who shall ascend into the hill of the \textsc{Lord}? or who shall stand in his holy place?
\vs Psa 24:4 He that hath clean hands, and a pure heart; who hath not lifted up his soul unto vanity, nor sworn deceitfully.
\fn{He...: Heb. The clean of hands.}
\vs Psa 24:5 He shall receive the blessing from the \textsc{Lord}, and righteousness from the God of his salvation.
\vs Psa 24:6 This \bibemph{is} the generation of them that seek him, that seek thy face, O Jacob. Selah.
\fn{O Jacob: or, O God of Jacob.}
\vs Psa 24:7 Lift up your heads, O ye gates; and be ye lift up, ye everlasting doors; and the King of glory shall come in.
\vs Psa 24:8 Who \bibemph{is} this King of glory? The \textsc{Lord} strong and mighty, the \textsc{Lord} mighty in battle.
\vs Psa 24:9 Lift up your heads, O ye gates; even lift \bibemph{them} up, ye everlasting doors; and the King of glory shall come in.
\vs Psa 24:10 Who is this King of glory? The \textsc{Lord} of hosts, he \bibemph{is} the King of glory. Selah.
\vs Psa 25:1 \bibemph{A Psalm} of David. Unto thee, O \textsc{Lord}, do I lift up my soul.
\vs Psa 25:2 O my God, I trust in thee: let me not be ashamed, let not mine enemies triumph over me.
\vs Psa 25:3 Yea, let none that wait on thee be ashamed: let them be ashamed which transgress without cause.
\vs Psa 25:4 Shew me thy ways, O \textsc{Lord}; teach me thy paths.
\vs Psa 25:5 Lead me in thy truth, and teach me: for thou \bibemph{art} the God of my salvation; on thee do I wait all the day.
\vs Psa 25:6 Remember, O \textsc{Lord}, thy tender mercies and thy lovingkindnesses; for they \bibemph{have been} ever of old.
\fn{tender...: Heb. bowels.}
\vs Psa 25:7 Remember not the sins of my youth, nor my transgressions: according to thy mercy remember thou me for thy goodness' sake, O \textsc{Lord}.
\vs Psa 25:8 Good and upright \bibemph{is} the \textsc{Lord}: therefore will he teach sinners in the way.
\vs Psa 25:9 The meek will he guide in judgment: and the meek will he teach his way.
\vs Psa 25:10 All the paths of the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{are} mercy and truth unto such as keep his covenant and his testimonies.
\vs Psa 25:11 For thy name's sake, O \textsc{Lord}, pardon mine iniquity; for it \bibemph{is} great.
\vs Psa 25:12 What man \bibemph{is} he that feareth the \textsc{Lord}? him shall he teach in the way \bibemph{that} he shall choose.
\vs Psa 25:13 His soul shall dwell at ease; and his seed shall inherit the earth.
\fn{dwell...: Heb. lodge in goodness.}
\vs Psa 25:14 The secret of the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} with them that fear him; and he will shew them his covenant.
\fn{and...: or, and his covenant to make them know it.}
\vs Psa 25:15 Mine eyes \bibemph{are} ever toward the \textsc{Lord}; for he shall pluck my feet out of the net.
\fn{pluck: Heb. bring forth.}
\vs Psa 25:16 Turn thee unto me, and have mercy upon me; for I \bibemph{am} desolate and afflicted.
\vs Psa 25:17 The troubles of my heart are enlarged: \bibemph{O} bring thou me out of my distresses.
\vs Psa 25:18 Look upon mine affliction and my pain; and forgive all my sins.
\vs Psa 25:19 Consider mine enemies; for they are many; and they hate me with cruel hatred.
\fn{cruel...: Heb. hatred of violence.}
\vs Psa 25:20 O keep my soul, and deliver me: let me not be ashamed; for I put my trust in thee.
\vs Psa 25:21 Let integrity and uprightness preserve me; for I wait on thee.
\vs Psa 25:22 Redeem Israel, O God, out of all his troubles.
