\vs Psa 26:2 Examine me, O \textsc{Lord}, and prove me; try my reins and my heart.
\vs Psa 26:3 For thy lovingkindness \bibemph{is} before mine eyes: and I have walked in thy truth.
\vs Psa 26:4 I have not sat with vain persons, neither will I go in with dissemblers.
\vs Psa 26:5 I have hated the congregation of evil doers; and will not sit with the wicked.
\vs Psa 26:6 I will wash mine hands in innocency: so will I compass thine altar, O \textsc{Lord}:
\vs Psa 26:7 That I may publish with the voice of thanksgiving, and tell of all thy wondrous works.
\vs Psa 26:8 \textsc{Lord}, I have loved the habitation of thy house, and the place where thine honour dwelleth.
\fn{where...: Heb. of the tabernacle of thy honour.}
\vs Psa 26:9 Gather not my soul with sinners, nor my life with bloody men:
\fn{Gather...: or, Take not away. bloody...: Heb. men of blood.}
\vs Psa 26:10 In whose hands \bibemph{is} mischief, and their right hand is full of bribes.
\fn{full...: Heb. filled with.}
\vs Psa 26:11 But as for me, I will walk in mine integrity: redeem me, and be merciful unto me.
\vs Psa 26:12 My foot standeth in an even place: in the congregations will I bless the \textsc{Lord}.
\vs Psa 27:1 \bibemph{A Psalm} of David. The \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} my light and my salvation; whom shall I fear? the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} the strength of my life; of whom shall I be afraid?
\vs Psa 27:2 When the wicked, \bibemph{even} mine enemies and my foes, came upon me to eat up my flesh, they stumbled and fell.
\fn{came...: Heb. approached against me.}
\vs Psa 27:3 Though an host should encamp against me, my heart shall not fear: though war should rise against me, in this \bibemph{will} I \bibemph{be} confident.
\vs Psa 27:4 One \bibemph{thing} have I desired of the \textsc{Lord}, that will I seek after; that I may dwell in the house of the \textsc{Lord} all the days of my life, to behold the beauty of the \textsc{Lord}, and to enquire in his temple.
\fn{the beauty: or, the delight.}
\vs Psa 27:5 For in the time of trouble he shall hide me in his pavilion: in the secret of his tabernacle shall he hide me; he shall set me up upon a rock.
\vs Psa 27:6 And now shall mine head be lifted up above mine enemies round about me: therefore will I offer in his tabernacle sacrifices of joy; I will sing, yea, I will sing praises unto the \textsc{Lord}.
\fn{joy: Heb. shouting.}
\vs Psa 27:7 Hear, O \textsc{Lord}, \bibemph{when} I cry with my voice: have mercy also upon me, and answer me.
\vs Psa 27:8 \bibemph{When thou saidst}, Seek ye my face; my heart said unto thee, Thy face, \textsc{Lord}, will I seek.
\fn{When...: or, My heart said unto thee, Let my face seek thy face, etc.}
\vs Psa 27:9 Hide not thy face \bibemph{far} from me; put not thy servant away in anger: thou hast been my help; leave me not, neither forsake me, O God of my salvation.
\vs Psa 27:10 When my father and my mother forsake me, then the \textsc{Lord} will take me up.
\fn{take...: Heb. gather me.}
\vs Psa 27:11 Teach me thy way, O \textsc{Lord}, and lead me in a plain path, because of mine enemies.
\fn{a plain...: Heb. a way of plainness. mine...: Heb. those which observe me.}
\vs Psa 27:12 Deliver me not over unto the will of mine enemies: for false witnesses are risen up against me, and such as breathe out cruelty.
\vs Psa 27:13 \bibemph{I had fainted}, unless I had believed to see the goodness of the \textsc{Lord} in the land of the living.
\vs Psa 27:14 Wait on the \textsc{Lord}: be of good courage, and he shall strengthen thine heart: wait, I say, on the \textsc{Lord}.
\vs Psa 28:1 \bibemph{A Psalm} of David. Unto thee will I cry, O \textsc{Lord} my rock; be not silent to me: lest, \bibemph{if} thou be silent to me, I become like them that go down into the pit.
\fn{to me: Heb. from me.}
\vs Psa 28:2 Hear the voice of my supplications, when I cry unto thee, when I lift up my hands toward thy holy oracle.
\fn{thy...: or, the oracle of thy sanctuary.}
\vs Psa 28:3 Draw me not away with the wicked, and with the workers of iniquity, which speak peace to their neighbours, but mischief \bibemph{is} in their hearts.
\vs Psa 28:4 Give them according to their deeds, and according to the wickedness of their endeavours: give them after the work of their hands; render to them their desert.
\vs Psa 28:5 Because they regard not the works of the \textsc{Lord}, nor the operation of his hands, he shall destroy them, and not build them up.
\vs Psa 28:6 Blessed \bibemph{be} the \textsc{Lord}, because he hath heard the voice of my supplications.
\vs Psa 28:7 The \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} my strength and my shield; my heart trusted in him, and I am helped: therefore my heart greatly rejoiceth; and with my song will I praise him.
\vs Psa 28:8 The \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} their strength, and he \bibemph{is} the saving strength of his anointed.
\fn{their: or, his. saving...: Heb. strength of salvations.}
\vs Psa 28:9 Save thy people, and bless thine inheritance: feed them also, and lift them up for ever.
\fn{feed: or, rule.}
\vs Psa 29:1 A Psalm of David. Give unto the \textsc{Lord}, O ye mighty, give unto the \textsc{Lord} glory and strength.
\fn{ye mighty: Heb. ye sons of the mighty.}
\vs Psa 29:2 Give unto the \textsc{Lord} the glory due unto his name; worship the \textsc{Lord} in the beauty of holiness.
\fn{the glory...: Heb. the honour of his name. in...: or, in his glorious sanctuary.}
\vs Psa 29:3 The voice of the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} upon the waters: the God of glory thundereth: the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} upon many waters.
\fn{many: or, great.}
\vs Psa 29:4 The voice of the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} powerful; the voice of the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} full of majesty.
\fn{powerful: Heb. in power. full...: Heb. in majesty.}
\vs Psa 29:5 The voice of the \textsc{Lord} breaketh the cedars; yea, the \textsc{Lord} breaketh the cedars of Lebanon.
\vs Psa 29:6 He maketh them also to skip like a calf; Lebanon and Sirion like a young unicorn.
\vs Psa 29:7 The voice of the \textsc{Lord} divideth the flames of fire.
\fn{divideth: Heb. cutteth out.}
\vs Psa 29:8 The voice of the \textsc{Lord} shaketh the wilderness; the \textsc{Lord} shaketh the wilderness of Kadesh.
\vs Psa 29:9 The voice of the \textsc{Lord} maketh the hinds to calve, and discovereth the forests: and in his temple doth every one speak of \bibemph{his} glory.
\fn{to calve: or, to be in pain. doth...: or, every whit of it uttereth, etc.}
\vs Psa 29:10 The \textsc{Lord} sitteth upon the flood; yea, the \textsc{Lord} sitteth King for ever.
\vs Psa 29:11 The \textsc{Lord} will give strength unto his people; the \textsc{Lord} will bless his people with peace.
\vs Psa 30:1 A Psalm \bibemph{and} Song \bibemph{at} the dedication of the house of David. I will extol thee, O \textsc{Lord}; for thou hast lifted me up, and hast not made my foes to rejoice over me.
\vs Psa 30:2 O \textsc{Lord} my God, I cried unto thee, and thou hast healed me.
\vs Psa 30:3 O \textsc{Lord}, thou hast brought up my soul from the grave: thou hast kept me alive, that I should not go down to the pit.
\vs Psa 30:4 Sing unto the \textsc{Lord}, O ye saints of his, and give thanks at the remembrance of his holiness.
\fn{at...: or, to the memorial.}
\vs Psa 30:5 For his anger \bibemph{endureth but} a moment; in his favour \bibemph{is} life: weeping may endure for a night, but joy \bibemph{cometh} in the morning.
\fn{his anger...: Heb. there is but a moment in his anger. for a night: Heb. in the evening. joy: Heb. singing.}
\vs Psa 30:6 And in my prosperity I said, I shall never be moved.
\vs Psa 30:7 \textsc{Lord}, by thy favour thou hast made my mountain to stand strong: thou didst hide thy face, \bibemph{and} I was troubled.
\fn{made...: Heb. settled strength for my mountain.}
\vs Psa 30:8 I cried to thee, O \textsc{Lord}; and unto the \textsc{Lord} I made supplication.
\vs Psa 30:9 What profit \bibemph{is there} in my blood, when I go down to the pit? Shall the dust praise thee? shall it declare thy truth?
\vs Psa 30:10 Hear, O \textsc{Lord}, and have mercy upon me: \textsc{Lord}, be thou my helper.
\vs Psa 30:11 Thou hast turned for me my mourning into dancing: thou hast put off my sackcloth, and girded me with gladness;
\vs Psa 30:12 To the end that \bibemph{my} glory may sing praise to thee, and not be silent. O \textsc{Lord} my God, I will give thanks unto thee for ever.
\fn{my glory: that is, my tongue, or, my soul.}
\vs Psa 31:1 To the chief Musician, A Psalm of David. In thee, O \textsc{Lord}, do I put my trust; let me never be ashamed: deliver me in thy righteousness.
\vs Psa 31:2 Bow down thine ear to me; deliver me speedily: be thou my strong rock, for an house of defence to save me.
\fn{my...: Heb. to me for rock of strength.}
\vs Psa 31:3 For thou \bibemph{art} my rock and my fortress; therefore for thy name's sake lead me, and guide me.
\vs Psa 31:4 Pull me out of the net that they have laid privily for me: for thou \bibemph{art} my strength.
\vs Psa 31:5 Into thine hand I commit my spirit: thou hast redeemed me, O \textsc{Lord} God of truth.
\vs Psa 31:6 I have hated them that regard lying vanities: but I trust in the \textsc{Lord}.
\vs Psa 31:7 I will be glad and rejoice in thy mercy: for thou hast considered my trouble; thou hast known my soul in adversities;
\vs Psa 31:8 And hast not shut me up into the hand of the enemy: thou hast set my feet in a large room.
\vs Psa 31:9 Have mercy upon me, O \textsc{Lord}, for I am in trouble: mine eye is consumed with grief, \bibemph{yea}, my soul and my belly.
\vs Psa 31:10 For my life is spent with grief, and my years with sighing: my strength faileth because of mine iniquity, and my bones are consumed.
\vs Psa 31:11 I was a reproach among all mine enemies, but especially among my neighbours, and a fear to mine acquaintance: they that did see me without fled from me.
\vs Psa 31:12 I am forgotten as a dead man out of mind: I am like a broken vessel.
\fn{a broken...: Heb. a vessel that perisheth.}
\vs Psa 31:13 For I have heard the slander of many: fear \bibemph{was} on every side: while they took counsel together against me, they devised to take away my life.
\vs Psa 31:14 But I trusted in thee, O \textsc{Lord}: I said, Thou \bibemph{art} my God.
\vs Psa 31:15 My times \bibemph{are} in thy hand: deliver me from the hand of mine enemies, and from them that persecute me.
\vs Psa 31:16 Make thy face to shine upon thy servant: save me for thy mercies' sake.
\vs Psa 31:17 Let me not be ashamed, O \textsc{Lord}; for I have called upon thee: let the wicked be ashamed, \bibemph{and} let them be silent in the grave.
\fn{silent...: or, cut off for.}
\vs Psa 31:18 Let the lying lips be put to silence; which speak grievous things proudly and contemptuously against the righteous.
\fn{grievous...: Heb. a hard thing.}
\vs Psa 31:19 \bibemph{Oh} how great \bibemph{is} thy goodness, which thou hast laid up for them that fear thee; \bibemph{which} thou hast wrought for them that trust in thee before the sons of men!
\vs Psa 31:20 Thou shalt hide them in the secret of thy presence from the pride of man: thou shalt keep them secretly in a pavilion from the strife of tongues.
\vs Psa 31:21 Blessed \bibemph{be} the \textsc{Lord}: for he hath shewed me his marvellous kindness in a strong city.
\fn{strong: or, fenced.}
\vs Psa 31:22 For I said in my haste, I am cut off from before thine eyes: nevertheless thou heardest the voice of my supplications when I cried unto thee.
\vs Psa 31:23 O love the \textsc{Lord}, all ye his saints: \bibemph{for} the \textsc{Lord} preserveth the faithful, and plentifully rewardeth the proud doer.
\vs Psa 31:24 Be of good courage, and he shall strengthen your heart, all ye that hope in the \textsc{Lord}.
\vs Psa 32:1 \bibemph{A Psalm} of David, Maschil. Blessed \bibemph{is he whose} transgression \bibemph{is} forgiven, \bibemph{whose} sin \bibemph{is} covered.
\fn{A Psalm...: or, A Psalm of David giving instruction.}
\vs Psa 32:2 Blessed \bibemph{is} the man unto whom the \textsc{Lord} imputeth not iniquity, and in whose spirit \bibemph{there is} no guile.
\vs Psa 32:3 When I kept silence, my bones waxed old through my roaring all the day long.
\vs Psa 32:4 For day and night thy hand was heavy upon me: my moisture is turned into the drought of summer. Selah.
\vs Psa 32:5 I acknowledged my sin unto thee, and mine iniquity have I not hid. I said, I will confess my transgressions unto the \textsc{Lord}; and thou forgavest the iniquity of my sin. Selah.
\vs Psa 32:6 For this shall every one that is godly pray unto thee in a time when thou mayest be found: surely in the floods of great waters they shall not come nigh unto him.
\fn{when...: Heb. of finding.}
\vs Psa 32:7 Thou \bibemph{art} my hiding place; thou shalt preserve me from trouble; thou shalt compass me about with songs of deliverance. Selah.
\vs Psa 32:8 I will instruct thee and teach thee in the way which thou shalt go: I will guide thee with mine eye.
\fn{guide...: Heb. counsel thee, mine eye shall be upon thee.}
\vs Psa 32:9 Be ye not as the horse, \bibemph{or} as the mule, \bibemph{which} have no understanding: whose mouth must be held in with bit and bridle, lest they come near unto thee.
\vs Psa 32:10 Many sorrows \bibemph{shall be} to the wicked: but he that trusteth in the \textsc{Lord}, mercy shall compass him about.
\vs Psa 32:11 Be glad in the \textsc{Lord}, and rejoice, ye righteous: and shout for joy, all \bibemph{ye that are} upright in heart.
\vs Psa 33:1 Rejoice in the \textsc{Lord}, O ye righteous: \bibemph{for} praise is comely for the upright.
\vs Psa 33:2 Praise the \textsc{Lord} with harp: sing unto him with the psaltery \bibemph{and} an instrument of ten strings.
\vs Psa 33:3 Sing unto him a new song; play skilfully with a loud noise.
\vs Psa 33:4 For the word of the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} right; and all his works \bibemph{are done} in truth.
\vs Psa 33:5 He loveth righteousness and judgment: the earth is full of the goodness of the \textsc{Lord}.
\fn{goodness: or, mercy.}
\vs Psa 33:6 By the word of the \textsc{Lord} were the heavens made; and all the host of them by the breath of his mouth.
\vs Psa 33:7 He gathereth the waters of the sea together as an heap: he layeth up the depth in storehouses.
\vs Psa 33:8 Let all the earth fear the \textsc{Lord}: let all the inhabitants of the world stand in awe of him.
\vs Psa 33:9 For he spake, and it was \bibemph{done}; he commanded, and it stood fast.
\vs Psa 33:10 The \textsc{Lord} bringeth the counsel of the heathen to nought: he maketh the devices of the people of none effect.
\fn{bringeth: Heb. maketh frustrate.}
\vs Psa 33:11 The counsel of the \textsc{Lord} standeth for ever, the thoughts of his heart to all generations.
\fn{to all...: Heb. to generation and generation.}
\vs Psa 33:12 Blessed \bibemph{is} the nation whose God \bibemph{is} the \textsc{Lord}; \bibemph{and} the people \bibemph{whom} he hath chosen for his own inheritance.
\vs Psa 33:13 The \textsc{Lord} looketh from heaven; he beholdeth all the sons of men.
\vs Psa 33:14 From the place of his habitation he looketh upon all the inhabitants of the earth.
\vs Psa 33:15 He fashioneth their hearts alike; he considereth all their works.
\vs Psa 33:16 There is no king saved by the multitude of an host: a mighty man is not delivered by much strength.
\vs Psa 33:17 An horse \bibemph{is} a vain thing for safety: neither shall he deliver \bibemph{any} by his great strength.
\vs Psa 33:18 Behold, the eye of the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} upon them that fear him, upon them that hope in his mercy;
\vs Psa 33:19 To deliver their soul from death, and to keep them alive in famine.
\vs Psa 33:20 Our soul waiteth for the \textsc{Lord}: he \bibemph{is} our help and our shield.
\vs Psa 33:21 For our heart shall rejoice in him, because we have trusted in his holy name.
\vs Psa 33:22 Let thy mercy, O \textsc{Lord}, be upon us, according as we hope in thee.
\vs Psa 34:1 \bibemph{A Psalm} of David, when he changed his behaviour before Abimelech; who drove him away, and he departed. I will bless the \textsc{Lord} at all times: his praise \bibemph{shall} continually \bibemph{be} in my mouth.
\fn{Abimelech: or, Achish.}
\vs Psa 34:2 My soul shall make her boast in the \textsc{Lord}: the humble shall hear \bibemph{thereof}, and be glad.
\vs Psa 34:3 O magnify the \textsc{Lord} with me, and let us exalt his name together.
\vs Psa 34:4 I sought the \textsc{Lord}, and he heard me, and delivered me from all my fears.
\vs Psa 34:5 They looked unto him, and were lightened: and their faces were not ashamed.
\fn{were lightened: or, they flowed unto him.}
\vs Psa 34:6 This poor man cried, and the \textsc{Lord} heard \bibemph{him}, and saved him out of all his troubles.
\vs Psa 34:7 The angel of the \textsc{Lord} encampeth round about them that fear him, and delivereth them.
\vs Psa 34:8 O taste and see that the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} good: blessed \bibemph{is} the man \bibemph{that} trusteth in him.
\vs Psa 34:9 O fear the \textsc{Lord}, ye his saints: for \bibemph{there is} no want to them that fear him.
\vs Psa 34:10 The young lions do lack, and suffer hunger: but they that seek the \textsc{Lord} shall not want any good \bibemph{thing}.
\vs Psa 34:11 Come, ye children, hearken unto me: I will teach you the fear of the \textsc{Lord}.
\vs Psa 34:12 What man \bibemph{is he that} desireth life, \bibemph{and} loveth \bibemph{many} days, that he may see good?
\vs Psa 34:13 Keep thy tongue from evil, and thy lips from speaking guile.
\vs Psa 34:14 Depart from evil, and do good; seek peace, and pursue it.
\vs Psa 34:15 The eyes of the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{are} upon the righteous, and his ears \bibemph{are open} unto their cry.
\vs Psa 34:16 The face of the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} against them that do evil, to cut off the remembrance of them from the earth.
\vs Psa 34:17 \bibemph{The righteous} cry, and the \textsc{Lord} heareth, and delivereth them out of all their troubles.
\vs Psa 34:18 The \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} nigh unto them that are of a broken heart; and saveth such as be of a contrite spirit.
\fn{unto...: Heb. to the broken of heart. of a contrite...: Heb. contrite of spirit.}
\vs Psa 34:19 Many \bibemph{are} the afflictions of the righteous: but the \textsc{Lord} delivereth him out of them all.
\vs Psa 34:20 He keepeth all his bones: not one of them is broken.
\vs Psa 34:21 Evil shall slay the wicked: and they that hate the righteous shall be desolate.
\fn{desolate: or, guilty.}
\vs Psa 34:22 The \textsc{Lord} redeemeth the soul of his servants: and none of them that trust in him shall be desolate.
\fn{desolate: or, guilty.}
\vs Psa 35:1 \bibemph{A Psalm} of David. Plead \bibemph{my cause}, O \textsc{Lord}, with them that strive with me: fight against them that fight against me.
\vs Psa 35:2 Take hold of shield and buckler, and stand up for mine help.
\vs Psa 35:3 Draw out also the spear, and stop \bibemph{the way} against them that persecute me: say unto my soul, I \bibemph{am} thy salvation.
\vs Psa 35:4 Let them be confounded and put to shame that seek after my soul: let them be turned back and brought to confusion that devise my hurt.
\vs Psa 35:5 Let them be as chaff before the wind: and let the angel of the \textsc{Lord} chase \bibemph{them}.
\vs Psa 35:6 Let their way be dark and slippery: and let the angel of the \textsc{Lord} persecute them.
\fn{dark...: Heb. darkness and slipperiness.}
\vs Psa 35:7 For without cause have they hid for me their net \bibemph{in} a pit, \bibemph{which} without cause they have digged for my soul.
\vs Psa 35:8 Let destruction come upon him at unawares; and let his net that he hath hid catch himself: into that very destruction let him fall.
\fn{at...: Heb. which he knoweth not of.}
\vs Psa 35:9 And my soul shall be joyful in the \textsc{Lord}: it shall rejoice in his salvation.
\vs Psa 35:10 All my bones shall say, \textsc{Lord}, who \bibemph{is} like unto thee, which deliverest the poor from him that is too strong for him, yea, the poor and the needy from him that spoileth him?
\vs Psa 35:11 False witnesses did rise up; they laid to my charge \bibemph{things} that I knew not.
\fn{False...: Heb. Witnesses of wrong. they...: Heb. they asked me.}
\vs Psa 35:12 They rewarded me evil for good \bibemph{to} the spoiling of my soul.
\fn{spoiling: Heb. depriving.}
\vs Psa 35:13 But as for me, when they were sick, my clothing \bibemph{was} sackcloth: I humbled my soul with fasting; and my prayer returned into mine own bosom.
\fn{humbled: or, afflicted.}
\vs Psa 35:14 I behaved myself as though \bibemph{he had been} my friend \bibemph{or} brother: I bowed down heavily, as one that mourneth \bibemph{for his} mother.
\fn{behaved myself: Heb. walked. as though...: Heb. as a friend, as a brother to me.}
\vs Psa 35:15 But in mine adversity they rejoiced, and gathered themselves together: \bibemph{yea}, the abjects gathered themselves together against me, and I knew \bibemph{it} not; they did tear \bibemph{me}, and ceased not:
\fn{adversity: Heb. halting.}
\vs Psa 35:16 With hypocritical mockers in feasts, they gnashed upon me with their teeth.
\vs Psa 35:17 Lord, how long wilt thou look on? rescue my soul from their destructions, my darling from the lions.
\fn{darling: Heb. only one.}
\vs Psa 35:18 I will give thee thanks in the great congregation: I will praise thee among much people.
\fn{much: Heb. strong.}
\vs Psa 35:19 Let not them that are mine enemies wrongfully rejoice over me: \bibemph{neither} let them wink with the eye that hate me without a cause.
\fn{wrongfully: Heb. falsely.}
\vs Psa 35:20 For they speak not peace: but they devise deceitful matters against \bibemph{them that are} quiet in the land.
\vs Psa 35:21 Yea, they opened their mouth wide against me, \bibemph{and} said, Aha, aha, our eye hath seen \bibemph{it}.
\vs Psa 35:22 \bibemph{This} thou hast seen, O \textsc{Lord}: keep not silence: O Lord, be not far from me.
\vs Psa 35:23 Stir up thyself, and awake to my judgment, \bibemph{even} unto my cause, my God and my Lord.
\vs Psa 35:24 Judge me, O \textsc{Lord} my God, according to thy righteousness; and let them not rejoice over me.
\vs Psa 35:25 Let them not say in their hearts, Ah, so would we have it: let them not say, We have swallowed him up.
\fn{Ah...: Heb. Ah, ah, our soul.}
\vs Psa 35:26 Let them be ashamed and brought to confusion together that rejoice at mine hurt: let them be clothed with shame and dishonour that magnify \bibemph{themselves} against me.
\vs Psa 35:27 Let them shout for joy, and be glad, that favour my righteous cause: yea, let them say continually, Let the \textsc{Lord} be magnified, which hath pleasure in the prosperity of his servant.
\fn{righteous...: Heb. righteousness.}
\vs Psa 35:28 And my tongue shall speak of thy righteousness \bibemph{and} of thy praise all the day long.
\vs Psa 36:1 To the chief Musician, \bibemph{A Psalm} of David the servant of the \textsc{Lord}. The transgression of the wicked saith within my heart, \bibemph{that there is} no fear of God before his eyes.
\vs Psa 36:2 For he flattereth himself in his own eyes, until his iniquity be found to be hateful.
\fn{until...: Heb. to find his iniquity to hate.}
\vs Psa 36:3 The words of his mouth \bibemph{are} iniquity and deceit: he hath left off to be wise, \bibemph{and} to do good.
\vs Psa 36:4 He deviseth mischief upon his bed; he setteth himself in a way \bibemph{that is} not good; he abhorreth not evil.
\fn{mischief: or, vanity.}
\vs Psa 36:5 Thy mercy, O \textsc{Lord}, \bibemph{is} in the heavens; \bibemph{and} thy faithfulness \bibemph{reacheth} unto the clouds.
\vs Psa 36:6 Thy righteousness \bibemph{is} like the great mountains; thy judgments \bibemph{are} a great deep: O \textsc{Lord}, thou preservest man and beast.
\fn{the...: Heb. the mountains of God.}
\vs Psa 36:7 How excellent \bibemph{is} thy lovingkindness, O God! therefore the children of men put their trust under the shadow of thy wings.
\fn{excellent: Heb. precious.}
\vs Psa 36:8 They shall be abundantly satisfied with the fatness of thy house; and thou shalt make them drink of the river of thy pleasures.
\fn{abundantly...: Heb. watered.}
\vs Psa 36:9 For with thee \bibemph{is} the fountain of life: in thy light shall we see light.
\vs Psa 36:10 O continue thy lovingkindness unto them that know thee; and thy righteousness to the upright in heart.
\fn{continue: Heb. draw out at length.}
\vs Psa 36:11 Let not the foot of pride come against me, and let not the hand of the wicked remove me.
\vs Psa 36:12 There are the workers of iniquity fallen: they are cast down, and shall not be able to rise.
\vs Psa 37:1 \bibemph{A Psalm} of David. Fret not thyself because of evildoers, neither be thou envious against the workers of iniquity.
\vs Psa 37:2 For they shall soon be cut down like the grass, and wither as the green herb.
\vs Psa 37:3 Trust in the \textsc{Lord}, and do good; \bibemph{so} shalt thou dwell in the land, and verily thou shalt be fed.
\fn{verily: Heb. in truth, or, stableness.}
\vs Psa 37:4 Delight thyself also in the \textsc{Lord}; and he shall give thee the desires of thine heart.
\vs Psa 37:5 Commit thy way unto the \textsc{Lord}; trust also in him; and he shall bring \bibemph{it} to pass.
\fn{Commit...: Heb. Roll thy way upon.}
\vs Psa 37:6 And he shall bring forth thy righteousness as the light, and thy judgment as the noonday.
\vs Psa 37:7 Rest in the \textsc{Lord}, and wait patiently for him: fret not thyself because of him who prospereth in his way, because of the man who bringeth wicked devices to pass.
\fn{Rest in: Heb. Be silent to.}
\vs Psa 37:8 Cease from anger, and forsake wrath: fret not thyself in any wise to do evil.
\vs Psa 37:9 For evildoers shall be cut off: but those that wait upon the \textsc{Lord}, they shall inherit the earth.
\vs Psa 37:10 For yet a little while, and the wicked \bibemph{shall} not \bibemph{be}: yea, thou shalt diligently consider his place, and it \bibemph{shall} not \bibemph{be}.
\vs Psa 37:11 But the meek shall inherit the earth; and shall delight themselves in the abundance of peace.
\vs Psa 37:12 The wicked plotteth against the just, and gnasheth upon him with his teeth.
\fn{plotteth: or, practiseth.}
\vs Psa 37:13 The Lord shall laugh at him: for he seeth that his day is coming.
\vs Psa 37:14 The wicked have drawn out the sword, and have bent their bow, to cast down the poor and needy, \bibemph{and} to slay such as be of upright conversation.
\fn{such...: Heb. the upright of way.}
\vs Psa 37:15 Their sword shall enter into their own heart, and their bows shall be broken.
\vs Psa 37:16 A little that a righteous man hath \bibemph{is} better than the riches of many wicked.
\vs Psa 37:17 For the arms of the wicked shall be broken: but the \textsc{Lord} upholdeth the righteous.
\vs Psa 37:18 The \textsc{Lord} knoweth the days of the upright: and their inheritance shall be for ever.
\vs Psa 37:19 They shall not be ashamed in the evil time: and in the days of famine they shall be satisfied.
\vs Psa 37:20 But the wicked shall perish, and the enemies of the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{shall be} as the fat of lambs: they shall consume; into smoke shall they consume away.
\fn{the fat: Heb. the preciousness.}
\vs Psa 37:21 The wicked borroweth, and payeth not again: but the righteous sheweth mercy, and giveth.
\vs Psa 37:22 For \bibemph{such as be} blessed of him shall inherit the earth; and \bibemph{they that be} cursed of him shall be cut off.
\vs Psa 37:23 The steps of a \bibemph{good} man are ordered by the \textsc{Lord}: and he delighteth in his way.
\fn{ordered: or, established.}
\vs Psa 37:24 Though he fall, he shall not be utterly cast down: for the \textsc{Lord} upholdeth \bibemph{him with} his hand.
\vs Psa 37:25 I have been young, and \bibemph{now} am old; yet have I not seen the righteous forsaken, nor his seed begging bread.
\vs Psa 37:26 \bibemph{He is} ever merciful, and lendeth; and his seed \bibemph{is} blessed.
\fn{ever: Heb. all the day.}
\vs Psa 37:27 Depart from evil, and do good; and dwell for evermore.
\vs Psa 37:28 For the \textsc{Lord} loveth judgment, and forsaketh not his saints; they are preserved for ever: but the seed of the wicked shall be cut off.
\vs Psa 37:29 The righteous shall inherit the land, and dwell therein for ever.
\vs Psa 37:30 The mouth of the righteous speaketh wisdom, and his tongue talketh of judgment.
\vs Psa 37:31 The law of his God \bibemph{is} in his heart; none of his steps shall slide.
\fn{steps: or, goings.}
\vs Psa 37:32 The wicked watcheth the righteous, and seeketh to slay him.
\vs Psa 37:33 The \textsc{Lord} will not leave him in his hand, nor condemn him when he is judged.
\vs Psa 37:34 Wait on the \textsc{Lord}, and keep his way, and he shall exalt thee to inherit the land: when the wicked are cut off, thou shalt see \bibemph{it}.
\vs Psa 37:35 I have seen the wicked in great power, and spreading himself like a green bay tree.
\fn{a green...: or, a green tree that groweth in his own soil.}
\vs Psa 37:36 Yet he passed away, and, lo, he \bibemph{was} not: yea, I sought him, but he could not be found.
\vs Psa 37:37 Mark the perfect \bibemph{man}, and behold the upright: for the end of \bibemph{that} man \bibemph{is} peace.
\vs Psa 37:38 But the transgressors shall be destroyed together: the end of the wicked shall be cut off.
\vs Psa 37:39 But the salvation of the righteous \bibemph{is} of the \textsc{Lord}: \bibemph{he is} their strength in the time of trouble.
\vs Psa 37:40 And the \textsc{Lord} shall help them, and deliver them: he shall deliver them from the wicked, and save them, because they trust in him.
\vs Psa 38:1 A Psalm of David, to bring to remembrance. O \textsc{Lord}, rebuke me not in thy wrath: neither chasten me in thy hot displeasure.
\vs Psa 38:2 For thine arrows stick fast in me, and thy hand presseth me sore.
\vs Psa 38:3 \bibemph{There is} no soundness in my flesh because of thine anger; neither \bibemph{is there any} rest in my bones because of my sin.
\fn{rest: Heb. peace, or, health.}
\vs Psa 38:4 For mine iniquities are gone over mine head: as an heavy burden they are too heavy for me.
\vs Psa 38:5 My wounds stink \bibemph{and} are corrupt because of my foolishness.
\vs Psa 38:6 I am troubled; I am bowed down greatly; I go mourning all the day long.
\fn{troubled: Heb. wried.}
\vs Psa 38:7 For my loins are filled with a loathsome \bibemph{disease}: and \bibemph{there is} no soundness in my flesh.
\vs Psa 38:8 I am feeble and sore broken: I have roared by reason of the disquietness of my heart.
\vs Psa 38:9 Lord, all my desire \bibemph{is} before thee; and my groaning is not hid from thee.
\vs Psa 38:10 My heart panteth, my strength faileth me: as for the light of mine eyes, it also is gone from me.
\fn{is gone...: Heb. is not with me.}
\vs Psa 38:11 My lovers and my friends stand aloof from my sore; and my kinsmen stand afar off.
\fn{sore: Heb. stroke. my kinsmen: or, my neighbours.}
\vs Psa 38:12 They also that seek after my life lay snares \bibemph{for me}: and they that seek my hurt speak mischievous things, and imagine deceits all the day long.
\vs Psa 38:13 But I, as a deaf \bibemph{man}, heard not; and \bibemph{I was} as a dumb man \bibemph{that} openeth not his mouth.
\vs Psa 38:14 Thus I was as a man that heareth not, and in whose mouth \bibemph{are} no reproofs.
\vs Psa 38:15 For in thee, O \textsc{Lord}, do I hope: thou wilt hear, O Lord my God.
\fn{in...: or, thee do I wait for. hear: or, answer.}
\vs Psa 38:16 For I said, \bibemph{Hear me}, lest \bibemph{otherwise} they should rejoice over me: when my foot slippeth, they magnify \bibemph{themselves} against me.
\vs Psa 38:17 For I \bibemph{am} ready to halt, and my sorrow \bibemph{is} continually before me.
\fn{to halt: Heb. for halting.}
\vs Psa 38:18 For I will declare mine iniquity; I will be sorry for my sin.
\vs Psa 38:19 But mine enemies \bibemph{are} lively, \bibemph{and} they are strong: and they that hate me wrongfully are multiplied.
\fn{are lively...: Heb. being living, are strong.}
\vs Psa 38:20 They also that render evil for good are mine adversaries; because I follow \bibemph{the thing that} good \bibemph{is}.
\vs Psa 38:21 Forsake me not, O \textsc{Lord}: O my God, be not far from me.
\vs Psa 38:22 Make haste to help me, O Lord my salvation.
\fn{to...: Heb. for my help.}
\vs Psa 39:1 To the chief Musician, \bibemph{even} to Jeduthun, A Psalm of David. I said, I will take heed to my ways, that I sin not with my tongue: I will keep my mouth with a bridle, while the wicked is before me.
\fn{my mouth...: Heb. a bridle, or, muzzle for my mouth.}
\vs Psa 39:2 I was dumb with silence, I held my peace, \bibemph{even} from good; and my sorrow was stirred.
\fn{stirred: Heb. troubled.}
\vs Psa 39:3 My heart was hot within me, while I was musing the fire burned: \bibemph{then} spake I with my tongue,
\vs Psa 39:4 \textsc{Lord}, make me to know mine end, and the measure of my days, what it \bibemph{is; that} I may know how frail I \bibemph{am}.
\fn{how...: or, what time I have here.}
\vs Psa 39:5 Behold, thou hast made my days \bibemph{as} an handbreadth; and mine age \bibemph{is} as nothing before thee: verily every man at his best state \bibemph{is} altogether vanity. Selah.
\fn{at...: Heb. settled.}
\vs Psa 39:6 Surely every man walketh in a vain shew: surely they are disquieted in vain: he heapeth up \bibemph{riches}, and knoweth not who shall gather them.
\fn{a vain...: Heb. an image.}
\vs Psa 39:7 And now, Lord, what wait I for? my hope \bibemph{is} in thee.
\vs Psa 39:8 Deliver me from all my transgressions: make me not the reproach of the foolish.
\vs Psa 39:9 I was dumb, I opened not my mouth; because thou didst \bibemph{it}.
\vs Psa 39:10 Remove thy stroke away from me: I am consumed by the blow of thine hand.
\fn{blow: Heb. conflict.}
\vs Psa 39:11 When thou with rebukes dost correct man for iniquity, thou makest his beauty to consume away like a moth: surely every man \bibemph{is} vanity. Selah.
\fn{his...: Heb. that which is to be desired in him to melt away.}
\vs Psa 39:12 Hear my prayer, O \textsc{Lord}, and give ear unto my cry; hold not thy peace at my tears: for I \bibemph{am} a stranger with thee, \bibemph{and} a sojourner, as all my fathers \bibemph{were}.
\vs Psa 39:13 O spare me, that I may recover strength, before I go hence, and be no more.
\vs Psa 40:1 To the chief Musician, A Psalm of David. I waited patiently for the \textsc{Lord}; and he inclined unto me, and heard my cry.
\fn{I waited...: Heb. In waiting I waited.}
\vs Psa 40:2 He brought me up also out of an horrible pit, out of the miry clay, and set my feet upon a rock, \bibemph{and} established my goings.
\fn{an...: Heb. a pit of noise.}
\vs Psa 40:3 And he hath put a new song in my mouth, \bibemph{even} praise unto our God: many shall see \bibemph{it}, and fear, and shall trust in the \textsc{Lord}.
\vs Psa 40:4 Blessed \bibemph{is} that man that maketh the \textsc{Lord} his trust, and respecteth not the proud, nor such as turn aside to lies.
\vs Psa 40:5 Many, O \textsc{Lord} my God, \bibemph{are} thy wonderful works \bibemph{which} thou hast done, and thy thoughts \bibemph{which are} to us-ward: they cannot be reckoned up in order unto thee: \bibemph{if} I would declare and speak \bibemph{of them}, they are more than can be numbered.
\fn{they can not...: or, none can order them unto thee.}
\vs Psa 40:6 Sacrifice and offering thou didst not desire; mine ears hast thou opened: burnt offering and sin offering hast thou not required.
\fn{opened: Heb. digged.}
\vs Psa 40:7 Then said I, Lo, I come: in the volume of the book \bibemph{it is} written of me,
\vs Psa 40:8 I delight to do thy will, O my God: yea, thy law \bibemph{is} within my heart.
\fn{within...: Heb. in the midst of my bowels.}
\vs Psa 40:9 I have preached righteousness in the great congregation: lo, I have not refrained my lips, O \textsc{Lord}, thou knowest.
\vs Psa 40:10 I have not hid thy righteousness within my heart; I have declared thy faithfulness and thy salvation: I have not concealed thy lovingkindness and thy truth from the great congregation.
\vs Psa 40:11 Withhold not thou thy tender mercies from me, O \textsc{Lord}: let thy lovingkindness and thy truth continually preserve me.
\vs Psa 40:12 For innumerable evils have compassed me about: mine iniquities have taken hold upon me, so that I am not able to look up; they are more than the hairs of mine head: therefore my heart faileth me.
\fn{falleth: Heb. forsaketh.}
\vs Psa 40:13 Be pleased, O \textsc{Lord}, to deliver me: O \textsc{Lord}, make haste to help me.
\vs Psa 40:14 Let them be ashamed and confounded together that seek after my soul to destroy it; let them be driven backward and put to shame that wish me evil.
\vs Psa 40:15 Let them be desolate for a reward of their shame that say unto me, Aha, aha.
\vs Psa 40:16 Let all those that seek thee rejoice and be glad in thee: let such as love thy salvation say continually, The \textsc{Lord} be magnified.
\vs Psa 40:17 But I \bibemph{am} poor and needy; \bibemph{yet} the Lord thinketh upon me: thou \bibemph{art} my help and my deliverer; make no tarrying, O my God.
\vs Psa 41:1 To the chief Musician, A Psalm of David. Blessed \bibemph{is} he that considereth the poor: the \textsc{Lord} will deliver him in time of trouble.
\fn{the poor: or, the weak, or, sick. in time...: Heb. in the day of evil.}
\vs Psa 41:2 The \textsc{Lord} will preserve him, and keep him alive; \bibemph{and} he shall be blessed upon the earth: and thou wilt not deliver him unto the will of his enemies.
\fn{thou...: or, do not thou deliver.}
\vs Psa 41:3 The \textsc{Lord} will strengthen him upon the bed of languishing: thou wilt make all his bed in his sickness.
\fn{make: Heb. turn.}
\vs Psa 41:4 I said, \textsc{Lord}, be merciful unto me: heal my soul; for I have sinned against thee.
\vs Psa 41:5 Mine enemies speak evil of me, When shall he die, and his name perish?
\vs Psa 41:6 And if he come to see \bibemph{me}, he speaketh vanity: his heart gathereth iniquity to itself; \bibemph{when} he goeth abroad, he telleth \bibemph{it}.
\vs Psa 41:7 All that hate me whisper together against me: against me do they devise my hurt.
\fn{my...: Heb. evil to me.}
\vs Psa 41:8 An evil disease, \bibemph{say they}, cleaveth fast unto him: and \bibemph{now} that he lieth he shall rise up no more.
\fn{An...: Heb. A thing of Belial.}
\vs Psa 41:9 Yea, mine own familiar friend, in whom I trusted, which did eat of my bread, hath lifted up \bibemph{his} heel against me.
\fn{mine...: Heb. the man of my peace. lifted...: Heb. magnified.}
\vs Psa 41:10 But thou, O \textsc{Lord}, be merciful unto me, and raise me up, that I may requite them.
\vs Psa 41:11 By this I know that thou favourest me, because mine enemy doth not triumph over me.
\vs Psa 41:12 And as for me, thou upholdest me in mine integrity, and settest me before thy face for ever.
\vs Psa 41:13 Blessed \bibemph{be} the \textsc{Lord} God of Israel from everlasting, and to everlasting. Amen, and Amen.
\vs Psa 42:1 To the chief Musician, Maschil, for the sons of Korah. As the hart panteth after the water brooks, so panteth my soul after thee, O God.
\fn{Maschil...: or, A Psalm giving instruction of the sons, etc. panteth: Heb. brayeth.}
\vs Psa 42:2 My soul thirsteth for God, for the living God: when shall I come and appear before God?
\vs Psa 42:3 My tears have been my meat day and night, while they continually say unto me, Where \bibemph{is} thy God?
\vs Psa 42:4 When I remember these \bibemph{things}, I pour out my soul in me: for I had gone with the multitude, I went with them to the house of God, with the voice of joy and praise, with a multitude that kept holyday.
\vs Psa 42:5 Why art thou cast down, O my soul? and \bibemph{why} art thou disquieted in me? hope thou in God: for I shall yet praise him \bibemph{for} the help of his countenance.
\fn{cast: Heb. bowed. praise: or, give thanks. for the...: or, his presence is salvation.}
\vs Psa 42:6 O my God, my soul is cast down within me: therefore will I remember thee from the land of Jordan, and of the Hermonites, from the hill Mizar.
\fn{the hill...: or, the little hill.}
\vs Psa 42:7 Deep calleth unto deep at the noise of thy waterspouts: all thy waves and thy billows are gone over me.
\vs Psa 42:8 \bibemph{Yet} the \textsc{Lord} will command his lovingkindness in the daytime, and in the night his song \bibemph{shall be} with me, \bibemph{and} my prayer unto the God of my life.
\vs Psa 42:9 I will say unto God my rock, Why hast thou forgotten me? why go I mourning because of the oppression of the enemy?
\vs Psa 42:10 \bibemph{As} with a sword in my bones, mine enemies reproach me; while they say daily unto me, Where \bibemph{is} thy God?
\fn{sword: or, killing.}
\vs Psa 42:11 Why art thou cast down, O my soul? and why art thou disquieted within me? hope thou in God: for I shall yet praise him, \bibemph{who is} the health of my countenance, and my God.

\fn{ungodly: or, unmerciful. the deceitful...: Heb. a man of deceit and iniquity.}
\vs Psa 43:2 For thou \bibemph{art} the God of my strength: why dost thou cast me off? why go I mourning because of the oppression of the enemy?
\vs Psa 43:3 O send out thy light and thy truth: let them lead me; let them bring me unto thy holy hill, and to thy tabernacles.
\vs Psa 43:4 Then will I go unto the altar of God, unto God my exceeding joy: yea, upon the harp will I praise thee, O God my God.
\fn{my exceeding...: Heb. the gladness of my joy.}
\vs Psa 43:5 Why art thou cast down, O my soul? and why art thou disquieted within me? hope in God: for I shall yet praise him, \bibemph{who is} the health of my countenance, and my God.
\vs Psa 44:1 To the chief Musician for the sons of Korah, Maschil. We have heard with our ears, O God, our fathers have told us, \bibemph{what} work thou didst in their days, in the times of old.
\vs Psa 44:2 \bibemph{How} thou didst drive out the heathen with thy hand, and plantedst them; \bibemph{how} thou didst afflict the people, and cast them out.
\vs Psa 44:3 For they got not the land in possession by their own sword, neither did their own arm save them: but thy right hand, and thine arm, and the light of thy countenance, because thou hadst a favour unto them.
\vs Psa 44:4 Thou art my King, O God: command deliverances for Jacob.
\vs Psa 44:5 Through thee will we push down our enemies: through thy name will we tread them under that rise up against us.
\vs Psa 44:6 For I will not trust in my bow, neither shall my sword save me.
\vs Psa 44:7 But thou hast saved us from our enemies, and hast put them to shame that hated us.
\vs Psa 44:8 In God we boast all the day long, and praise thy name for ever. Selah.
\vs Psa 44:9 But thou hast cast off, and put us to shame; and goest not forth with our armies.
\vs Psa 44:10 Thou makest us to turn back from the enemy: and they which hate us spoil for themselves.
\vs Psa 44:11 Thou hast given us like sheep \bibemph{appointed} for meat; and hast scattered us among the heathen.
\fn{like...: Heb. as sheep of meat.}
\vs Psa 44:12 Thou sellest thy people for nought, and dost not increase \bibemph{thy wealth} by their price.
\fn{for...: Heb. without riches.}
\vs Psa 44:13 Thou makest us a reproach to our neighbours, a scorn and a derision to them that are round about us.
\vs Psa 44:14 Thou makest us a byword among the heathen, a shaking of the head among the people.
\vs Psa 44:15 My confusion \bibemph{is} continually before me, and the shame of my face hath covered me,
\vs Psa 44:16 For the voice of him that reproacheth and blasphemeth; by reason of the enemy and avenger.
\vs Psa 44:17 All this is come upon us; yet have we not forgotten thee, neither have we dealt falsely in thy covenant.
\vs Psa 44:18 Our heart is not turned back, neither have our steps declined from thy way;
\fn{steps: or, goings.}
\vs Psa 44:19 Though thou hast sore broken us in the place of dragons, and covered us with the shadow of death.
\vs Psa 44:20 If we have forgotten the name of our God, or stretched out our hands to a strange god;
\vs Psa 44:21 Shall not God search this out? for he knoweth the secrets of the heart.
\vs Psa 44:22 Yea, for thy sake are we killed all the day long; we are counted as sheep for the slaughter.
\vs Psa 44:23 Awake, why sleepest thou, O Lord? arise, cast \bibemph{us} not off for ever.
\vs Psa 44:24 Wherefore hidest thou thy face, \bibemph{and} forgettest our affliction and our oppression?
\vs Psa 44:25 For our soul is bowed down to the dust: our belly cleaveth unto the earth.
\vs Psa 44:26 Arise for our help, and redeem us for thy mercies' sake.
\fn{for our...: Heb. a help for us.}
\vs Psa 45:1 To the chief Musician upon Shoshannim, for the sons of Korah, Maschil, A Song of loves. My heart is inditing a good matter: I speak of the things which I have made touching the king: my tongue \bibemph{is} the pen of a ready writer.
\fn{Maschil: or, of instruction. is inditing: Heb. boileth, or, bubbleth up.}
\vs Psa 45:2 Thou art fairer than the children of men: grace is poured into thy lips: therefore God hath blessed thee for ever.
\vs Psa 45:3 Gird thy sword upon \bibemph{thy} thigh, O \bibemph{most} mighty, with thy glory and thy majesty.
\vs Psa 45:4 And in thy majesty ride prosperously because of truth and meekness \bibemph{and} righteousness; and thy right hand shall teach thee terrible things.
\fn{ride...: Heb. prosper thou, ride thou.}
\vs Psa 45:5 Thine arrows \bibemph{are} sharp in the heart of the king's enemies; \bibemph{whereby} the people fall under thee.
\vs Psa 45:6 Thy throne, O God, \bibemph{is} for ever and ever: the sceptre of thy kingdom \bibemph{is} a right sceptre.
\vs Psa 45:7 Thou lovest righteousness, and hatest wickedness: therefore God, thy God, hath anointed thee with the oil of gladness above thy fellows.
\vs Psa 45:8 All thy garments \bibemph{smell} of myrrh, and aloes, \bibemph{and} cassia, out of the ivory palaces, whereby they have made thee glad.
\vs Psa 45:9 Kings' daughters \bibemph{were} among thy honourable women: upon thy right hand did stand the queen in gold of Ophir.
\vs Psa 45:10 Hearken, O daughter, and consider, and incline thine ear; forget also thine own people, and thy father's house;
\vs Psa 45:11 So shall the king greatly desire thy beauty: for he \bibemph{is} thy Lord; and worship thou him.
\vs Psa 45:12 And the daughter of Tyre \bibemph{shall be there} with a gift; \bibemph{even} the rich among the people shall intreat thy favour.
\fn{favour: Heb. face.}
\vs Psa 45:13 The king's daughter \bibemph{is} all glorious within: her clothing \bibemph{is} of wrought gold.
\vs Psa 45:14 She shall be brought unto the king in raiment of needlework: the virgins her companions that follow her shall be brought unto thee.
\vs Psa 45:15 With gladness and rejoicing shall they be brought: they shall enter into the king's palace.
\vs Psa 45:16 Instead of thy fathers shall be thy children, whom thou mayest make princes in all the earth.
\vs Psa 45:17 I will make thy name to be remembered in all generations: therefore shall the people praise thee for ever and ever.
