\vs Psa 49:1 To the chief Musician, A Psalm for the sons of Korah. Hear this, all \bibemph{ye} people; give ear, all \bibemph{ye} inhabitants of the world:
\fn{for: or, of.}
\vs Psa 49:2 Both low and high, rich and poor, together.
\vs Psa 49:3 My mouth shall speak of wisdom; and the meditation of my heart \bibemph{shall be} of understanding.
\vs Psa 49:4 I will incline mine ear to a parable: I will open my dark saying upon the harp.
\vs Psa 49:5 Wherefore should I fear in the days of evil, \bibemph{when} the iniquity of my heels shall compass me about?
\vs Psa 49:6 They that trust in their wealth, and boast themselves in the multitude of their riches;
\vs Psa 49:7 None \bibemph{of them} can by any means redeem his brother, nor give to God a ransom for him:
\vs Psa 49:8 (For the redemption of their soul \bibemph{is} precious, and it ceaseth for ever:)
\vs Psa 49:9 That he should still live for ever, \bibemph{and} not see corruption.
\vs Psa 49:10 For he seeth \bibemph{that} wise men die, likewise the fool and the brutish person perish, and leave their wealth to others.
\vs Psa 49:11 Their inward thought \bibemph{is, that} their houses \bibemph{shall continue} for ever, \bibemph{and} their dwelling places to all generations; they call \bibemph{their} lands after their own names.
\fn{all...: Heb. generation and generation.}
\vs Psa 49:12 Nevertheless man \bibemph{being} in honour abideth not: he is like the beasts \bibemph{that} perish.
\vs Psa 49:13 This their way \bibemph{is} their folly: yet their posterity approve their sayings. Selah.
\fn{approve...: Heb. delight in their mouth.}
\vs Psa 49:14 Like sheep they are laid in the grave; death shall feed on them; and the upright shall have dominion over them in the morning; and their beauty shall consume in the grave from their dwelling.
\fn{beauty: or, strength. in the grave from...: or, the grave being an habitation to every one of them.}
\vs Psa 49:15 But God will redeem my soul from the power of the grave: for he shall receive me. Selah.
\fn{power: Heb. hand. the grave: or, hell.}
\vs Psa 49:16 Be not thou afraid when one is made rich, when the glory of his house is increased;
\vs Psa 49:17 For when he dieth he shall carry nothing away: his glory shall not descend after him.
\vs Psa 49:18 Though while he lived he blessed his soul: and \bibemph{men} will praise thee, when thou doest well to thyself.
\fn{while...: Heb. in his life.}
\vs Psa 49:19 He shall go to the generation of his fathers; they shall never see light.
\fn{He...: Heb. The soul shall.}
\vs Psa 49:20 Man \bibemph{that is} in honour, and understandeth not, is like the beasts \bibemph{that} perish.
\vs Psa 50:1 A Psalm of Asaph. The mighty God, \bibemph{even} the \textsc{Lord}, hath spoken, and called the earth from the rising of the sun unto the going down thereof.
\fn{of...: or, for Asaph.}
\vs Psa 50:2 Out of Zion, the perfection of beauty, God hath shined.
\vs Psa 50:3 Our God shall come, and shall not keep silence: a fire shall devour before him, and it shall be very tempestuous round about him.
\vs Psa 50:4 He shall call to the heavens from above, and to the earth, that he may judge his people.
\vs Psa 50:5 Gather my saints together unto me; those that have made a covenant with me by sacrifice.
\vs Psa 50:6 And the heavens shall declare his righteousness: for God \bibemph{is} judge himself. Selah.
\vs Psa 50:7 Hear, O my people, and I will speak; O Israel, and I will testify against thee: I \bibemph{am} God, \bibemph{even} thy God.
\vs Psa 50:8 I will not reprove thee for thy sacrifices or thy burnt offerings, \bibemph{to have been} continually before me.
\vs Psa 50:9 I will take no bullock out of thy house, \bibemph{nor} he goats out of thy folds.
\vs Psa 50:10 For every beast of the forest \bibemph{is} mine, \bibemph{and} the cattle upon a thousand hills.
\vs Psa 50:11 I know all the fowls of the mountains: and the wild beasts of the field \bibemph{are} mine.
\fn{mine: Heb. with me.}
\vs Psa 50:12 If I were hungry, I would not tell thee: for the world \bibemph{is} mine, and the fulness thereof.
\vs Psa 50:13 Will I eat the flesh of bulls, or drink the blood of goats?
\vs Psa 50:14 Offer unto God thanksgiving; and pay thy vows unto the most High:
\vs Psa 50:15 And call upon me in the day of trouble: I will deliver thee, and thou shalt glorify me.
\vs Psa 50:16 But unto the wicked God saith, What hast thou to do to declare my statutes, or \bibemph{that} thou shouldest take my covenant in thy mouth?
\vs Psa 50:17 Seeing thou hatest instruction, and castest my words behind thee.
\vs Psa 50:18 When thou sawest a thief, then thou consentedst with him, and hast been partaker with adulterers.
\fn{hast...: Heb. thy portion was with.}
\vs Psa 50:19 Thou givest thy mouth to evil, and thy tongue frameth deceit.
\fn{givest: Heb. sendest.}
\vs Psa 50:20 Thou sittest \bibemph{and} speakest against thy brother; thou slanderest thine own mother's son.
\vs Psa 50:21 These \bibemph{things} hast thou done, and I kept silence; thou thoughtest that I was altogether \bibemph{such an one} as thyself: \bibemph{but} I will reprove thee, and set \bibemph{them} in order before thine eyes.
\vs Psa 50:22 Now consider this, ye that forget God, lest I tear \bibemph{you} in pieces, and \bibemph{there be} none to deliver.
\vs Psa 50:23 Whoso offereth praise glorifieth me: and to him that ordereth \bibemph{his} conversation \bibemph{aright} will I shew the salvation of God.
\fn{that...: Heb. that disposeth his way.}
\vs Psa 51:1 To the chief Musician, A Psalm of David, when Nathan the prophet came unto him, after he had gone in to Bathsheba. Have mercy upon me, O God, according to thy lovingkindness: according unto the multitude of thy tender mercies blot out my transgressions.
\vs Psa 51:2 Wash me throughly from mine iniquity, and cleanse me from my sin.
\vs Psa 51:3 For I acknowledge my transgressions: and my sin \bibemph{is} ever before me.
\vs Psa 51:4 Against thee, thee only, have I sinned, and done \bibemph{this} evil in thy sight: that thou mightest be justified when thou speakest, \bibemph{and} be clear when thou judgest.
\vs Psa 51:5 Behold, I was shapen in iniquity; and in sin did my mother conceive me.
\fn{conceive...: Heb. warm me.}
\vs Psa 51:6 Behold, thou desirest truth in the inward parts: and in the hidden \bibemph{part} thou shalt make me to know wisdom.
\vs Psa 51:7 Purge me with hyssop, and I shall be clean: wash me, and I shall be whiter than snow.
\vs Psa 51:8 Make me to hear joy and gladness; \bibemph{that} the bones \bibemph{which} thou hast broken may rejoice.
\vs Psa 51:9 Hide thy face from my sins, and blot out all mine iniquities.
\vs Psa 51:10 Create in me a clean heart, O God; and renew a right spirit within me.
\fn{right: or, constant.}
\vs Psa 51:11 Cast me not away from thy presence; and take not thy holy spirit from me.
\vs Psa 51:12 Restore unto me the joy of thy salvation; and uphold me \bibemph{with thy} free spirit.
\vs Psa 51:13 \bibemph{Then} will I teach transgressors thy ways; and sinners shall be converted unto thee.
\vs Psa 51:14 Deliver me from bloodguiltiness, O God, thou God of my salvation: \bibemph{and} my tongue shall sing aloud of thy righteousness.
\fn{bloodguiltiness: Heb. bloods.}
\vs Psa 51:15 O Lord, open thou my lips; and my mouth shall shew forth thy praise.
\vs Psa 51:16 For thou desirest not sacrifice; else would I give \bibemph{it}: thou delightest not in burnt offering.
\fn{else...: or, that I should.}
\vs Psa 51:17 The sacrifices of God \bibemph{are} a broken spirit: a broken and a contrite heart, O God, thou wilt not despise.
\vs Psa 51:18 Do good in thy good pleasure unto Zion: build thou the walls of Jerusalem.
\vs Psa 51:19 Then shalt thou be pleased with the sacrifices of righteousness, with burnt offering and whole burnt offering: then shall they offer bullocks upon thine altar.
\vs Psa 52:1 To the chief Musician, Maschil, \bibemph{A Psalm} of David, when Doeg the Edomite came and told Saul, and said unto him, David is come to the house of Ahimelech. Why boastest thou thyself in mischief, O mighty man? the goodness of God \bibemph{endureth} continually.
\vs Psa 52:2 Thy tongue deviseth mischiefs; like a sharp razor, working deceitfully.
\vs Psa 52:3 Thou lovest evil more than good; \bibemph{and} lying rather than to speak righteousness. Selah.
\vs Psa 52:4 Thou lovest all devouring words, O \bibemph{thou} deceitful tongue.
\fn{O thou...: or, and the deceitful tongue.}
\vs Psa 52:5 God shall likewise destroy thee for ever, he shall take thee away, and pluck thee out of \bibemph{thy} dwelling place, and root thee out of the land of the living. Selah.
\fn{destroy...: Heb. beat thee down.}
\vs Psa 52:6 The righteous also shall see, and fear, and shall laugh at him:
\vs Psa 52:7 Lo, \bibemph{this is} the man \bibemph{that} made not God his strength; but trusted in the abundance of his riches, \bibemph{and} strengthened himself in his wickedness.
\fn{wickedness: or, substance.}
\vs Psa 52:8 But I \bibemph{am} like a green olive tree in the house of God: I trust in the mercy of God for ever and ever.
\vs Psa 52:9 I will praise thee for ever, because thou hast done \bibemph{it}: and I will wait on thy name; for \bibemph{it is} good before thy saints.
\vs Psa 53:1 To the chief Musician upon Mahalath, Maschil, \bibemph{A Psalm} of David. The fool hath said in his heart, \bibemph{There is} no God. Corrupt are they, and have done abominable iniquity: \bibemph{there is} none that doeth good.
\vs Psa 53:2 God looked down from heaven upon the children of men, to see if there were \bibemph{any} that did understand, that did seek God.
\vs Psa 53:3 Every one of them is gone back: they are altogether become filthy; \bibemph{there is} none that doeth good, no, not one.
\vs Psa 53:4 Have the workers of iniquity no knowledge? who eat up my people \bibemph{as} they eat bread: they have not called upon God.
\vs Psa 53:5 There were they in great fear, \bibemph{where} no fear was: for God hath scattered the bones of him that encampeth \bibemph{against} thee: thou hast put \bibemph{them} to shame, because God hath despised them.
\fn{were...: Heb. they feared a fear.}
\vs Psa 53:6 Oh that the salvation of Israel \bibemph{were come} out of Zion! When God bringeth back the captivity of his people, Jacob shall rejoice, \bibemph{and} Israel shall be glad.
\fn{Oh that...: Heb. Who will give salvation, etc.}
\vs Psa 54:1 To the chief Musician on Neginoth, Maschil, \bibemph{A Psalm} of David, when the Ziphims came and said to Saul, Doth not David hide himself with us? Save me, O God, by thy name, and judge me by thy strength.
\vs Psa 54:2 Hear my prayer, O God; give ear to the words of my mouth.
\vs Psa 54:3 For strangers are risen up against me, and oppressors seek after my soul: they have not set God before them. Selah.
\vs Psa 54:4 Behold, God \bibemph{is} mine helper: the Lord \bibemph{is} with them that uphold my soul.
\vs Psa 54:5 He shall reward evil unto mine enemies: cut them off in thy truth.
\fn{mine...: Heb. those that observe me.}
\vs Psa 54:6 I will freely sacrifice unto thee: I will praise thy name, O \textsc{Lord}; for \bibemph{it is} good.
\vs Psa 54:7 For he hath delivered me out of all trouble: and mine eye hath seen \bibemph{his desire} upon mine enemies.
\vs Psa 55:1 To the chief Musician on Neginoth, Maschil, \bibemph{A Psalm} of David. Give ear to my prayer, O God; and hide not thyself from my supplication.
\vs Psa 55:2 Attend unto me, and hear me: I mourn in my complaint, and make a noise;
\vs Psa 55:3 Because of the voice of the enemy, because of the oppression of the wicked: for they cast iniquity upon me, and in wrath they hate me.
\vs Psa 55:4 My heart is sore pained within me: and the terrors of death are fallen upon me.
\vs Psa 55:5 Fearfulness and trembling are come upon me, and horror hath overwhelmed me.
\fn{overwhelmed: Heb. covered.}
\vs Psa 55:6 And I said, Oh that I had wings like a dove! \bibemph{for then} would I fly away, and be at rest.
\vs Psa 55:7 Lo, \bibemph{then} would I wander far off, \bibemph{and} remain in the wilderness. Selah.
\vs Psa 55:8 I would hasten my escape from the windy storm \bibemph{and} tempest.
\vs Psa 55:9 Destroy, O Lord, \bibemph{and} divide their tongues: for I have seen violence and strife in the city.
\vs Psa 55:10 Day and night they go about it upon the walls thereof: mischief also and sorrow \bibemph{are} in the midst of it.
\vs Psa 55:11 Wickedness \bibemph{is} in the midst thereof: deceit and guile depart not from her streets.
\vs Psa 55:12 For \bibemph{it was} not an enemy \bibemph{that} reproached me; then I could have borne \bibemph{it}: neither \bibemph{was it} he that hated me \bibemph{that} did magnify \bibemph{himself} against me; then I would have hid myself from him:
\vs Psa 55:13 But \bibemph{it was} thou, a man mine equal, my guide, and mine acquaintance.
\fn{mine equal: Heb. according to my rank.}
\vs Psa 55:14 We took sweet counsel together, \bibemph{and} walked unto the house of God in company.
\fn{We...: Heb. Who sweetened counsel.}
\vs Psa 55:15 Let death seize upon them, \bibemph{and} let them go down quick into hell: for wickedness \bibemph{is} in their dwellings, \bibemph{and} among them.
\fn{hell: or, the grave.}
\vs Psa 55:16 As for me, I will call upon God; and the \textsc{Lord} shall save me.
\vs Psa 55:17 Evening, and morning, and at noon, will I pray, and cry aloud: and he shall hear my voice.
\vs Psa 55:18 He hath delivered my soul in peace from the battle \bibemph{that was} against me: for there were many with me.
\vs Psa 55:19 God shall hear, and afflict them, even he that abideth of old. Selah. Because they have no changes, therefore they fear not God.
\fn{Because...: or, With whom also there be no changes, yet they.}
\vs Psa 55:20 He hath put forth his hands against such as be at peace with him: he hath broken his covenant.
\fn{broken: Heb. profaned.}
\vs Psa 55:21 \bibemph{The words} of his mouth were smoother than butter, but war \bibemph{was} in his heart: his words were softer than oil, yet \bibemph{were} they drawn swords.
\vs Psa 55:22 Cast thy burden upon the \textsc{Lord}, and he shall sustain thee: he shall never suffer the righteous to be moved.
\fn{burden: or, gift.}
\vs Psa 55:23 But thou, O God, shalt bring them down into the pit of destruction: bloody and deceitful men shall not live out half their days; but I will trust in thee.
\fn{bloody...: Heb. men of bloods and deceit. shall...: Heb. shall not half their days.}
\vs Psa 56:1 To the chief Musician upon Jonathelemrechokim, Michtam of David, when the Philistines took him in Gath. Be merciful unto me, O God: for man would swallow me up; he fighting daily oppresseth me.
\fn{Michtam...: or, A golden Psalm of David.}
\vs Psa 56:2 Mine enemies would daily swallow \bibemph{me} up: for \bibemph{they be} many that fight against me, O thou most High.
\fn{enemies: Heb. observers.}
\vs Psa 56:3 What time I am afraid, I will trust in thee.
\vs Psa 56:4 In God I will praise his word, in God I have put my trust; I will not fear what flesh can do unto me.
\vs Psa 56:5 Every day they wrest my words: all their thoughts \bibemph{are} against me for evil.
\vs Psa 56:6 They gather themselves together, they hide themselves, they mark my steps, when they wait for my soul.
\vs Psa 56:7 Shall they escape by iniquity? in \bibemph{thine} anger cast down the people, O God.
\vs Psa 56:8 Thou tellest my wanderings: put thou my tears into thy bottle: \bibemph{are they} not in thy book?
\vs Psa 56:9 When I cry \bibemph{unto thee}, then shall mine enemies turn back: this I know; for God \bibemph{is} for me.
\vs Psa 56:10 In God will I praise \bibemph{his} word: in the \textsc{Lord} will I praise \bibemph{his} word.
\vs Psa 56:11 In God have I put my trust: I will not be afraid what man can do unto me.
\vs Psa 56:12 Thy vows \bibemph{are} upon me, O God: I will render praises unto thee.
\vs Psa 56:13 For thou hast delivered my soul from death: \bibemph{wilt} not \bibemph{thou deliver} my feet from falling, that I may walk before God in the light of the living?
\vs Psa 57:1 To the chief Musician, Altaschith, Michtam of David, when he fled from Saul in the cave. Be merciful unto me, O God, be merciful unto me: for my soul trusteth in thee: yea, in the shadow of thy wings will I make my refuge, until \bibemph{these} calamities be overpast.
\fn{Altaschith: or, Destroy not.}
\vs Psa 57:2 I will cry unto God most high; unto God that performeth \bibemph{all things} for me.
\vs Psa 57:3 He shall send from heaven, and save me \bibemph{from} the reproach of him that would swallow me up. Selah. God shall send forth his mercy and his truth.
\fn{from the...: or, he reproacheth him that.}
\vs Psa 57:4 My soul \bibemph{is} among lions: \bibemph{and} I lie \bibemph{even among} them that are set on fire, \bibemph{even} the sons of men, whose teeth \bibemph{are} spears and arrows, and their tongue a sharp sword.
\vs Psa 57:5 Be thou exalted, O God, above the heavens; \bibemph{let} thy glory \bibemph{be} above all the earth.
\vs Psa 57:6 They have prepared a net for my steps; my soul is bowed down: they have digged a pit before me, into the midst whereof they are fallen \bibemph{themselves}. Selah.
\vs Psa 57:7 My heart is fixed, O God, my heart is fixed: I will sing and give praise.
\fn{fixed: or, prepared.}
\vs Psa 57:8 Awake up, my glory; awake, psaltery and harp: I \bibemph{myself} will awake early.
\vs Psa 57:9 I will praise thee, O Lord, among the people: I will sing unto thee among the nations.
\vs Psa 57:10 For thy mercy \bibemph{is} great unto the heavens, and thy truth unto the clouds.
\vs Psa 57:11 Be thou exalted, O God, above the heavens: \bibemph{let} thy glory \bibemph{be} above all the earth.
\vs Psa 58:1 To the chief Musician, Altaschith, Michtam of David. Do ye indeed speak righteousness, O congregation? do ye judge uprightly, O ye sons of men?
\fn{Altaschith...: or, Destroy not, A golden Psalm of David.}
\vs Psa 58:2 Yea, in heart ye work wickedness; ye weigh the violence of your hands in the earth.
\vs Psa 58:3 The wicked are estranged from the womb: they go astray as soon as they be born, speaking lies.
\fn{as soon...: Heb. from the belly.}
\vs Psa 58:4 Their poison \bibemph{is} like the poison of a serpent: \bibemph{they are} like the deaf adder \bibemph{that} stoppeth her ear;
\fn{like the poison: Heb. according to the likeness, etc. adder: or, asp.}
\vs Psa 58:5 Which will not hearken to the voice of charmers, charming never so wisely.
\fn{charming...: or, be the charmer never so cunning.}
\vs Psa 58:6 Break their teeth, O God, in their mouth: break out the great teeth of the young lions, O \textsc{Lord}.
\vs Psa 58:7 Let them melt away as waters \bibemph{which} run continually: \bibemph{when} he bendeth \bibemph{his bow to shoot} his arrows, let them be as cut in pieces.
\vs Psa 58:8 As a snail \bibemph{which} melteth, let \bibemph{every one of them} pass away: \bibemph{like} the untimely birth of a woman, \bibemph{that} they may not see the sun.
\vs Psa 58:9 Before your pots can feel the thorns, he shall take them away as with a whirlwind, both living, and in \bibemph{his} wrath.
\fn{both...: Heb. as living as wrath.}
\vs Psa 58:10 The righteous shall rejoice when he seeth the vengeance: he shall wash his feet in the blood of the wicked.
\vs Psa 58:11 So that a man shall say, Verily \bibemph{there is} a reward for the righteous: verily he is a God that judgeth in the earth.
\fn{a reward...: Heb. fruit of the, etc.}
\vs Psa 59:1 To the chief Musician, Altaschith, Michtam of David; when Saul sent, and they watched the house to kill him. Deliver me from mine enemies, O my God: defend me from them that rise up against me.
\fn{Altaschith...: or, Destroy not, A golden Psalm of David. defend...: Heb. set me on high.}
\vs Psa 59:2 Deliver me from the workers of iniquity, and save me from bloody men.
\vs Psa 59:3 For, lo, they lie in wait for my soul: the mighty are gathered against me; not \bibemph{for} my transgression, nor \bibemph{for} my sin, O \textsc{Lord}.
\vs Psa 59:4 They run and prepare themselves without \bibemph{my} fault: awake to help me, and behold.
\fn{help: Heb. meet.}
\vs Psa 59:5 Thou therefore, O \textsc{Lord} God of hosts, the God of Israel, awake to visit all the heathen: be not merciful to any wicked transgressors. Selah.
\vs Psa 59:6 They return at evening: they make a noise like a dog, and go round about the city.
\vs Psa 59:7 Behold, they belch out with their mouth: swords \bibemph{are} in their lips: for who, \bibemph{say they}, doth hear?
\vs Psa 59:8 But thou, O \textsc{Lord}, shalt laugh at them; thou shalt have all the heathen in derision.
\vs Psa 59:9 \bibemph{Because of} his strength will I wait upon thee: for God \bibemph{is} my defence.
\fn{defence: Heb. high place.}
\vs Psa 59:10 The God of my mercy shall prevent me: God shall let me see \bibemph{my desire} upon mine enemies.
\fn{enemies: Heb. observers.}
\vs Psa 59:11 Slay them not, lest my people forget: scatter them by thy power; and bring them down, O Lord our shield.
\vs Psa 59:12 \bibemph{For} the sin of their mouth \bibemph{and} the words of their lips let them even be taken in their pride: and for cursing and lying \bibemph{which} they speak.
\vs Psa 59:13 Consume \bibemph{them} in wrath, consume \bibemph{them}, that they \bibemph{may} not \bibemph{be}: and let them know that God ruleth in Jacob unto the ends of the earth. Selah.
\vs Psa 59:14 And at evening let them return; \bibemph{and} let them make a noise like a dog, and go round about the city.
\vs Psa 59:15 Let them wander up and down for meat, and grudge if they be not satisfied.
\fn{for meat: Heb. to eat. and grudge...: or, if they be not satisfied, then they will stay all night.}
\vs Psa 59:16 But I will sing of thy power; yea, I will sing aloud of thy mercy in the morning: for thou hast been my defence and refuge in the day of my trouble.
\vs Psa 59:17 Unto thee, O my strength, will I sing: for God \bibemph{is} my defence, \bibemph{and} the God of my mercy.
\vs Psa 60:1 To the chief Musician upon Shushaneduth, Michtam of David, to teach; when he strove with Aramnaharaim and with Aramzobah, when Joab returned, and smote of Edom in the valley of salt twelve thousand. O God, thou hast cast us off, thou hast scattered us, thou hast been displeased; O turn thyself to us again.
\fn{Michtam: or, A golden Psalm. scattered: Heb. broken.}
\vs Psa 60:2 Thou hast made the earth to tremble; thou hast broken it: heal the breaches thereof; for it shaketh.
\vs Psa 60:3 Thou hast shewed thy people hard things: thou hast made us to drink the wine of astonishment.
\vs Psa 60:4 Thou hast given a banner to them that fear thee, that it may be displayed because of the truth. Selah.
\vs Psa 60:5 That thy beloved may be delivered; save \bibemph{with} thy right hand, and hear me.
\vs Psa 60:6 God hath spoken in his holiness; I will rejoice, I will divide Shechem, and mete out the valley of Succoth.
\vs Psa 60:7 Gilead \bibemph{is} mine, and Manasseh \bibemph{is} mine; Ephraim also \bibemph{is} the strength of mine head; Judah \bibemph{is} my lawgiver;
\vs Psa 60:8 Moab \bibemph{is} my washpot; over Edom will I cast out my shoe: Philistia, triumph thou because of me.
\fn{triumph...: or, triumph thou over me: (by an irony).}
\vs Psa 60:9 Who will bring me \bibemph{into} the strong city? who will lead me into Edom?
\fn{strong...: Heb. city of strength?.}
\vs Psa 60:10 \bibemph{Wilt} not thou, O God, \bibemph{which} hadst cast us off? and \bibemph{thou}, O God, \bibemph{which} didst not go out with our armies?
\vs Psa 60:11 Give us help from trouble: for vain \bibemph{is} the help of man.
\fn{help of man: Heb. salvation, etc.}
\vs Psa 60:12 Through God we shall do valiantly: for he \bibemph{it is that} shall tread down our enemies.
\vs Psa 61:1 To the chief Musician upon Neginah, \bibemph{A Psalm} of David. Hear my cry, O God; attend unto my prayer.
\vs Psa 61:2 From the end of the earth will I cry unto thee, when my heart is overwhelmed: lead me to the rock \bibemph{that} is higher than I.
\vs Psa 61:3 For thou hast been a shelter for me, \bibemph{and} a strong tower from the enemy.
\vs Psa 61:4 I will abide in thy tabernacle for ever: I will trust in the covert of thy wings. Selah.
\fn{trust: or, make my refuge.}
\vs Psa 61:5 For thou, O God, hast heard my vows: thou hast given \bibemph{me} the heritage of those that fear thy name.
\vs Psa 61:6 Thou wilt prolong the king's life: \bibemph{and} his years as many generations.
\fn{Thou...: Heb. Thou shalt add days to the days of the king. as...: Heb. as generation and generation.}
\vs Psa 61:7 He shall abide before God for ever: O prepare mercy and truth, \bibemph{which} may preserve him.
\vs Psa 61:8 So will I sing praise unto thy name for ever, that I may daily perform my vows.
\vs Psa 62:1 To the chief Musician, to Jeduthun, A Psalm of David. Truly my soul waiteth upon God: from him \bibemph{cometh} my salvation.
\fn{Truly: or, Only. waiteth: Heb. is silent.}
\vs Psa 62:2 He only \bibemph{is} my rock and my salvation; \bibemph{he is} my defence; I shall not be greatly moved.
\fn{defence: Heb. high place.}
\vs Psa 62:3 How long will ye imagine mischief against a man? ye shall be slain all of you: as a bowing wall \bibemph{shall ye be, and as} a tottering fence.
\vs Psa 62:4 They only consult to cast \bibemph{him} down from his excellency: they delight in lies: they bless with their mouth, but they curse inwardly. Selah.
\fn{inwardly: Heb. in their inward parts.}
\vs Psa 62:5 My soul, wait thou only upon God; for my expectation \bibemph{is} from him.
\vs Psa 62:6 He only \bibemph{is} my rock and my salvation: \bibemph{he is} my defence; I shall not be moved.
\vs Psa 62:7 In God \bibemph{is} my salvation and my glory: the rock of my strength, \bibemph{and} my refuge, \bibemph{is} in God.
\vs Psa 62:8 Trust in him at all times; \bibemph{ye} people, pour out your heart before him: God \bibemph{is} a refuge for us. Selah.
\vs Psa 62:9 Surely men of low degree \bibemph{are} vanity, \bibemph{and} men of high degree \bibemph{are} a lie: to be laid in the balance, they \bibemph{are} altogether \bibemph{lighter} than vanity.
\fn{altogether: or, alike.}
\vs Psa 62:10 Trust not in oppression, and become not vain in robbery: if riches increase, set not your heart \bibemph{upon them}.
\vs Psa 62:11 God hath spoken once; twice have I heard this; that power \bibemph{belongeth} unto God.
\fn{power: or, strength.}
\vs Psa 62:12 Also unto thee, O Lord, \bibemph{belongeth} mercy: for thou renderest to every man according to his work.
\vs Psa 63:1 A Psalm of David, when he was in the wilderness of Judah. O God, thou \bibemph{art} my God; early will I seek thee: my soul thirsteth for thee, my flesh longeth for thee in a dry and thirsty land, where no water is;
\fn{thirsty: Heb. weary. where...: without water.}
\vs Psa 63:2 To see thy power and thy glory, so \bibemph{as} I have seen thee in the sanctuary.
\vs Psa 63:3 Because thy lovingkindness \bibemph{is} better than life, my lips shall praise thee.
\vs Psa 63:4 Thus will I bless thee while I live: I will lift up my hands in thy name.
\vs Psa 63:5 My soul shall be satisfied as \bibemph{with} marrow and fatness; and my mouth shall praise \bibemph{thee} with joyful lips:
\fn{marrow: Heb. fatness.}
\vs Psa 63:6 When I remember thee upon my bed, \bibemph{and} meditate on thee in the \bibemph{night} watches.
\vs Psa 63:7 Because thou hast been my help, therefore in the shadow of thy wings will I rejoice.
\vs Psa 63:8 My soul followeth hard after thee: thy right hand upholdeth me.
\vs Psa 63:9 But those \bibemph{that} seek my soul, to destroy \bibemph{it}, shall go into the lower parts of the earth.
\vs Psa 63:10 They shall fall by the sword: they shall be a portion for foxes.
\fn{They shall fall...: Heb. They shall make him run out like water by the hands of.}
\vs Psa 63:11 But the king shall rejoice in God; every one that sweareth by him shall glory: but the mouth of them that speak lies shall be stopped.
\vs Psa 64:1 To the chief Musician, A Psalm of David. Hear my voice, O God, in my prayer: preserve my life from fear of the enemy.
\vs Psa 64:2 Hide me from the secret counsel of the wicked; from the insurrection of the workers of iniquity:
\vs Psa 64:3 Who whet their tongue like a sword, \bibemph{and} bend \bibemph{their bows to shoot} their arrows, \bibemph{even} bitter words:
\vs Psa 64:4 That they may shoot in secret at the perfect: suddenly do they shoot at him, and fear not.
\vs Psa 64:5 They encourage themselves \bibemph{in} an evil matter: they commune of laying snares privily; they say, Who shall see them?
\fn{matter: or, speech. of...: Heb. to hide his snares.}
\vs Psa 64:6 They search out iniquities; they accomplish a diligent search: both the inward \bibemph{thought} of every one \bibemph{of them}, and the heart, \bibemph{is} deep.
\fn{they...: or, we are consumed by that which they have throughly searched. a diligent...: Heb. a search searched.}
\vs Psa 64:7 But God shall shoot at them \bibemph{with} an arrow; suddenly shall they be wounded.
\fn{shall they...: Heb. their wound shall be.}
\vs Psa 64:8 So they shall make their own tongue to fall upon themselves: all that see them shall flee away.
\vs Psa 64:9 And all men shall fear, and shall declare the work of God; for they shall wisely consider of his doing.
\vs Psa 64:10 The righteous shall be glad in the \textsc{Lord}, and shall trust in him; and all the upright in heart shall glory.
\vs Psa 65:1 To the chief Musician, A Psalm \bibemph{and} Song of David. Praise waiteth for thee, O God, in Sion: and unto thee shall the vow be performed.
\fn{waiteth: Heb. is silent.}
\vs Psa 65:2 O thou that hearest prayer, unto thee shall all flesh come.
\vs Psa 65:3 Iniquities prevail against me: \bibemph{as for} our transgressions, thou shalt purge them away.
\fn{iniquities: Heb. Words, or, Matters of iniquities.}
\vs Psa 65:4 Blessed \bibemph{is the man whom} thou choosest, and causest to approach \bibemph{unto thee, that} he may dwell in thy courts: we shall be satisfied with the goodness of thy house, \bibemph{even} of thy holy temple.
\vs Psa 65:5 \bibemph{By} terrible things in righteousness wilt thou answer us, O God of our salvation; \bibemph{who art} the confidence of all the ends of the earth, and of them that are afar off \bibemph{upon} the sea:
\vs Psa 65:6 Which by his strength setteth fast the mountains; \bibemph{being} girded with power:
\vs Psa 65:7 Which stilleth the noise of the seas, the noise of their waves, and the tumult of the people.
\vs Psa 65:8 They also that dwell in the uttermost parts are afraid at thy tokens: thou makest the outgoings of the morning and evening to rejoice.
\fn{rejoice: or, sing.}
\vs Psa 65:9 Thou visitest the earth, and waterest it: thou greatly enrichest it with the river of God, \bibemph{which} is full of water: thou preparest them corn, when thou hast so provided for it.
\fn{and...: or, after thou hadst made it to desire rain.}
\vs Psa 65:10 Thou waterest the ridges thereof abundantly: thou settlest the furrows thereof: thou makest it soft with showers: thou blessest the springing thereof.
\fn{settlest: or, causest rain to descend into. makest...: Heb. dissolvest it.}
\vs Psa 65:11 Thou crownest the year with thy goodness; and thy paths drop fatness.
\fn{with: Heb. of.}
\vs Psa 65:12 They drop \bibemph{upon} the pastures of the wilderness: and the little hills rejoice on every side.
\fn{rejoice...: Heb. are girded with joy.}
\vs Psa 65:13 The pastures are clothed with flocks; the valleys also are covered over with corn; they shout for joy, they also sing.
\vs Psa 66:1 To the chief Musician, A Song \bibemph{or} Psalm. Make a joyful noise unto God, all ye lands:
\fn{all...: Heb. all the earth.}
\vs Psa 66:2 Sing forth the honour of his name: make his praise glorious.
\vs Psa 66:3 Say unto God, How terrible \bibemph{art thou in} thy works! through the greatness of thy power shall thine enemies submit themselves unto thee.
\fn{submit...: or, yield feigned obedience: Heb. lie.}
\vs Psa 66:4 All the earth shall worship thee, and shall sing unto thee; they shall sing \bibemph{to} thy name. Selah.
\vs Psa 66:5 Come and see the works of God: \bibemph{he is} terrible \bibemph{in his} doing toward the children of men.
\vs Psa 66:6 He turned the sea into dry \bibemph{land}: they went through the flood on foot: there did we rejoice in him.
\vs Psa 66:7 He ruleth by his power for ever; his eyes behold the nations: let not the rebellious exalt themselves. Selah.
\vs Psa 66:8 O bless our God, ye people, and make the voice of his praise to be heard:
\vs Psa 66:9 Which holdeth our soul in life, and suffereth not our feet to be moved.
\fn{holdeth: Heb. putteth.}
\vs Psa 66:10 For thou, O God, hast proved us: thou hast tried us, as silver is tried.
\vs Psa 66:11 Thou broughtest us into the net; thou laidst affliction upon our loins.
\vs Psa 66:12 Thou hast caused men to ride over our heads; we went through fire and through water: but thou broughtest us out into a wealthy \bibemph{place}.
\fn{wealthy: Heb. moist.}
\vs Psa 66:13 I will go into thy house with burnt offerings: I will pay thee my vows,
\vs Psa 66:14 Which my lips have uttered, and my mouth hath spoken, when I was in trouble.
\fn{uttered: Heb. opened.}
\vs Psa 66:15 I will offer unto thee burnt sacrifices of fatlings, with the incense of rams; I will offer bullocks with goats. Selah.
\fn{fatlings: Heb. marrow.}
\vs Psa 66:16 Come \bibemph{and} hear, all ye that fear God, and I will declare what he hath done for my soul.
\vs Psa 66:17 I cried unto him with my mouth, and he was extolled with my tongue.
\vs Psa 66:18 If I regard iniquity in my heart, the Lord will not hear \bibemph{me}:
\vs Psa 66:19 \bibemph{But} verily God hath heard \bibemph{me}; he hath attended to the voice of my prayer.
\vs Psa 66:20 Blessed \bibemph{be} God, which hath not turned away my prayer, nor his mercy from me.

\vs Psa 67:2 That thy way may be known upon earth, thy saving health among all nations.

\vs Psa 68:1 To the chief Musician, A Psalm \bibemph{or} Song of David. Let God arise, let his enemies be scattered: let them also that hate him flee before him.
\fn{before...: Heb. from his face.}

\vs Psa 68:3 But let the righteous be glad; let them rejoice before God: yea, let them exceedingly rejoice.
\fn{exceedingly...: Heb. rejoice with gladness.}
\vs Psa 68:4 Sing unto God, sing praises to his name: extol him that rideth upon the heavens by his name JAH, and rejoice before him.
\vs Psa 68:5 A father of the fatherless, and a judge of the widows, \bibemph{is} God in his holy habitation.
\vs Psa 68:6 God setteth the solitary in families: he bringeth out those which are bound with chains: but the rebellious dwell in a dry \bibemph{land}.
\fn{in families: Heb. in a house.}
\vs Psa 68:7 O God, when thou wentest forth before thy people, when thou didst march through the wilderness; Selah:
\vs Psa 68:8 The earth shook, the heavens also dropped at the presence of God: \bibemph{even} Sinai itself \bibemph{was moved} at the presence of God, the God of Israel.
\vs Psa 68:9 Thou, O God, didst send a plentiful rain, whereby thou didst confirm thine inheritance, when it was weary.
\fn{send: Heb. shake out. confirm: Heb. confirm it.}
\vs Psa 68:10 Thy congregation hath dwelt therein: thou, O God, hast prepared of thy goodness for the poor.
\vs Psa 68:11 The Lord gave the word: great \bibemph{was} the company of those that published \bibemph{it}.
\fn{company: Heb. army.}
\vs Psa 68:12 Kings of armies did flee apace: and she that tarried at home divided the spoil.
\fn{did...: Heb. did flee, did flee.}
\vs Psa 68:13 Though ye have lien among the pots, \bibemph{yet shall ye be as} the wings of a dove covered with silver, and her feathers with yellow gold.
\vs Psa 68:14 When the Almighty scattered kings in it, it was \bibemph{white} as snow in Salmon.
\fn{in it...: or, for her, she.}

\vs Psa 68:16 Why leap ye, ye high hills? \bibemph{this is} the hill \bibemph{which} God desireth to dwell in; yea, the \textsc{Lord} will dwell \bibemph{in it} for ever.
\vs Psa 68:17 The chariots of God \bibemph{are} twenty thousand, \bibemph{even} thousands of angels: the Lord \bibemph{is} among them, \bibemph{as in} Sinai, in the holy \bibemph{place}.
\fn{even...: or, even many thousands.}
\vs Psa 68:18 Thou hast ascended on high, thou hast led captivity captive: thou hast received gifts for men; yea, \bibemph{for} the rebellious also, that the \textsc{Lord} God might dwell \bibemph{among them}.
\fn{for men: Heb. in the man.}
\vs Psa 68:19 Blessed \bibemph{be} the Lord, \bibemph{who} daily loadeth us \bibemph{with benefits, even} the God of our salvation. Selah.
\vs Psa 68:20 \bibemph{He that is} our God \bibemph{is} the God of salvation; and unto GOD the Lord \bibemph{belong} the issues from death.
\vs Psa 68:21 But God shall wound the head of his enemies, \bibemph{and} the hairy scalp of such an one as goeth on still in his trespasses.
\vs Psa 68:22 The Lord said, I will bring again from Bashan, I will bring \bibemph{my people} again from the depths of the sea:
\vs Psa 68:23 That thy foot may be dipped in the blood of \bibemph{thine} enemies, \bibemph{and} the tongue of thy dogs in the same.
\fn{dipped: or, red.}

\vs Psa 68:25 The singers went before, the players on instruments \bibemph{followed} after; among \bibemph{them were} the damsels playing with timbrels.

\fn{from...: or, ye that are of the fountain of Israel.}
\vs Psa 68:27 There \bibemph{is} little Benjamin \bibemph{with} their ruler, the princes of Judah \bibemph{and} their council, the princes of Zebulun, \bibemph{and} the princes of Naphtali.
\fn{and their...: or, with their company.}

\vs Psa 68:29 Because of thy temple at Jerusalem shall kings bring presents unto thee.

\fn{the company...: or, the beasts of the reeds. scatter...: or, he scattereth.}

\fn{send...: Heb. give.}
