\fn{clouds: or, heavens.}
\vs Psa 68:35 O God, \bibemph{thou art} terrible out of thy holy places: the God of Israel \bibemph{is} he that giveth strength and power unto \bibemph{his} people. Blessed \bibemph{be} God.
\vs Psa 69:1 To the chief Musician upon Shoshannim, \bibemph{A Psalm} of David. Save me, O God; for the waters are come in unto \bibemph{my} soul.
\vs Psa 69:2 I sink in deep mire, where \bibemph{there is} no standing: I am come into deep waters, where the floods overflow me.
\fn{deep mire: Heb. the mire of depth. deep waters: Heb. depth of waters.}
\vs Psa 69:3 I am weary of my crying: my throat is dried: mine eyes fail while I wait for my God.
\vs Psa 69:4 They that hate me without a cause are more than the hairs of mine head: they that would destroy me, \bibemph{being} mine enemies wrongfully, are mighty: then I restored \bibemph{that} which I took not away.
\vs Psa 69:5 O God, thou knowest my foolishness; and my sins are not hid from thee.
\fn{sins: Heb. guiltiness.}
\vs Psa 69:6 Let not them that wait on thee, O Lord GOD of hosts, be ashamed for my sake: let not those that seek thee be confounded for my sake, O God of Israel.
\vs Psa 69:7 Because for thy sake I have borne reproach; shame hath covered my face.
\vs Psa 69:8 I am become a stranger unto my brethren, and an alien unto my mother's children.
\vs Psa 69:9 For the zeal of thine house hath eaten me up; and the reproaches of them that reproached thee are fallen upon me.
\vs Psa 69:10 When I wept, \bibemph{and chastened} my soul with fasting, that was to my reproach.
\vs Psa 69:11 I made sackcloth also my garment; and I became a proverb to them.
\vs Psa 69:12 They that sit in the gate speak against me; and I \bibemph{was} the song of the drunkards.
\fn{drunkards: Heb. drinkers of strong drink.}
\vs Psa 69:13 But as for me, my prayer \bibemph{is} unto thee, O \textsc{Lord}, \bibemph{in} an acceptable time: O God, in the multitude of thy mercy hear me, in the truth of thy salvation.
\vs Psa 69:14 Deliver me out of the mire, and let me not sink: let me be delivered from them that hate me, and out of the deep waters.
\vs Psa 69:15 Let not the waterflood overflow me, neither let the deep swallow me up, and let not the pit shut her mouth upon me.
\vs Psa 69:16 Hear me, O \textsc{Lord}; for thy lovingkindness \bibemph{is} good: turn unto me according to the multitude of thy tender mercies.
\vs Psa 69:17 And hide not thy face from thy servant; for I am in trouble: hear me speedily.
\fn{hear...: Heb. make haste to hear me.}
\vs Psa 69:18 Draw nigh unto my soul, \bibemph{and} redeem it: deliver me because of mine enemies.
\vs Psa 69:19 Thou hast known my reproach, and my shame, and my dishonour: mine adversaries \bibemph{are} all before thee.
\vs Psa 69:20 Reproach hath broken my heart; and I am full of heaviness: and I looked \bibemph{for some} to take pity, but \bibemph{there was} none; and for comforters, but I found none.
\fn{to take...: Heb. to lament with me.}
\vs Psa 69:21 They gave me also gall for my meat; and in my thirst they gave me vinegar to drink.
\vs Psa 69:22 Let their table become a snare before them: and \bibemph{that which should have been} for \bibemph{their} welfare, \bibemph{let it become} a trap.
\vs Psa 69:23 Let their eyes be darkened, that they see not; and make their loins continually to shake.
\vs Psa 69:24 Pour out thine indignation upon them, and let thy wrathful anger take hold of them.
\vs Psa 69:25 Let their habitation be desolate; \bibemph{and} let none dwell in their tents.
\fn{their habitation: Heb. their palace. let none...: Heb. let there not be a dweller.}
\vs Psa 69:26 For they persecute \bibemph{him} whom thou hast smitten; and they talk to the grief of those whom thou hast wounded.
\fn{those...: Heb. thy wounded.}
\vs Psa 69:27 Add iniquity unto their iniquity: and let them not come into thy righteousness.
\fn{iniquity unto...: or, punishment of iniquity, etc.}
\vs Psa 69:28 Let them be blotted out of the book of the living, and not be written with the righteous.
\vs Psa 69:29 But I \bibemph{am} poor and sorrowful: let thy salvation, O God, set me up on high.
\vs Psa 69:30 I will praise the name of God with a song, and will magnify him with thanksgiving.
\vs Psa 69:31 \bibemph{This} also shall please the \textsc{Lord} better than an ox \bibemph{or} bullock that hath horns and hoofs.
\vs Psa 69:32 The humble shall see \bibemph{this, and} be glad: and your heart shall live that seek God.
\fn{humble: or, meek.}
\vs Psa 69:33 For the \textsc{Lord} heareth the poor, and despiseth not his prisoners.
\vs Psa 69:34 Let the heaven and earth praise him, the seas, and every thing that moveth therein.
\fn{moveth: Heb. creepeth.}
\vs Psa 69:35 For God will save Zion, and will build the cities of Judah: that they may dwell there, and have it in possession.
\vs Psa 69:36 The seed also of his servants shall inherit it: and they that love his name shall dwell therein.
\vs Psa 70:1 To the chief Musician, \bibemph{A Psalm} of David, to bring to remembrance. \bibemph{Make haste}, O God, to deliver me; make haste to help me, O \textsc{Lord}.
\fn{to help...: Heb. to my help.}
\vs Psa 70:2 Let them be ashamed and confounded that seek after my soul: let them be turned backward, and put to confusion, that desire my hurt.
\vs Psa 70:3 Let them be turned back for a reward of their shame that say, Aha, aha.
\vs Psa 70:4 Let all those that seek thee rejoice and be glad in thee: and let such as love thy salvation say continually, Let God be magnified.
\vs Psa 70:5 But I \bibemph{am} poor and needy: make haste unto me, O God: thou \bibemph{art} my help and my deliverer; O \textsc{Lord}, make no tarrying.
\vs Psa 71:1 In thee, O \textsc{Lord}, do I put my trust: let me never be put to confusion.
\vs Psa 71:2 Deliver me in thy righteousness, and cause me to escape: incline thine ear unto me, and save me.
\vs Psa 71:3 Be thou my strong habitation, whereunto I may continually resort: thou hast given commandment to save me; for thou \bibemph{art} my rock and my fortress.
\fn{Be...: Heb. Be thou to me for a rock of habitation.}
\vs Psa 71:4 Deliver me, O my God, out of the hand of the wicked, out of the hand of the unrighteous and cruel man.
\vs Psa 71:5 For thou \bibemph{art} my hope, O Lord GOD: \bibemph{thou art} my trust from my youth.
\vs Psa 71:6 By thee have I been holden up from the womb: thou art he that took me out of my mother's bowels: my praise \bibemph{shall be} continually of thee.
\vs Psa 71:7 I am as a wonder unto many; but thou \bibemph{art} my strong refuge.
\vs Psa 71:8 Let my mouth be filled \bibemph{with} thy praise \bibemph{and with} thy honour all the day.
\vs Psa 71:9 Cast me not off in the time of old age; forsake me not when my strength faileth.
\vs Psa 71:10 For mine enemies speak against me; and they that lay wait for my soul take counsel together,
\fn{lay...: Heb. watch, or, observe.}
\vs Psa 71:11 Saying, God hath forsaken him: persecute and take him; for \bibemph{there is} none to deliver \bibemph{him}.
\vs Psa 71:12 O God, be not far from me: O my God, make haste for my help.
\vs Psa 71:13 Let them be confounded \bibemph{and} consumed that are adversaries to my soul; let them be covered \bibemph{with} reproach and dishonour that seek my hurt.
\vs Psa 71:14 But I will hope continually, and will yet praise thee more and more.
\vs Psa 71:15 My mouth shall shew forth thy righteousness \bibemph{and} thy salvation all the day; for I know not the numbers \bibemph{thereof}.
\vs Psa 71:16 I will go in the strength of the Lord GOD: I will make mention of thy righteousness, \bibemph{even} of thine only.
\vs Psa 71:17 O God, thou hast taught me from my youth: and hitherto have I declared thy wondrous works.
\vs Psa 71:18 Now also when I am old and grayheaded, O God, forsake me not; until I have shewed thy strength unto \bibemph{this} generation, \bibemph{and} thy power to every one \bibemph{that} is to come.
\fn{when...: Heb. unto old age and gray hairs. thy strength: Heb. thine arm.}
\vs Psa 71:19 Thy righteousness also, O God, \bibemph{is} very high, who hast done great things: O God, who \bibemph{is} like unto thee!
\vs Psa 71:20 \bibemph{Thou}, which hast shewed me great and sore troubles, shalt quicken me again, and shalt bring me up again from the depths of the earth.
\vs Psa 71:21 Thou shalt increase my greatness, and comfort me on every side.
\vs Psa 71:22 I will also praise thee with the psaltery, \bibemph{even} thy truth, O my God: unto thee will I sing with the harp, O thou Holy One of Israel.
\fn{the psaltery: Heb. the instrument of psaltery.}
\vs Psa 71:23 My lips shall greatly rejoice when I sing unto thee; and my soul, which thou hast redeemed.
\vs Psa 71:24 My tongue also shall talk of thy righteousness all the day long: for they are confounded, for they are brought unto shame, that seek my hurt.
\vs Psa 72:1 \bibemph{A Psalm} for Solomon. Give the king thy judgments, O God, and thy righteousness unto the king's son.
\fn{for: or, of.}
\vs Psa 72:2 He shall judge thy people with righteousness, and thy poor with judgment.
\vs Psa 72:3 The mountains shall bring peace to the people, and the little hills, by righteousness.
\vs Psa 72:4 He shall judge the poor of the people, he shall save the children of the needy, and shall break in pieces the oppressor.
\vs Psa 72:5 They shall fear thee as long as the sun and moon endure, throughout all generations.
\vs Psa 72:6 He shall come down like rain upon the mown grass: as showers \bibemph{that} water the earth.
\vs Psa 72:7 In his days shall the righteous flourish; and abundance of peace so long as the moon endureth.
\fn{so long...: Heb. till there be no moon.}
\vs Psa 72:8 He shall have dominion also from sea to sea, and from the river unto the ends of the earth.
\vs Psa 72:9 They that dwell in the wilderness shall bow before him; and his enemies shall lick the dust.
\vs Psa 72:10 The kings of Tarshish and of the isles shall bring presents: the kings of Sheba and Seba shall offer gifts.
\vs Psa 72:11 Yea, all kings shall fall down before him: all nations shall serve him.
\vs Psa 72:12 For he shall deliver the needy when he crieth; the poor also, and \bibemph{him} that hath no helper.
\vs Psa 72:13 He shall spare the poor and needy, and shall save the souls of the needy.
\vs Psa 72:14 He shall redeem their soul from deceit and violence: and precious shall their blood be in his sight.
\vs Psa 72:15 And he shall live, and to him shall be given of the gold of Sheba: prayer also shall be made for him continually; \bibemph{and} daily shall he be praised.
\fn{shall be given: Heb. one shall give.}
\vs Psa 72:16 There shall be an handful of corn in the earth upon the top of the mountains; the fruit thereof shall shake like Lebanon: and \bibemph{they} of the city shall flourish like grass of the earth.
\vs Psa 72:17 His name shall endure for ever: his name shall be continued as long as the sun: and \bibemph{men} shall be blessed in him: all nations shall call him blessed.
\fn{endure: Heb. be. his name shall be...: Heb. shall be as a son to continue his father's name for ever.}
\vs Psa 72:18 Blessed \bibemph{be} the \textsc{Lord} God, the God of Israel, who only doeth wondrous things.
\vs Psa 72:19 And blessed \bibemph{be} his glorious name for ever: and let the whole earth be filled \bibemph{with} his glory; Amen, and Amen.
\vs Psa 72:20 The prayers of David the son of Jesse are ended.
\vs Psa 73:1 A Psalm of Asaph. Truly God \bibemph{is} good to Israel, \bibemph{even} to such as are of a clean heart.
\fn{Truly: or, Yet. of...: Heb. clean of heart. of: or, for.}
\vs Psa 73:2 But as for me, my feet were almost gone; my steps had well nigh slipped.
\vs Psa 73:3 For I was envious at the foolish, \bibemph{when} I saw the prosperity of the wicked.
\vs Psa 73:4 For \bibemph{there are} no bands in their death: but their strength \bibemph{is} firm.
\fn{firm: Heb. fat.}
\vs Psa 73:5 They \bibemph{are} not in trouble \bibemph{as other} men; neither are they plagued like \bibemph{other} men.
\fn{in...: Heb. in the trouble of other men. like: Heb. with.}
\vs Psa 73:6 Therefore pride compasseth them about as a chain; violence covereth them \bibemph{as} a garment.
\vs Psa 73:7 Their eyes stand out with fatness: they have more than heart could wish.
\fn{have...: Heb. pass the thoughts of the heart.}
\vs Psa 73:8 They are corrupt, and speak wickedly \bibemph{concerning} oppression: they speak loftily.
\vs Psa 73:9 They set their mouth against the heavens, and their tongue walketh through the earth.
\vs Psa 73:10 Therefore his people return hither: and waters of a full \bibemph{cup} are wrung out to them.
\vs Psa 73:11 And they say, How doth God know? and is there knowledge in the most High?
\vs Psa 73:12 Behold, these \bibemph{are} the ungodly, who prosper in the world; they increase \bibemph{in} riches.
\vs Psa 73:13 Verily I have cleansed my heart \bibemph{in} vain, and washed my hands in innocency.
\vs Psa 73:14 For all the day long have I been plagued, and chastened every morning.
\fn{chastened: Heb. my chastisement was.}
\vs Psa 73:15 If I say, I will speak thus; behold, I should offend \bibemph{against} the generation of thy children.
\vs Psa 73:16 When I thought to know this, it \bibemph{was} too painful for me;
\fn{too...: Heb. labour in mine eyes.}
\vs Psa 73:17 Until I went into the sanctuary of God; \bibemph{then} understood I their end.
\vs Psa 73:18 Surely thou didst set them in slippery places: thou castedst them down into destruction.
\vs Psa 73:19 How are they \bibemph{brought} into desolation, as in a moment! they are utterly consumed with terrors.
\vs Psa 73:20 As a dream when \bibemph{one} awaketh; \bibemph{so}, O Lord, when thou awakest, thou shalt despise their image.
\vs Psa 73:21 Thus my heart was grieved, and I was pricked in my reins.
\vs Psa 73:22 So foolish \bibemph{was} I, and ignorant: I was \bibemph{as} a beast before thee.
\fn{ignorant: Heb. I knew not. before Heb. with.}
\vs Psa 73:23 Nevertheless I \bibemph{am} continually with thee: thou hast holden \bibemph{me} by my right hand.
\vs Psa 73:24 Thou shalt guide me with thy counsel, and afterward receive me \bibemph{to} glory.
\vs Psa 73:25 Whom have I in heaven \bibemph{but thee}? and \bibemph{there is} none upon earth \bibemph{that} I desire beside thee.
\vs Psa 73:26 My flesh and my heart faileth: \bibemph{but} God \bibemph{is} the strength of my heart, and my portion for ever.
\fn{strength: Heb. rock.}
\vs Psa 73:27 For, lo, they that are far from thee shall perish: thou hast destroyed all them that go a whoring from thee.
\vs Psa 73:28 But \bibemph{it is} good for me to draw near to God: I have put my trust in the Lord GOD, that I may declare all thy works.
\vs Psa 74:1 Maschil of Asaph. O God, why hast thou cast \bibemph{us} off for ever? \bibemph{why} doth thine anger smoke against the sheep of thy pasture?
\fn{Maschil...: or, A Psalm for Asaph to give instruction.}
\vs Psa 74:2 Remember thy congregation, \bibemph{which} thou hast purchased of old; the rod of thine inheritance, \bibemph{which} thou hast redeemed; this mount Zion, wherein thou hast dwelt.
\fn{rod: or, tribe.}
\vs Psa 74:3 Lift up thy feet unto the perpetual desolations; \bibemph{even} all \bibemph{that} the enemy hath done wickedly in the sanctuary.
\vs Psa 74:4 Thine enemies roar in the midst of thy congregations; they set up their ensigns \bibemph{for} signs.
\vs Psa 74:5 \bibemph{A man} was famous according as he had lifted up axes upon the thick trees.
\vs Psa 74:6 But now they break down the carved work thereof at once with axes and hammers.
\vs Psa 74:7 They have cast fire into thy sanctuary, they have defiled \bibemph{by casting down} the dwelling place of thy name to the ground.
\fn{They have cast...: Heb. They have sent thy sanctuary unto the fire.}
\vs Psa 74:8 They said in their hearts, Let us destroy them together: they have burned up all the synagogues of God in the land.
\fn{destroy: Heb. break.}
\vs Psa 74:9 We see not our signs: \bibemph{there is} no more any prophet: neither \bibemph{is there} among us any that knoweth how long.
\vs Psa 74:10 O God, how long shall the adversary reproach? shall the enemy blaspheme thy name for ever?
\vs Psa 74:11 Why withdrawest thou thy hand, even thy right hand? pluck \bibemph{it} out of thy bosom.
\vs Psa 74:12 For God \bibemph{is} my King of old, working salvation in the midst of the earth.
\vs Psa 74:13 Thou didst divide the sea by thy strength: thou brakest the heads of the dragons in the waters.
\fn{divide: Heb. break. dragons: or, whales.}
\vs Psa 74:14 Thou brakest the heads of leviathan in pieces, \bibemph{and} gavest him \bibemph{to be} meat to the people inhabiting the wilderness.
\vs Psa 74:15 Thou didst cleave the fountain and the flood: thou driedst up mighty rivers.
\fn{mighty...: Heb. rivers of strength.}
\vs Psa 74:16 The day \bibemph{is} thine, the night also \bibemph{is} thine: thou hast prepared the light and the sun.
\vs Psa 74:17 Thou hast set all the borders of the earth: thou hast made summer and winter.
\fn{made: Heb. made them.}
\vs Psa 74:18 Remember this, \bibemph{that} the enemy hath reproached, O \textsc{Lord}, and \bibemph{that} the foolish people have blasphemed thy name.
\vs Psa 74:19 O deliver not the soul of thy turtledove unto the multitude \bibemph{of the wicked}: forget not the congregation of thy poor for ever.
\vs Psa 74:20 Have respect unto the covenant: for the dark places of the earth are full of the habitations of cruelty.
\vs Psa 74:21 O let not the oppressed return ashamed: let the poor and needy praise thy name.
\vs Psa 74:22 Arise, O God, plead thine own cause: remember how the foolish man reproacheth thee daily.
\vs Psa 74:23 Forget not the voice of thine enemies: the tumult of those that rise up against thee increaseth continually.
\fn{increaseth: Heb. ascendeth.}
\vs Psa 75:1 To the chief Musician, Altaschith, A Psalm \bibemph{or} Song of Asaph. Unto thee, O God, do we give thanks, \bibemph{unto thee} do we give thanks: for \bibemph{that} thy name is near thy wondrous works declare.
\fn{Altaschith: or, Destroy not. of: or, for.}
\vs Psa 75:2 When I shall receive the congregation I will judge uprightly.
\fn{receive...: or, take a set time.}
\vs Psa 75:3 The earth and all the inhabitants thereof are dissolved: I bear up the pillars of it. Selah.
\vs Psa 75:4 I said unto the fools, Deal not foolishly: and to the wicked, Lift not up the horn:
\vs Psa 75:5 Lift not up your horn on high: speak \bibemph{not with} a stiff neck.
\vs Psa 75:6 For promotion \bibemph{cometh} neither from the east, nor from the west, nor from the south.
\fn{south: Heb. desert.}
\vs Psa 75:7 But God \bibemph{is} the judge: he putteth down one, and setteth up another.
\vs Psa 75:8 For in the hand of the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{there is} a cup, and the wine is red; it is full of mixture; and he poureth out of the same: but the dregs thereof, all the wicked of the earth shall wring \bibemph{them} out, \bibemph{and} drink \bibemph{them}.
\vs Psa 75:9 But I will declare for ever; I will sing praises to the God of Jacob.
\vs Psa 75:10 All the horns of the wicked also will I cut off; \bibemph{but} the horns of the righteous shall be exalted.
\vs Psa 76:1 To the chief Musician on Neginoth, A Psalm \bibemph{or} Song of Asaph. In Judah \bibemph{is} God known: his name \bibemph{is} great in Israel.
\fn{of: or, for.}
\vs Psa 76:2 In Salem also is his tabernacle, and his dwelling place in Zion.
\vs Psa 76:3 There brake he the arrows of the bow, the shield, and the sword, and the battle. Selah.
\vs Psa 76:4 Thou \bibemph{art} more glorious \bibemph{and} excellent than the mountains of prey.
\vs Psa 76:5 The stouthearted are spoiled, they have slept their sleep: and none of the men of might have found their hands.
\vs Psa 76:6 At thy rebuke, O God of Jacob, both the chariot and horse are cast into a dead sleep.
\vs Psa 76:7 Thou, \bibemph{even} thou, \bibemph{art} to be feared: and who may stand in thy sight when once thou art angry?
\vs Psa 76:8 Thou didst cause judgment to be heard from heaven; the earth feared, and was still,
\vs Psa 76:9 When God arose to judgment, to save all the meek of the earth. Selah.
\vs Psa 76:10 Surely the wrath of man shall praise thee: the remainder of wrath shalt thou restrain.
\vs Psa 76:11 Vow, and pay unto the \textsc{Lord} your God: let all that be round about him bring presents unto him that ought to be feared.
\fn{unto him...: Heb. to fear.}
\vs Psa 76:12 He shall cut off the spirit of princes: \bibemph{he is} terrible to the kings of the earth.
\vs Psa 77:1 To the chief Musician, to Jeduthun, A Psalm of Asaph. I cried unto God with my voice, \bibemph{even} unto God with my voice; and he gave ear unto me.
\fn{of: or, for.}
\vs Psa 77:2 In the day of my trouble I sought the Lord: my sore ran in the night, and ceased not: my soul refused to be comforted.
\fn{sore: Heb. hand.}
\vs Psa 77:3 I remembered God, and was troubled: I complained, and my spirit was overwhelmed. Selah.
\vs Psa 77:4 Thou holdest mine eyes waking: I am so troubled that I cannot speak.
\vs Psa 77:5 I have considered the days of old, the years of ancient times.
\vs Psa 77:6 I call to remembrance my song in the night: I commune with mine own heart: and my spirit made diligent search.
\vs Psa 77:7 Will the Lord cast off for ever? and will he be favourable no more?
\vs Psa 77:8 Is his mercy clean gone for ever? doth \bibemph{his} promise fail for evermore?
\fn{for evermore: Heb. to generation and generation?.}
\vs Psa 77:9 Hath God forgotten to be gracious? hath he in anger shut up his tender mercies? Selah.
\vs Psa 77:10 And I said, This \bibemph{is} my infirmity: \bibemph{but I will remember} the years of the right hand of the most High.
\vs Psa 77:11 I will remember the works of the \textsc{Lord}: surely I will remember thy wonders of old.
\vs Psa 77:12 I will meditate also of all thy work, and talk of thy doings.
\vs Psa 77:13 Thy way, O God, \bibemph{is} in the sanctuary: who \bibemph{is so} great a God as \bibemph{our} God?
\vs Psa 77:14 Thou \bibemph{art} the God that doest wonders: thou hast declared thy strength among the people.
\vs Psa 77:15 Thou hast with \bibemph{thine} arm redeemed thy people, the sons of Jacob and Joseph. Selah.
\vs Psa 77:16 The waters saw thee, O God, the waters saw thee; they were afraid: the depths also were troubled.
\vs Psa 77:17 The clouds poured out water: the skies sent out a sound: thine arrows also went abroad.
\fn{poured...: Heb. were poured forth with water.}
\vs Psa 77:18 The voice of thy thunder \bibemph{was} in the heaven: the lightnings lightened the world: the earth trembled and shook.
\vs Psa 77:19 Thy way \bibemph{is} in the sea, and thy path in the great waters, and thy footsteps are not known.
\vs Psa 77:20 Thou leddest thy people like a flock by the hand of Moses and Aaron.
\vs Psa 78:1 Maschil of Asaph. Give ear, O my people, \bibemph{to} my law: incline your ears to the words of my mouth.
\fn{Maschil...: or, A Psalm for Asaph to give instruction.}
\vs Psa 78:2 I will open my mouth in a parable: I will utter dark sayings of old:
\vs Psa 78:3 Which we have heard and known, and our fathers have told us.
\vs Psa 78:4 We will not hide \bibemph{them} from their children, shewing to the generation to come the praises of the \textsc{Lord}, and his strength, and his wonderful works that he hath done.
\vs Psa 78:5 For he established a testimony in Jacob, and appointed a law in Israel, which he commanded our fathers, that they should make them known to their children:
\vs Psa 78:6 That the generation to come might know \bibemph{them, even} the children \bibemph{which} should be born; \bibemph{who} should arise and declare \bibemph{them} to their children:
\vs Psa 78:7 That they might set their hope in God, and not forget the works of God, but keep his commandments:
\vs Psa 78:8 And might not be as their fathers, a stubborn and rebellious generation; a generation \bibemph{that} set not their heart aright, and whose spirit was not stedfast with God.
\fn{that...: Heb. that prepared not their heart.}
\vs Psa 78:9 The children of Ephraim, \bibemph{being} armed, \bibemph{and} carrying bows, turned back in the day of battle.
\fn{carrying: Heb. throwing forth.}
\vs Psa 78:10 They kept not the covenant of God, and refused to walk in his law;
\vs Psa 78:11 And forgat his works, and his wonders that he had shewed them.
\vs Psa 78:12 Marvellous things did he in the sight of their fathers, in the land of Egypt, \bibemph{in} the field of Zoan.
\vs Psa 78:13 He divided the sea, and caused them to pass through; and he made the waters to stand as an heap.
\vs Psa 78:14 In the daytime also he led them with a cloud, and all the night with a light of fire.
\vs Psa 78:15 He clave the rocks in the wilderness, and gave \bibemph{them} drink as \bibemph{out of} the great depths.
\vs Psa 78:16 He brought streams also out of the rock, and caused waters to run down like rivers.
\vs Psa 78:17 And they sinned yet more against him by provoking the most High in the wilderness.
\vs Psa 78:18 And they tempted God in their heart by asking meat for their lust.
\vs Psa 78:19 Yea, they spake against God; they said, Can God furnish a table in the wilderness?
\fn{furnish: Heb. order.}
\vs Psa 78:20 Behold, he smote the rock, that the waters gushed out, and the streams overflowed; can he give bread also? can he provide flesh for his people?
\vs Psa 78:21 Therefore the \textsc{Lord} heard \bibemph{this}, and was wroth: so a fire was kindled against Jacob, and anger also came up against Israel;
\vs Psa 78:22 Because they believed not in God, and trusted not in his salvation:
\vs Psa 78:23 Though he had commanded the clouds from above, and opened the doors of heaven,
\vs Psa 78:24 And had rained down manna upon them to eat, and had given them of the corn of heaven.
\vs Psa 78:25 Man did eat angels' food: he sent them meat to the full.
\fn{Man...: or, Every one did eat the bread of the mighty.}
\vs Psa 78:26 He caused an east wind to blow in the heaven: and by his power he brought in the south wind.
\fn{to blow: Heb. to go.}
\vs Psa 78:27 He rained flesh also upon them as dust, and feathered fowls like as the sand of the sea:
\fn{feathered...: Heb. fowl of wing.}
\vs Psa 78:28 And he let \bibemph{it} fall in the midst of their camp, round about their habitations.
\vs Psa 78:29 So they did eat, and were well filled: for he gave them their own desire;
\vs Psa 78:30 They were not estranged from their lust. But while their meat \bibemph{was} yet in their mouths,
\vs Psa 78:31 The wrath of God came upon them, and slew the fattest of them, and smote down the chosen \bibemph{men} of Israel.
\fn{smote...: Heb. made to bow. Chosen...: or, young men.}
\vs Psa 78:32 For all this they sinned still, and believed not for his wondrous works.
\vs Psa 78:33 Therefore their days did he consume in vanity, and their years in trouble.
\vs Psa 78:34 When he slew them, then they sought him: and they returned and enquired early after God.
\vs Psa 78:35 And they remembered that God \bibemph{was} their rock, and the high God their redeemer.
\vs Psa 78:36 Nevertheless they did flatter him with their mouth, and they lied unto him with their tongues.
\vs Psa 78:37 For their heart was not right with him, neither were they stedfast in his covenant.
\vs Psa 78:38 But he, \bibemph{being} full of compassion, forgave \bibemph{their} iniquity, and destroyed \bibemph{them} not: yea, many a time turned he his anger away, and did not stir up all his wrath.
\vs Psa 78:39 For he remembered that they \bibemph{were but} flesh; a wind that passeth away, and cometh not again.
\vs Psa 78:40 How oft did they provoke him in the wilderness, \bibemph{and} grieve him in the desert!
\fn{provoke: or, rebel against.}
\vs Psa 78:41 Yea, they turned back and tempted God, and limited the Holy One of Israel.
\vs Psa 78:42 They remembered not his hand, \bibemph{nor} the day when he delivered them from the enemy.
\fn{from...: or, from affliction.}
\vs Psa 78:43 How he had wrought his signs in Egypt, and his wonders in the field of Zoan:
\fn{wrought: Heb. set.}
\vs Psa 78:44 And had turned their rivers into blood; and their floods, that they could not drink.
\vs Psa 78:45 He sent divers sorts of flies among them, which devoured them; and frogs, which destroyed them.
\vs Psa 78:46 He gave also their increase unto the caterpiller, and their labour unto the locust.
\vs Psa 78:47 He destroyed their vines with hail, and their sycomore trees with frost.
\fn{destroyed: Heb. killed. frost: or, great hailstones.}
\vs Psa 78:48 He gave up their cattle also to the hail, and their flocks to hot thunderbolts.
\fn{gave...: Heb. shut up. hot...: or, lightnings.}
\vs Psa 78:49 He cast upon them the fierceness of his anger, wrath, and indignation, and trouble, by sending evil angels \bibemph{among them}.
\vs Psa 78:50 He made a way to his anger; he spared not their soul from death, but gave their life over to the pestilence;
\fn{He made...: Heb. He weighed a path. life...: or, beasts to the murrain.}
\vs Psa 78:51 And smote all the firstborn in Egypt; the chief of \bibemph{their} strength in the tabernacles of Ham:
\vs Psa 78:52 But made his own people to go forth like sheep, and guided them in the wilderness like a flock.
\vs Psa 78:53 And he led them on safely, so that they feared not: but the sea overwhelmed their enemies.
\fn{overwhelmed: Heb. covered.}
\vs Psa 78:54 And he brought them to the border of his sanctuary, \bibemph{even to} this mountain, \bibemph{which} his right hand had purchased.
\vs Psa 78:55 He cast out the heathen also before them, and divided them an inheritance by line, and made the tribes of Israel to dwell in their tents.
\vs Psa 78:56 Yet they tempted and provoked the most high God, and kept not his testimonies:
\vs Psa 78:57 But turned back, and dealt unfaithfully like their fathers: they were turned aside like a deceitful bow.
\vs Psa 78:58 For they provoked him to anger with their high places, and moved him to jealousy with their graven images.
\vs Psa 78:59 When God heard \bibemph{this}, he was wroth, and greatly abhorred Israel:
\vs Psa 78:60 So that he forsook the tabernacle of Shiloh, the tent \bibemph{which} he placed among men;
\vs Psa 78:61 And delivered his strength into captivity, and his glory into the enemy's hand.
\vs Psa 78:62 He gave his people over also unto the sword; and was wroth with his inheritance.
\vs Psa 78:63 The fire consumed their young men; and their maidens were not given to marriage.
\fn{given...: Heb. praised.}
\vs Psa 78:64 Their priests fell by the sword; and their widows made no lamentation.
\vs Psa 78:65 Then the Lord awaked as one out of sleep, \bibemph{and} like a mighty man that shouteth by reason of wine.
\vs Psa 78:66 And he smote his enemies in the hinder parts: he put them to a perpetual reproach.
\vs Psa 78:67 Moreover he refused the tabernacle of Joseph, and chose not the tribe of Ephraim:
\vs Psa 78:68 But chose the tribe of Judah, the mount Zion which he loved.
\vs Psa 78:69 And he built his sanctuary like high \bibemph{palaces}, like the earth which he hath established for ever.
\fn{established: Heb. founded.}
\vs Psa 78:70 He chose David also his servant, and took him from the sheepfolds:
\vs Psa 78:71 From following the ewes great with young he brought him to feed Jacob his people, and Israel his inheritance.
\fn{following: Heb. after.}
\vs Psa 78:72 So he fed them according to the integrity of his heart; and guided them by the skilfulness of his hands.
\vs Psa 79:1 A Psalm of Asaph. O God, the heathen are come into thine inheritance; thy holy temple have they defiled; they have laid Jerusalem on heaps.
\fn{of: or, for.}
\vs Psa 79:2 The dead bodies of thy servants have they given \bibemph{to be} meat unto the fowls of the heaven, the flesh of thy saints unto the beasts of the earth.
\vs Psa 79:3 Their blood have they shed like water round about Jerusalem; and \bibemph{there was} none to bury \bibemph{them}.
\vs Psa 79:4 We are become a reproach to our neighbours, a scorn and derision to them that are round about us.
\vs Psa 79:5 How long, \textsc{Lord}? wilt thou be angry for ever? shall thy jealousy burn like fire?
\vs Psa 79:6 Pour out thy wrath upon the heathen that have not known thee, and upon the kingdoms that have not called upon thy name.
\vs Psa 79:7 For they have devoured Jacob, and laid waste his dwelling place.
\vs Psa 79:8 O remember not against us former iniquities: let thy tender mercies speedily prevent us: for we are brought very low.
\fn{former...: or, the iniquities of them that were before us.}
\vs Psa 79:9 Help us, O God of our salvation, for the glory of thy name: and deliver us, and purge away our sins, for thy name's sake.
\vs Psa 79:10 Wherefore should the heathen say, Where \bibemph{is} their God? let him be known among the heathen in our sight \bibemph{by} the revenging of the blood of thy servants \bibemph{which is} shed.
\fn{revenging: Heb. vengeance.}
\vs Psa 79:11 Let the sighing of the prisoner come before thee; according to the greatness of thy power preserve thou those that are appointed to die;
\fn{thy...: Heb. thine arm. preserve...: Heb. reserve the children of death.}
\vs Psa 79:12 And render unto our neighbours sevenfold into their bosom their reproach, wherewith they have reproached thee, O Lord.
\vs Psa 79:13 So we thy people and sheep of thy pasture will give thee thanks for ever: we will shew forth thy praise to all generations.
\fn{to all...: Heb. to generation and generation.}
\vs Psa 80:1 To the chief Musician upon Shoshannimeduth, A Psalm of Asaph. Give ear, O Shepherd of Israel, thou that leadest Joseph like a flock; thou that dwellest \bibemph{between} the cherubims, shine forth.
\fn{of: or, for.}
\vs Psa 80:2 Before Ephraim and Benjamin and Manasseh stir up thy strength, and come \bibemph{and} save us.
\fn{come...: Heb. come for salvation to us.}
\vs Psa 80:3 Turn us again, O God, and cause thy face to shine; and we shall be saved.
\vs Psa 80:4 O \textsc{Lord} God of hosts, how long wilt thou be angry against the prayer of thy people?
\fn{be...: Heb. smoke.}
\vs Psa 80:5 Thou feedest them with the bread of tears; and givest them tears to drink in great measure.
\vs Psa 80:6 Thou makest us a strife unto our neighbours: and our enemies laugh among themselves.
\vs Psa 80:7 Turn us again, O God of hosts, and cause thy face to shine; and we shall be saved.
\vs Psa 80:8 Thou hast brought a vine out of Egypt: thou hast cast out the heathen, and planted it.
\vs Psa 80:9 Thou preparedst \bibemph{room} before it, and didst cause it to take deep root, and it filled the land.
\vs Psa 80:10 The hills were covered with the shadow of it, and the boughs thereof \bibemph{were like} the goodly cedars.
\fn{goodly...: Heb. cedars of God.}
\vs Psa 80:11 She sent out her boughs unto the sea, and her branches unto the river.
\vs Psa 80:12 Why hast thou \bibemph{then} broken down her hedges, so that all they which pass by the way do pluck her?
\vs Psa 80:13 The boar out of the wood doth waste it, and the wild beast of the field doth devour it.
\vs Psa 80:14 Return, we beseech thee, O God of hosts: look down from heaven, and behold, and visit this vine;
\vs Psa 80:15 And the vineyard which thy right hand hath planted, and the branch \bibemph{that} thou madest strong for thyself.
\vs Psa 80:16 \bibemph{It is} burned with fire, \bibemph{it is} cut down: they perish at the rebuke of thy countenance.
\vs Psa 80:17 Let thy hand be upon the man of thy right hand, upon the son of man \bibemph{whom} thou madest strong for thyself.
\vs Psa 80:18 So will not we go back from thee: quicken us, and we will call upon thy name.
\vs Psa 80:19 Turn us again, O \textsc{Lord} God of hosts, cause thy face to shine; and we shall be saved.
\vs Psa 81:1 To the chief Musician upon Gittith, \bibemph{A Psalm} of Asaph. Sing aloud unto God our strength: make a joyful noise unto the God of Jacob.
\fn{of Asaph: or, for Asaph.}
\vs Psa 81:2 Take a psalm, and bring hither the timbrel, the pleasant harp with the psaltery.
\vs Psa 81:3 Blow up the trumpet in the new moon, in the time appointed, on our solemn feast day.
\vs Psa 81:4 For this \bibemph{was} a statute for Israel, \bibemph{and} a law of the God of Jacob.
\vs Psa 81:5 This he ordained in Joseph \bibemph{for} a testimony, when he went out through the land of Egypt: \bibemph{where} I heard a language \bibemph{that} I understood not.
\fn{through: or, against.}
\vs Psa 81:6 I removed his shoulder from the burden: his hands were delivered from the pots.
\fn{were...: Heb. passed away.}
\vs Psa 81:7 Thou calledst in trouble, and I delivered thee; I answered thee in the secret place of thunder: I proved thee at the waters of Meribah. Selah.
\fn{Meribah: or, Strife.}
\vs Psa 81:8 Hear, O my people, and I will testify unto thee: O Israel, if thou wilt hearken unto me;
\vs Psa 81:9 There shall no strange god be in thee; neither shalt thou worship any strange god.
\vs Psa 81:10 I \bibemph{am} the \textsc{Lord} thy God, which brought thee out of the land of Egypt: open thy mouth wide, and I will fill it.
\vs Psa 81:11 But my people would not hearken to my voice; and Israel would none of me.
\vs Psa 81:12 So I gave them up unto their own hearts' lust: \bibemph{and} they walked in their own counsels.
\fn{unto...: or, to the hardness of their hearts, or, imagination.}
\vs Psa 81:13 Oh that my people had hearkened unto me, \bibemph{and} Israel had walked in my ways!
\vs Psa 81:14 I should soon have subdued their enemies, and turned my hand against their adversaries.
\vs Psa 81:15 The haters of the \textsc{Lord} should have submitted themselves unto him: but their time should have endured for ever.
\fn{submitted...: or, yielded feigned obedience: Heb. lied.}
\vs Psa 81:16 He should have fed them also with the finest of the wheat: and with honey out of the rock should I have satisfied thee.
\fn{finest...: Heb. fat of wheat.}
\vs Psa 82:1 A Psalm of Asaph. God standeth in the congregation of the mighty; he judgeth among the gods.
\fn{of Asaph: or, for Asaph.}
\vs Psa 82:2 How long will ye judge unjustly, and accept the persons of the wicked? Selah.
\vs Psa 82:3 Defend the poor and fatherless: do justice to the afflicted and needy.
\fn{Defend: Heb. Judge.}
\vs Psa 82:4 Deliver the poor and needy: rid \bibemph{them} out of the hand of the wicked.
\vs Psa 82:5 They know not, neither will they understand; they walk on in darkness: all the foundations of the earth are out of course.
\fn{out...: Heb. moved.}
\vs Psa 82:6 I have said, Ye \bibemph{are} gods; and all of you \bibemph{are} children of the most High.
\vs Psa 82:7 But ye shall die like men, and fall like one of the princes.
\vs Psa 82:8 Arise, O God, judge the earth: for thou shalt inherit all nations.
\vs Psa 83:1 A Song \bibemph{or} Psalm of Asaph. Keep not thou silence, O God: hold not thy peace, and be not still, O God.
\fn{of Asaph: or, for Asaph.}
\vs Psa 83:2 For, lo, thine enemies make a tumult: and they that hate thee have lifted up the head.
\vs Psa 83:3 They have taken crafty counsel against thy people, and consulted against thy hidden ones.
\vs Psa 83:4 They have said, Come, and let us cut them off from \bibemph{being} a nation; that the name of Israel may be no more in remembrance.
\vs Psa 83:5 For they have consulted together with one consent: they are confederate against thee:
\fn{consent: Heb. heart.}
\vs Psa 83:6 The tabernacles of Edom, and the Ishmaelites; of Moab, and the Hagarenes;
\vs Psa 83:7 Gebal, and Ammon, and Amalek; the Philistines with the inhabitants of Tyre;
\vs Psa 83:8 Assur also is joined with them: they have holpen the children of Lot. Selah.
\fn{holpen: Heb. been an arm to.}
\vs Psa 83:9 Do unto them as \bibemph{unto} the Midianites; as \bibemph{to} Sisera, as \bibemph{to} Jabin, at the brook of Kison:
\vs Psa 83:10 \bibemph{Which} perished at Endor: they became \bibemph{as} dung for the earth.
\vs Psa 83:11 Make their nobles like Oreb, and like Zeeb: yea, all their princes as Zebah, and as Zalmunna:
\vs Psa 83:12 Who said, Let us take to ourselves the houses of God in possession.
\vs Psa 83:13 O my God, make them like a wheel; as the stubble before the wind.
\vs Psa 83:14 As the fire burneth a wood, and as the flame setteth the mountains on fire;
\vs Psa 83:15 So persecute them with thy tempest, and make them afraid with thy storm.
\vs Psa 83:16 Fill their faces with shame; that they may seek thy name, O \textsc{Lord}.
\vs Psa 83:17 Let them be confounded and troubled for ever; yea, let them be put to shame, and perish:
\vs Psa 83:18 That \bibemph{men} may know that thou, whose name alone \bibemph{is} JEHOVAH, \bibemph{art} the most high over all the earth.
\vs Psa 84:1 To the chief Musician upon Gittith, A Psalm for the sons of Korah. How amiable \bibemph{are} thy tabernacles, O \textsc{Lord} of hosts!
\fn{for the sons: or, of the sons.}
\vs Psa 84:2 My soul longeth, yea, even fainteth for the courts of the \textsc{Lord}: my heart and my flesh crieth out for the living God.
\vs Psa 84:3 Yea, the sparrow hath found an house, and the swallow a nest for herself, where she may lay her young, \bibemph{even} thine altars, O \textsc{Lord} of hosts, my King, and my God.
\vs Psa 84:4 Blessed \bibemph{are} they that dwell in thy house: they will be still praising thee. Selah.
\vs Psa 84:5 Blessed \bibemph{is} the man whose strength \bibemph{is} in thee; in whose heart \bibemph{are} the ways \bibemph{of them}.
\vs Psa 84:6 \bibemph{Who} passing through the valley of Baca make it a well; the rain also filleth the pools.
\fn{Baca...: or, mulberry trees make him a well, etc. filleth: Heb. covereth.}
\vs Psa 84:7 They go from strength to strength, \bibemph{every one of them} in Zion appeareth before God.
\fn{strength to...: or, company to company.}
\vs Psa 84:8 O \textsc{Lord} God of hosts, hear my prayer: give ear, O God of Jacob. Selah.
\vs Psa 84:9 Behold, O God our shield, and look upon the face of thine anointed.
\vs Psa 84:10 For a day in thy courts \bibemph{is} better than a thousand. I had rather be a doorkeeper in the house of my God, than to dwell in the tents of wickedness.
\fn{I had...: Heb. I would choose rather to sit at the threshold.}
\vs Psa 84:11 For the \textsc{Lord} God \bibemph{is} a sun and shield: the \textsc{Lord} will give grace and glory: no good \bibemph{thing} will he withhold from them that walk uprightly.
\vs Psa 84:12 O \textsc{Lord} of hosts, blessed \bibemph{is} the man that trusteth in thee.
\vs Psa 85:1 To the chief Musician, A Psalm for the sons of Korah. \textsc{Lord}, thou hast been favourable unto thy land: thou hast brought back the captivity of Jacob.
\fn{for the sons: or, of the sons. favourable: or, well pleased.}
\vs Psa 85:2 Thou hast forgiven the iniquity of thy people, thou hast covered all their sin. Selah.
\vs Psa 85:3 Thou hast taken away all thy wrath: thou hast turned \bibemph{thyself} from the fierceness of thine anger.
\fn{thyself...: or, thine anger from waxing hot.}
\vs Psa 85:4 Turn us, O God of our salvation, and cause thine anger toward us to cease.
\vs Psa 85:5 Wilt thou be angry with us for ever? wilt thou draw out thine anger to all generations?
\vs Psa 85:6 Wilt thou not revive us again: that thy people may rejoice in thee?
\vs Psa 85:7 Shew us thy mercy, O \textsc{Lord}, and grant us thy salvation.
\vs Psa 85:8 I will hear what God the \textsc{Lord} will speak: for he will speak peace unto his people, and to his saints: but let them not turn again to folly.
\vs Psa 85:9 Surely his salvation \bibemph{is} nigh them that fear him; that glory may dwell in our land.
\vs Psa 85:10 Mercy and truth are met together; righteousness and peace have kissed \bibemph{each other}.
\vs Psa 85:11 Truth shall spring out of the earth; and righteousness shall look down from heaven.
\vs Psa 85:12 Yea, the \textsc{Lord} shall give \bibemph{that which is} good; and our land shall yield her increase.
\vs Psa 85:13 Righteousness shall go before him; and shall set \bibemph{us} in the way of his steps.
\vs Psa 86:1 A Prayer of David. Bow down thine ear, O \textsc{Lord}, hear me: for I \bibemph{am} poor and needy.
\fn{A Prayer...: or, A Prayer, being a psalm of David.}
\vs Psa 86:2 Preserve my soul; for I \bibemph{am} holy: O thou my God, save thy servant that trusteth in thee.
\fn{holy: or, one whom thou favourest.}
\vs Psa 86:3 Be merciful unto me, O Lord: for I cry unto thee daily.
\fn{daily: or, all the day.}
\vs Psa 86:4 Rejoice the soul of thy servant: for unto thee, O Lord, do I lift up my soul.
\vs Psa 86:5 For thou, Lord, \bibemph{art} good, and ready to forgive; and plenteous in mercy unto all them that call upon thee.
\vs Psa 86:6 Give ear, O \textsc{Lord}, unto my prayer; and attend to the voice of my supplications.
\vs Psa 86:7 In the day of my trouble I will call upon thee: for thou wilt answer me.
\vs Psa 86:8 Among the gods \bibemph{there is} none like unto thee, O Lord; neither \bibemph{are there any works} like unto thy works.
\vs Psa 86:9 All nations whom thou hast made shall come and worship before thee, O Lord; and shall glorify thy name.
\vs Psa 86:10 For thou \bibemph{art} great, and doest wondrous things: thou \bibemph{art} God alone.
\vs Psa 86:11 Teach me thy way, O \textsc{Lord}; I will walk in thy truth: unite my heart to fear thy name.
\vs Psa 86:12 I will praise thee, O Lord my God, with all my heart: and I will glorify thy name for evermore.
\vs Psa 86:13 For great \bibemph{is} thy mercy toward me: and thou hast delivered my soul from the lowest hell.
\fn{hell: or, grave.}
\vs Psa 86:14 O God, the proud are risen against me, and the assemblies of violent \bibemph{men} have sought after my soul; and have not set thee before them.
\fn{violent: Heb. terrible.}
\vs Psa 86:15 But thou, O Lord, \bibemph{art} a God full of compassion, and gracious, longsuffering, and plenteous in mercy and truth.
\vs Psa 86:16 O turn unto me, and have mercy upon me; give thy strength unto thy servant, and save the son of thine handmaid.
\vs Psa 86:17 Shew me a token for good; that they which hate me may see \bibemph{it}, and be ashamed: because thou, \textsc{Lord}, hast holpen me, and comforted me.

\vs Psa 88:1 A Song \bibemph{or} Psalm for the sons of Korah, to the chief Musician upon Mahalath Leannoth, Maschil of Heman the Ezrahite. O \textsc{Lord} God of my salvation, I have cried day \bibemph{and} night before thee:
\fn{for the sons: or, of the sons. Maschil...: or, A Psalm of Heman the Ezrahite, giving instruction.}
\vs Psa 88:2 Let my prayer come before thee: incline thine ear unto my cry;
\vs Psa 88:3 For my soul is full of troubles: and my life draweth nigh unto the grave.
\vs Psa 88:4 I am counted with them that go down into the pit: I am as a man \bibemph{that hath} no strength:
\vs Psa 88:5 Free among the dead, like the slain that lie in the grave, whom thou rememberest no more: and they are cut off from thy hand.
\fn{from: or, by.}
\vs Psa 88:6 Thou hast laid me in the lowest pit, in darkness, in the deeps.
\vs Psa 88:7 Thy wrath lieth hard upon me, and thou hast afflicted \bibemph{me} with all thy waves. Selah.
\vs Psa 88:8 Thou hast put away mine acquaintance far from me; thou hast made me an abomination unto them: \bibemph{I am} shut up, and I cannot come forth.
\vs Psa 88:9 Mine eye mourneth by reason of affliction: \textsc{Lord}, I have called daily upon thee, I have stretched out my hands unto thee.
\vs Psa 88:10 Wilt thou shew wonders to the dead? shall the dead arise \bibemph{and} praise thee? Selah.
\vs Psa 88:11 Shall thy lovingkindness be declared in the grave? \bibemph{or} thy faithfulness in destruction?
\vs Psa 88:12 Shall thy wonders be known in the dark? and thy righteousness in the land of forgetfulness?
\vs Psa 88:13 But unto thee have I cried, O \textsc{Lord}; and in the morning shall my prayer prevent thee.
\vs Psa 88:14 \textsc{Lord}, why castest thou off my soul? \bibemph{why} hidest thou thy face from me?
\vs Psa 88:15 I \bibemph{am} afflicted and ready to die from \bibemph{my} youth up: \bibemph{while} I suffer thy terrors I am distracted.
\vs Psa 88:16 Thy fierce wrath goeth over me; thy terrors have cut me off.
\vs Psa 88:17 They came round about me daily like water; they compassed me about together.
\fn{daily: or, all the day.}
\vs Psa 88:18 Lover and friend hast thou put far from me, \bibemph{and} mine acquaintance into darkness.
\vs Psa 89:1 Maschil of Ethan the Ezrahite. I will sing of the mercies of the \textsc{Lord} for ever: with my mouth will I make known thy faithfulness to all generations.

\vs Psa 89:2 For I have said, Mercy shall be built up for ever: thy faithfulness shalt thou establish in the very heavens.
\vs Psa 89:3 I have made a covenant with my chosen, I have sworn unto David my servant,
\vs Psa 89:4 Thy seed will I establish for ever, and build up thy throne to all generations. Selah.
\vs Psa 89:5 And the heavens shall praise thy wonders, O \textsc{Lord}: thy faithfulness also in the congregation of the saints.
\vs Psa 89:6 For who in the heaven can be compared unto the \textsc{Lord}? \bibemph{who} among the sons of the mighty can be likened unto the \textsc{Lord}?
\vs Psa 89:7 God is greatly to be feared in the assembly of the saints, and to be had in reverence of all \bibemph{them that are} about him.
\vs Psa 89:8 O \textsc{Lord} God of hosts, who \bibemph{is} a strong \textsc{Lord} like unto thee? or to thy faithfulness round about thee?
\vs Psa 89:9 Thou rulest the raging of the sea: when the waves thereof arise, thou stillest them.
\vs Psa 89:10 Thou hast broken Rahab in pieces, as one that is slain; thou hast scattered thine enemies with thy strong arm.
\fn{Rahab: or, Egypt. thy...: Heb. the arm of thy strength.}
\vs Psa 89:11 The heavens \bibemph{are} thine, the earth also \bibemph{is} thine: \bibemph{as for} the world and the fulness thereof, thou hast founded them.
\fn{the fulness...: or, all it containeth.}
\vs Psa 89:12 The north and the south thou hast created them: Tabor and Hermon shall rejoice in thy name.
\vs Psa 89:13 Thou hast a mighty arm: strong is thy hand, \bibemph{and} high is thy right hand.
\fn{a...: Heb. an arm with might.}
\vs Psa 89:14 Justice and judgment \bibemph{are} the habitation of thy throne: mercy and truth shall go before thy face.
\fn{habitation: or, establishment.}
\vs Psa 89:15 Blessed \bibemph{is} the people that know the joyful sound: they shall walk, O \textsc{Lord}, in the light of thy countenance.
\vs Psa 89:16 In thy name shall they rejoice all the day: and in thy righteousness shall they be exalted.
\vs Psa 89:17 For thou \bibemph{art} the glory of their strength: and in thy favour our horn shall be exalted.
\vs Psa 89:18 For the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} our defence; and the Holy One of Israel \bibemph{is} our king.
\fn{the \textsc{Lord}...: or, our shield is of the \textsc{Lord}, and our king is of the Holy One of Israel.}
\vs Psa 89:19 Then thou spakest in vision to thy holy one, and saidst, I have laid help upon \bibemph{one that is} mighty; I have exalted \bibemph{one} chosen out of the people.
\vs Psa 89:20 I have found David my servant; with my holy oil have I anointed him:
\vs Psa 89:21 With whom my hand shall be established: mine arm also shall strengthen him.
\vs Psa 89:22 The enemy shall not exact upon him; nor the son of wickedness afflict him.
\vs Psa 89:23 And I will beat down his foes before his face, and plague them that hate him.
\vs Psa 89:24 But my faithfulness and my mercy \bibemph{shall be} with him: and in my name shall his horn be exalted.
\vs Psa 89:25 I will set his hand also in the sea, and his right hand in the rivers.
\vs Psa 89:26 He shall cry unto me, Thou \bibemph{art} my father, my God, and the rock of my salvation.
\vs Psa 89:27 Also I will make him \bibemph{my} firstborn, higher than the kings of the earth.
\vs Psa 89:28 My mercy will I keep for him for evermore, and my covenant shall stand fast with him.
\vs Psa 89:29 His seed also will I make \bibemph{to endure} for ever, and his throne as the days of heaven.
\vs Psa 89:30 If his children forsake my law, and walk not in my judgments;
\vs Psa 89:31 If they break my statutes, and keep not my commandments;
\fn{break: Heb. profane.}
\vs Psa 89:32 Then will I visit their transgression with the rod, and their iniquity with stripes.
\vs Psa 89:33 Nevertheless my lovingkindness will I not utterly take from him, nor suffer my faithfulness to fail.
\fn{will...: Heb. I will not make void from him. to fall: Heb. to lie.}
\vs Psa 89:34 My covenant will I not break, nor alter the thing that is gone out of my lips.
\vs Psa 89:35 Once have I sworn by my holiness that I will not lie unto David.
\fn{that...: Heb. if I lie.}
\vs Psa 89:36 His seed shall endure for ever, and his throne as the sun before me.
\vs Psa 89:37 It shall be established for ever as the moon, and \bibemph{as} a faithful witness in heaven. Selah.
\vs Psa 89:38 But thou hast cast off and abhorred, thou hast been wroth with thine anointed.
\vs Psa 89:39 Thou hast made void the covenant of thy servant: thou hast profaned his crown \bibemph{by casting it} to the ground.
\vs Psa 89:40 Thou hast broken down all his hedges; thou hast brought his strong holds to ruin.
\vs Psa 89:41 All that pass by the way spoil him: he is a reproach to his neighbours.
\vs Psa 89:42 Thou hast set up the right hand of his adversaries; thou hast made all his enemies to rejoice.
\vs Psa 89:43 Thou hast also turned the edge of his sword, and hast not made him to stand in the battle.
\vs Psa 89:44 Thou hast made his glory to cease, and cast his throne down to the ground.
\fn{glory: Heb. brightness.}
\vs Psa 89:45 The days of his youth hast thou shortened: thou hast covered him with shame. Selah.
\vs Psa 89:46 How long, \textsc{Lord}? wilt thou hide thyself for ever? shall thy wrath burn like fire?
\vs Psa 89:47 Remember how short my time is: wherefore hast thou made all men in vain?
\vs Psa 89:48 What man \bibemph{is he that} liveth, and shall not see death? shall he deliver his soul from the hand of the grave? Selah.
\vs Psa 89:49 Lord, where \bibemph{are} thy former lovingkindnesses, \bibemph{which} thou swarest unto David in thy truth?
\vs Psa 89:50 Remember, Lord, the reproach of thy servants; \bibemph{how} I do bear in my bosom \bibemph{the reproach of} all the mighty people;
\vs Psa 89:51 Wherewith thine enemies have reproached, O \textsc{Lord}; wherewith they have reproached the footsteps of thine anointed.
\vs Psa 89:52 Blessed \bibemph{be} the \textsc{Lord} for evermore. Amen, and Amen.

\vs Psa 90:3 Thou turnest man to destruction; and sayest, Return, ye children of men.

\fn{when...: or, when he hath passed them.}

\fn{groweth...: or, is changed.}

\vs Psa 90:7 For we are consumed by thine anger, and by thy wrath are we troubled.
\vs Psa 90:8 Thou hast set our iniquities before thee, our secret \bibemph{sins} in the light of thy countenance.
\vs Psa 90:9 For all our days are passed away in thy wrath: we spend our years as a tale \bibemph{that is told}.
\fn{passed...: Heb. turned away. as a...: or, as a meditation.}
\vs Psa 90:10 The days of our years \bibemph{are} threescore years and ten; and if by reason of strength \bibemph{they be} fourscore years, yet \bibemph{is} their strength labour and sorrow; for it is soon cut off, and we fly away.
\fn{The days...: Heb. As for the days of our years, in them are seventy years.}
\vs Psa 90:11 Who knoweth the power of thine anger? even according to thy fear, \bibemph{so is} thy wrath.
\vs Psa 90:12 So teach \bibemph{us} to number our days, that we may apply \bibemph{our} hearts unto wisdom.
\fn{apply: Heb. cause to come.}
\vs Psa 90:13 Return, O \textsc{Lord}, how long? and let it repent thee concerning thy servants.
\vs Psa 90:14 O satisfy us early with thy mercy; that we may rejoice and be glad all our days.
\vs Psa 90:15 Make us glad according to the days \bibemph{wherein} thou hast afflicted us, \bibemph{and} the years \bibemph{wherein} we have seen evil.
\vs Psa 90:16 Let thy work appear unto thy servants, and thy glory unto their children.
\vs Psa 90:17 And let the beauty of the \textsc{Lord} our God be upon us: and establish thou the work of our hands upon us; yea, the work of our hands establish thou it.

\vs Psa 91:4 He shall cover thee with his feathers, and under his wings shalt thou trust: his truth \bibemph{shall be thy} shield and buckler.

\vs Psa 92:2 To shew forth thy lovingkindness in the morning, and thy faithfulness every night,
\fn{every...: Heb. in the nights.}
\vs Psa 92:3 Upon an instrument of ten strings, and upon the psaltery; upon the harp with a solemn sound.
\fn{the harp...: or, the solemn sound with the harp. a solemn...: Heb. Higgaion.}
\vs Psa 92:4 For thou, \textsc{Lord}, hast made me glad through thy work: I will triumph in the works of thy hands.
\vs Psa 92:5 O \textsc{Lord}, how great are thy works! \bibemph{and} thy thoughts are very deep.
\vs Psa 92:6 A brutish man knoweth not; neither doth a fool understand this.
\vs Psa 92:7 When the wicked spring as the grass, and when all the workers of iniquity do flourish; \bibemph{it is} that they shall be destroyed for ever:
\vs Psa 92:8 But thou, \textsc{Lord}, \bibemph{art most} high for evermore.
\vs Psa 92:9 For, lo, thine enemies, O \textsc{Lord}, for, lo, thine enemies shall perish; all the workers of iniquity shall be scattered.
\vs Psa 92:10 But my horn shalt thou exalt like \bibemph{the horn of} an unicorn: I shall be anointed with fresh oil.
\vs Psa 92:11 Mine eye also shall see \bibemph{my desire} on mine enemies, \bibemph{and} mine ears shall hear \bibemph{my desire} of the wicked that rise up against me.
\vs Psa 92:12 The righteous shall flourish like the palm tree: he shall grow like a cedar in Lebanon.
\vs Psa 92:13 Those that be planted in the house of the \textsc{Lord} shall flourish in the courts of our God.
\vs Psa 92:14 They shall still bring forth fruit in old age; they shall be fat and flourishing;
\fn{flourishing: Heb. green.}
\vs Psa 92:15 To shew that the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} upright: \bibemph{he is} my rock, and \bibemph{there is} no unrighteousness in him.

\vs Psa 94:1 O \textsc{Lord} God, to whom vengeance belongeth; O God, to whom vengeance belongeth, shew thyself.
\fn{God...: Heb. God of revenges. shew...: Heb. shine forth.}
\vs Psa 94:2 Lift up thyself, thou judge of the earth: render a reward to the proud.
\vs Psa 94:3 \textsc{Lord}, how long shall the wicked, how long shall the wicked triumph?
\vs Psa 94:4 \bibemph{How long} shall they utter \bibemph{and} speak hard things? \bibemph{and} all the workers of iniquity boast themselves?
\vs Psa 94:5 They break in pieces thy people, O \textsc{Lord}, and afflict thine heritage.
\vs Psa 94:6 They slay the widow and the stranger, and murder the fatherless.
\vs Psa 94:7 Yet they say, The \textsc{Lord} shall not see, neither shall the God of Jacob regard \bibemph{it}.
\vs Psa 94:8 Understand, ye brutish among the people: and \bibemph{ye} fools, when will ye be wise?
\vs Psa 94:9 He that planted the ear, shall he not hear? he that formed the eye, shall he not see?
\vs Psa 94:10 He that chastiseth the heathen, shall not he correct? he that teacheth man knowledge, \bibemph{shall not he know}?
\vs Psa 94:11 The \textsc{Lord} knoweth the thoughts of man, that they \bibemph{are} vanity.
\vs Psa 94:12 Blessed \bibemph{is} the man whom thou chastenest, O \textsc{Lord}, and teachest him out of thy law;
\vs Psa 94:13 That thou mayest give him rest from the days of adversity, until the pit be digged for the wicked.
\vs Psa 94:14 For the \textsc{Lord} will not cast off his people, neither will he forsake his inheritance.
\vs Psa 94:15 But judgment shall return unto righteousness: and all the upright in heart shall follow it.
\fn{shall follow...: Heb. shall be after it.}
\vs Psa 94:16 Who will rise up for me against the evildoers? \bibemph{or} who will stand up for me against the workers of iniquity?
\vs Psa 94:17 Unless the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{had been} my help, my soul had almost dwelt in silence.
\fn{almost: or, quickly.}
\vs Psa 94:18 When I said, My foot slippeth; thy mercy, O \textsc{Lord}, held me up.
\vs Psa 94:19 In the multitude of my thoughts within me thy comforts delight my soul.
\vs Psa 94:20 Shall the throne of iniquity have fellowship with thee, which frameth mischief by a law?
\vs Psa 94:21 They gather themselves together against the soul of the righteous, and condemn the innocent blood.
\vs Psa 94:22 But the \textsc{Lord} is my defence; and my God \bibemph{is} the rock of my refuge.
\vs Psa 94:23 And he shall bring upon them their own iniquity, and shall cut them off in their own wickedness; \bibemph{yea}, the \textsc{Lord} our God shall cut them off.
\vs Psa 95:1 O come, let us sing unto the \textsc{Lord}: let us make a joyful noise to the rock of our salvation.

\fn{come...: Heb. prevent his face.}
\vs Psa 95:3 For the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} a great God, and a great King above all gods.
\vs Psa 95:4 In his hand \bibemph{are} the deep places of the earth: the strength of the hills \bibemph{is} his also.
\fn{In...: Heb. In whose. the strength...: or, the heights of the hills are his.}
\vs Psa 95:5 The sea \bibemph{is} his, and he made it: and his hands formed the dry \bibemph{land}.
\fn{The sea...: Heb. Whose the sea is.}
\vs Psa 95:6 O come, let us worship and bow down: let us kneel before the \textsc{Lord} our maker.
\vs Psa 95:7 For he \bibemph{is} our God; and we \bibemph{are} the people of his pasture, and the sheep of his hand. To day if ye will hear his voice,
\vs Psa 95:8 Harden not your heart, as in the provocation, \bibemph{and} as \bibemph{in} the day of temptation in the wilderness:
\fn{provocation: Heb. contention.}
\vs Psa 95:9 When your fathers tempted me, proved me, and saw my work.

\vs Psa 95:11 Unto whom I sware in my wrath that they should not enter into my rest.

\vs Psa 96:1 O sing unto the \textsc{Lord} a new song: sing unto the \textsc{Lord}, all the earth.

\vs Psa 96:3 Declare his glory among the heathen, his wonders among all people.
\vs Psa 96:4 For the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} great, and greatly to be praised: he \bibemph{is} to be feared above all gods.
\vs Psa 96:5 For all the gods of the nations \bibemph{are} idols: but the \textsc{Lord} made the heavens.
\vs Psa 96:6 Honour and majesty \bibemph{are} before him: strength and beauty \bibemph{are} in his sanctuary.
\vs Psa 96:7 Give unto the \textsc{Lord}, O ye kindreds of the people, give unto the \textsc{Lord} glory and strength.
\vs Psa 96:8 Give unto the \textsc{Lord} the glory \bibemph{due unto} his name: bring an offering, and come into his courts.
\fn{due...: Heb. of his name.}
\vs Psa 96:9 O worship the \textsc{Lord} in the beauty of holiness: fear before him, all the earth.
\fn{in the...: or, in the glorious sanctuary.}
\vs Psa 96:10 Say among the heathen \bibemph{that} the \textsc{Lord} reigneth: the world also shall be established that it shall not be moved: he shall judge the people righteously.

\fn{the fulness...: or, all it containeth.}

\vs Psa 96:13 Before the \textsc{Lord}: for he cometh, for he cometh to judge the earth: he shall judge the world with righteousness, and the people with his truth.

\vs Psa 97:12 Rejoice in the \textsc{Lord}, ye righteous; and give thanks at the remembrance of his holiness.
