\vs Psa 101:1 A Psalm of David. I will sing of mercy and judgment: unto thee, O \textsc{Lord}, will I sing.
\vs Psa 101:2 I will behave myself wisely in a perfect way. O when wilt thou come unto me? I will walk within my house with a perfect heart.
\vs Psa 101:3 I will set no wicked thing before mine eyes: I hate the work of them that turn aside; \bibemph{it} shall not cleave to me.
\fn{wicked...: Heb. thing of Belial.}
\vs Psa 101:4 A froward heart shall depart from me: I will not know a wicked \bibemph{person}.
\vs Psa 101:5 Whoso privily slandereth his neighbour, him will I cut off: him that hath an high look and a proud heart will not I suffer.
\vs Psa 101:6 Mine eyes \bibemph{shall be} upon the faithful of the land, that they may dwell with me: he that walketh in a perfect way, he shall serve me.
\fn{in a...: or, perfect in the way.}
\vs Psa 101:7 He that worketh deceit shall not dwell within my house: he that telleth lies shall not tarry in my sight.
\fn{shall not tarry: Heb. shall not be established.}
\vs Psa 101:8 I will early destroy all the wicked of the land; that I may cut off all wicked doers from the city of the \textsc{Lord}.
\vs Psa 102:1 A Prayer of the afflicted, when he is overwhelmed, and poureth out his complaint before the \textsc{Lord}. Hear my prayer, O \textsc{Lord}, and let my cry come unto thee.
\fn{of: or, for.}
\vs Psa 102:2 Hide not thy face from me in the day \bibemph{when} I am in trouble; incline thine ear unto me: in the day \bibemph{when} I call answer me speedily.
\vs Psa 102:3 For my days are consumed like smoke, and my bones are burned as an hearth.
\fn{like...: or, (as some read) into smoke.}
\vs Psa 102:4 My heart is smitten, and withered like grass; so that I forget to eat my bread.
\vs Psa 102:5 By reason of the voice of my groaning my bones cleave to my skin.
\fn{skin: or, flesh.}
\vs Psa 102:6 I am like a pelican of the wilderness: I am like an owl of the desert.
\vs Psa 102:7 I watch, and am as a sparrow alone upon the house top.
\vs Psa 102:8 Mine enemies reproach me all the day; \bibemph{and} they that are mad against me are sworn against me.
\vs Psa 102:9 For I have eaten ashes like bread, and mingled my drink with weeping,
\vs Psa 102:10 Because of thine indignation and thy wrath: for thou hast lifted me up, and cast me down.
\vs Psa 102:11 My days \bibemph{are} like a shadow that declineth; and I am withered like grass.
\vs Psa 102:12 But thou, O \textsc{Lord}, shalt endure for ever; and thy remembrance unto all generations.
\vs Psa 102:13 Thou shalt arise, \bibemph{and} have mercy upon Zion: for the time to favour her, yea, the set time, is come.
\vs Psa 102:14 For thy servants take pleasure in her stones, and favour the dust thereof.
\vs Psa 102:15 So the heathen shall fear the name of the \textsc{Lord}, and all the kings of the earth thy glory.
\vs Psa 102:16 When the \textsc{Lord} shall build up Zion, he shall appear in his glory.
\vs Psa 102:17 He will regard the prayer of the destitute, and not despise their prayer.
\vs Psa 102:18 This shall be written for the generation to come: and the people which shall be created shall praise the \textsc{Lord}.
\vs Psa 102:19 For he hath looked down from the height of his sanctuary; from heaven did the \textsc{Lord} behold the earth;
\vs Psa 102:20 To hear the groaning of the prisoner; to loose those that are appointed to death;
\fn{those...: Heb. the children of death.}
\vs Psa 102:21 To declare the name of the \textsc{Lord} in Zion, and his praise in Jerusalem;
\vs Psa 102:22 When the people are gathered together, and the kingdoms, to serve the \textsc{Lord}.
\vs Psa 102:23 He weakened my strength in the way; he shortened my days.
\fn{weakened: Heb. afflicted.}
\vs Psa 102:24 I said, O my God, take me not away in the midst of my days: thy years \bibemph{are} throughout all generations.
\vs Psa 102:25 Of old hast thou laid the foundation of the earth: and the heavens \bibemph{are} the work of thy hands.
\vs Psa 102:26 They shall perish, but thou shalt endure: yea, all of them shall wax old like a garment; as a vesture shalt thou change them, and they shall be changed:
\fn{endure: Heb. stand.}
\vs Psa 102:27 But thou \bibemph{art} the same, and thy years shall have no end.
\vs Psa 102:28 The children of thy servants shall continue, and their seed shall be established before thee.
\vs Psa 103:1 \bibemph{A Psalm} of David. Bless the \textsc{Lord}, O my soul: and all that is within me, \bibemph{bless} his holy name.
\vs Psa 103:2 Bless the \textsc{Lord}, O my soul, and forget not all his benefits:
\vs Psa 103:3 Who forgiveth all thine iniquities; who healeth all thy diseases;
\vs Psa 103:4 Who redeemeth thy life from destruction; who crowneth thee with lovingkindness and tender mercies;
\vs Psa 103:5 Who satisfieth thy mouth with good \bibemph{things; so that} thy youth is renewed like the eagle's.
\vs Psa 103:6 The \textsc{Lord} executeth righteousness and judgment for all that are oppressed.
\vs Psa 103:7 He made known his ways unto Moses, his acts unto the children of Israel.
\vs Psa 103:8 The \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} merciful and gracious, slow to anger, and plenteous in mercy.
\vs Psa 103:9 He will not always chide: neither will he keep \bibemph{his anger} for ever.
\vs Psa 103:10 He hath not dealt with us after our sins; nor rewarded us according to our iniquities.
\vs Psa 103:11 For as the heaven is high above the earth, \bibemph{so} great is his mercy toward them that fear him.
\fn{as...: Heb. according to the height of the heaven.}
\vs Psa 103:12 As far as the east is from the west, \bibemph{so} far hath he removed our transgressions from us.
\vs Psa 103:13 Like as a father pitieth \bibemph{his} children, \bibemph{so} the \textsc{Lord} pitieth them that fear him.
\vs Psa 103:14 For he knoweth our frame; he remembereth that we \bibemph{are} dust.
\vs Psa 103:15 \bibemph{As for} man, his days \bibemph{are} as grass: as a flower of the field, so he flourisheth.
\vs Psa 103:16 For the wind passeth over it, and it is gone; and the place thereof shall know it no more.
\fn{it is...: Heb. it is not.}
\vs Psa 103:17 But the mercy of the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} from everlasting to everlasting upon them that fear him, and his righteousness unto children's children;
\vs Psa 103:18 To such as keep his covenant, and to those that remember his commandments to do them.
\vs Psa 103:19 The \textsc{Lord} hath prepared his throne in the heavens; and his kingdom ruleth over all.
\vs Psa 103:20 Bless the \textsc{Lord}, ye his angels, that excel in strength, that do his commandments, hearkening unto the voice of his word.
\fn{that excel...: Heb. mighty in strength.}
\vs Psa 103:21 Bless ye the \textsc{Lord}, all \bibemph{ye} his hosts; \bibemph{ye} ministers of his, that do his pleasure.
\vs Psa 103:22 Bless the \textsc{Lord}, all his works in all places of his dominion: bless the \textsc{Lord}, O my soul.
\vs Psa 104:1 Bless the \textsc{Lord}, O my soul. O \textsc{Lord} my God, thou art very great; thou art clothed with honour and majesty.
\vs Psa 104:2 Who coverest \bibemph{thyself} with light as \bibemph{with} a garment: who stretchest out the heavens like a curtain:
\vs Psa 104:3 Who layeth the beams of his chambers in the waters: who maketh the clouds his chariot: who walketh upon the wings of the wind:
\vs Psa 104:4 Who maketh his angels spirits; his ministers a flaming fire:
\vs Psa 104:5 \bibemph{Who} laid the foundations of the earth, \bibemph{that} it should not be removed for ever.
\fn{Who...: Heb. He hath founded the earth upon her bases.}
\vs Psa 104:6 Thou coveredst it with the deep as \bibemph{with} a garment: the waters stood above the mountains.
\vs Psa 104:7 At thy rebuke they fled; at the voice of thy thunder they hasted away.
\vs Psa 104:8 They go up by the mountains; they go down by the valleys unto the place which thou hast founded for them.
\fn{They go up...: or, The mountains ascend, the valleys descend.}
\vs Psa 104:9 Thou hast set a bound that they may not pass over; that they turn not again to cover the earth.
\vs Psa 104:10 He sendeth the springs into the valleys, \bibemph{which} run among the hills.
\fn{He: Heb. Who. run: Heb. walk.}
\vs Psa 104:11 They give drink to every beast of the field: the wild asses quench their thirst.
\fn{quench: Heb. break.}
\vs Psa 104:12 By them shall the fowls of the heaven have their habitation, \bibemph{which} sing among the branches.
\fn{sing: Heb. give a voice.}
\vs Psa 104:13 He watereth the hills from his chambers: the earth is satisfied with the fruit of thy works.
\vs Psa 104:14 He causeth the grass to grow for the cattle, and herb for the service of man: that he may bring forth food out of the earth;
\vs Psa 104:15 And wine \bibemph{that} maketh glad the heart of man, \bibemph{and} oil to make \bibemph{his} face to shine, and bread \bibemph{which} strengtheneth man's heart.
\fn{oil...: Heb. to make his face shine with oil, or, more than oil.}
\vs Psa 104:16 The trees of the \textsc{Lord} are full \bibemph{of sap}; the cedars of Lebanon, which he hath planted;
\vs Psa 104:17 Where the birds make their nests: \bibemph{as for} the stork, the fir trees \bibemph{are} her house.
\vs Psa 104:18 The high hills \bibemph{are} a refuge for the wild goats; \bibemph{and} the rocks for the conies.
\vs Psa 104:19 He appointed the moon for seasons: the sun knoweth his going down.
\vs Psa 104:20 Thou makest darkness, and it is night: wherein all the beasts of the forest do creep \bibemph{forth}.
\fn{beasts...: Heb. beasts thereof do trample on the forest.}
\vs Psa 104:21 The young lions roar after their prey, and seek their meat from God.
\vs Psa 104:22 The sun ariseth, they gather themselves together, and lay them down in their dens.
\vs Psa 104:23 Man goeth forth unto his work and to his labour until the evening.
\vs Psa 104:24 O \textsc{Lord}, how manifold are thy works! in wisdom hast thou made them all: the earth is full of thy riches.
\vs Psa 104:25 \bibemph{So is} this great and wide sea, wherein \bibemph{are} things creeping innumerable, both small and great beasts.
\vs Psa 104:26 There go the ships: \bibemph{there is} that leviathan, \bibemph{whom} thou hast made to play therein.
\fn{made: Heb. formed.}
\vs Psa 104:27 These wait all upon thee; that thou mayest give \bibemph{them} their meat in due season.
\vs Psa 104:28 \bibemph{That} thou givest them they gather: thou openest thine hand, they are filled with good.
\vs Psa 104:29 Thou hidest thy face, they are troubled: thou takest away their breath, they die, and return to their dust.
\vs Psa 104:30 Thou sendest forth thy spirit, they are created: and thou renewest the face of the earth.
\vs Psa 104:31 The glory of the \textsc{Lord} shall endure for ever: the \textsc{Lord} shall rejoice in his works.
\fn{endure: Heb. be.}
\vs Psa 104:32 He looketh on the earth, and it trembleth: he toucheth the hills, and they smoke.
\vs Psa 104:33 I will sing unto the \textsc{Lord} as long as I live: I will sing praise to my God while I have my being.
\vs Psa 104:34 My meditation of him shall be sweet: I will be glad in the \textsc{Lord}.
\vs Psa 104:35 Let the sinners be consumed out of the earth, and let the wicked be no more. Bless thou the \textsc{Lord}, O my soul. Praise ye the \textsc{Lord}.
\vs Psa 105:1 O give thanks unto the \textsc{Lord}; call upon his name: make known his deeds among the people.
\vs Psa 105:2 Sing unto him, sing psalms unto him: talk ye of all his wondrous works.
\vs Psa 105:3 Glory ye in his holy name: let the heart of them rejoice that seek the \textsc{Lord}.
\vs Psa 105:4 Seek the \textsc{Lord}, and his strength: seek his face evermore.
\vs Psa 105:5 Remember his marvellous works that he hath done; his wonders, and the judgments of his mouth;
\vs Psa 105:6 O ye seed of Abraham his servant, ye children of Jacob his chosen.
\vs Psa 105:7 He \bibemph{is} the \textsc{Lord} our God: his judgments \bibemph{are} in all the earth.
\vs Psa 105:8 He hath remembered his covenant for ever, the word \bibemph{which} he commanded to a thousand generations.
\vs Psa 105:9 Which \bibemph{covenant} he made with Abraham, and his oath unto Isaac;
\vs Psa 105:10 And confirmed the same unto Jacob for a law, \bibemph{and} to Israel \bibemph{for} an everlasting covenant:
\vs Psa 105:11 Saying, Unto thee will I give the land of Canaan, the lot of your inheritance:
\fn{lot: Heb. cord.}
\vs Psa 105:12 When they were \bibemph{but} a few men in number; yea, very few, and strangers in it.
\vs Psa 105:13 When they went from one nation to another, from \bibemph{one} kingdom to another people;
\vs Psa 105:14 He suffered no man to do them wrong: yea, he reproved kings for their sakes;
\vs Psa 105:15 \bibemph{Saying}, Touch not mine anointed, and do my prophets no harm.
\vs Psa 105:16 Moreover he called for a famine upon the land: he brake the whole staff of bread.
\vs Psa 105:17 He sent a man before them, \bibemph{even} Joseph, \bibemph{who} was sold for a servant:
\vs Psa 105:18 Whose feet they hurt with fetters: he was laid in iron:
\fn{he...: Heb. his soul came into iron.}
\vs Psa 105:19 Until the time that his word came: the word of the \textsc{Lord} tried him.
\vs Psa 105:20 The king sent and loosed him; \bibemph{even} the ruler of the people, and let him go free.
\vs Psa 105:21 He made him lord of his house, and ruler of all his substance:
\fn{substance: Heb. possession.}
\vs Psa 105:22 To bind his princes at his pleasure; and teach his senators wisdom.
\vs Psa 105:23 Israel also came into Egypt; and Jacob sojourned in the land of Ham.
\vs Psa 105:24 And he increased his people greatly; and made them stronger than their enemies.
\vs Psa 105:25 He turned their heart to hate his people, to deal subtilly with his servants.
\vs Psa 105:26 He sent Moses his servant; \bibemph{and} Aaron whom he had chosen.
\vs Psa 105:27 They shewed his signs among them, and wonders in the land of Ham.
\fn{his...: Heb. words of his signs.}
\vs Psa 105:28 He sent darkness, and made it dark; and they rebelled not against his word.
\vs Psa 105:29 He turned their waters into blood, and slew their fish.
\vs Psa 105:30 Their land brought forth frogs in abundance, in the chambers of their kings.
\vs Psa 105:31 He spake, and there came divers sorts of flies, \bibemph{and} lice in all their coasts.
\vs Psa 105:32 He gave them hail for rain, \bibemph{and} flaming fire in their land.
\fn{them...: Heb. their rain hail.}
\vs Psa 105:33 He smote their vines also and their fig trees; and brake the trees of their coasts.
\vs Psa 105:34 He spake, and the locusts came, and caterpillers, and that without number,
\vs Psa 105:35 And did eat up all the herbs in their land, and devoured the fruit of their ground.
\vs Psa 105:36 He smote also all the firstborn in their land, the chief of all their strength.
\vs Psa 105:37 He brought them forth also with silver and gold: and \bibemph{there was} not one feeble \bibemph{person} among their tribes.
\vs Psa 105:38 Egypt was glad when they departed: for the fear of them fell upon them.
\vs Psa 105:39 He spread a cloud for a covering; and fire to give light in the night.
\vs Psa 105:40 \bibemph{The people} asked, and he brought quails, and satisfied them with the bread of heaven.
\vs Psa 105:41 He opened the rock, and the waters gushed out; they ran in the dry places \bibemph{like} a river.
\vs Psa 105:42 For he remembered his holy promise, \bibemph{and} Abraham his servant.
\vs Psa 105:43 And he brought forth his people with joy, \bibemph{and} his chosen with gladness:
\fn{gladness: Heb. singing.}
\vs Psa 105:44 And gave them the lands of the heathen: and they inherited the labour of the people;
\vs Psa 105:45 That they might observe his statutes, and keep his laws. Praise ye the \textsc{Lord}.
\fn{Praise...: Heb. Hallelujah.}
\vs Psa 106:1 Praise ye the \textsc{Lord}. O give thanks unto the \textsc{Lord}; for \bibemph{he is} good: for his mercy \bibemph{endureth} for ever.
\fn{Praise...: Heb. Hallelujah.}
\vs Psa 106:2 Who can utter the mighty acts of the \textsc{Lord}? \bibemph{who} can shew forth all his praise?
\vs Psa 106:3 Blessed \bibemph{are} they that keep judgment, \bibemph{and} he that doeth righteousness at all times.
\vs Psa 106:4 Remember me, O \textsc{Lord}, with the favour \bibemph{that thou bearest unto} thy people: O visit me with thy salvation;
\vs Psa 106:5 That I may see the good of thy chosen, that I may rejoice in the gladness of thy nation, that I may glory with thine inheritance.
\vs Psa 106:6 We have sinned with our fathers, we have committed iniquity, we have done wickedly.
\vs Psa 106:7 Our fathers understood not thy wonders in Egypt; they remembered not the multitude of thy mercies; but provoked \bibemph{him} at the sea, \bibemph{even} at the Red sea.
\vs Psa 106:8 Nevertheless he saved them for his name's sake, that he might make his mighty power to be known.
\vs Psa 106:9 He rebuked the Red sea also, and it was dried up: so he led them through the depths, as through the wilderness.
\vs Psa 106:10 And he saved them from the hand of him that hated \bibemph{them}, and redeemed them from the hand of the enemy.
\vs Psa 106:11 And the waters covered their enemies: there was not one of them left.
\vs Psa 106:12 Then believed they his words; they sang his praise.
\vs Psa 106:13 They soon forgat his works; they waited not for his counsel:
\fn{They soon...: Heb. They made haste, they forgat.}
\vs Psa 106:14 But lusted exceedingly in the wilderness, and tempted God in the desert.
\fn{lusted...: Heb. lusted a lust.}
\vs Psa 106:15 And he gave them their request; but sent leanness into their soul.
\vs Psa 106:16 They envied Moses also in the camp, \bibemph{and} Aaron the saint of the \textsc{Lord}.
\vs Psa 106:17 The earth opened and swallowed up Dathan, and covered the company of Abiram.
\vs Psa 106:18 And a fire was kindled in their company; the flame burned up the wicked.
\vs Psa 106:19 They made a calf in Horeb, and worshipped the molten image.
\vs Psa 106:20 Thus they changed their glory into the similitude of an ox that eateth grass.
\vs Psa 106:21 They forgat God their saviour, which had done great things in Egypt;
\vs Psa 106:22 Wondrous works in the land of Ham, \bibemph{and} terrible things by the Red sea.
\vs Psa 106:23 Therefore he said that he would destroy them, had not Moses his chosen stood before him in the breach, to turn away his wrath, lest he should destroy \bibemph{them}.
\vs Psa 106:24 Yea, they despised the pleasant land, they believed not his word:
\fn{the pleasant...: Heb. a land of desire.}
\vs Psa 106:25 But murmured in their tents, \bibemph{and} hearkened not unto the voice of the \textsc{Lord}.
\vs Psa 106:26 Therefore he lifted up his hand against them, to overthrow them in the wilderness:
\fn{to overthrow: Heb. to make them fall.}
\vs Psa 106:27 To overthrow their seed also among the nations, and to scatter them in the lands.
\fn{to overthrow: Heb. to make them fall.}
\vs Psa 106:28 They joined themselves also unto Baalpeor, and ate the sacrifices of the dead.
\vs Psa 106:29 Thus they provoked \bibemph{him} to anger with their inventions: and the plague brake in upon them.
\vs Psa 106:30 Then stood up Phinehas, and executed judgment: and \bibemph{so} the plague was stayed.
\vs Psa 106:31 And that was counted unto him for righteousness unto all generations for evermore.
\vs Psa 106:32 They angered \bibemph{him} also at the waters of strife, so that it went ill with Moses for their sakes:
\vs Psa 106:33 Because they provoked his spirit, so that he spake unadvisedly with his lips.
\vs Psa 106:34 They did not destroy the nations, concerning whom the \textsc{Lord} commanded them:
\vs Psa 106:35 But were mingled among the heathen, and learned their works.
\vs Psa 106:36 And they served their idols: which were a snare unto them.
\vs Psa 106:37 Yea, they sacrificed their sons and their daughters unto devils,
\vs Psa 106:38 And shed innocent blood, \bibemph{even} the blood of their sons and of their daughters, whom they sacrificed unto the idols of Canaan: and the land was polluted with blood.
\vs Psa 106:39 Thus were they defiled with their own works, and went a whoring with their own inventions.
\vs Psa 106:40 Therefore was the wrath of the \textsc{Lord} kindled against his people, insomuch that he abhorred his own inheritance.
\vs Psa 106:41 And he gave them into the hand of the heathen; and they that hated them ruled over them.
\vs Psa 106:42 Their enemies also oppressed them, and they were brought into subjection under their hand.
\vs Psa 106:43 Many times did he deliver them; but they provoked \bibemph{him} with their counsel, and were brought low for their iniquity.
\fn{brought...: or, impoverished, or, weakened.}
\vs Psa 106:44 Nevertheless he regarded their affliction, when he heard their cry:
\vs Psa 106:45 And he remembered for them his covenant, and repented according to the multitude of his mercies.
\vs Psa 106:46 He made them also to be pitied of all those that carried them captives.
\vs Psa 106:47 Save us, O \textsc{Lord} our God, and gather us from among the heathen, to give thanks unto thy holy name, \bibemph{and} to triumph in thy praise.
\vs Psa 106:48 Blessed \bibemph{be} the \textsc{Lord} God of Israel from everlasting to everlasting: and let all the people say, Amen. Praise ye the \textsc{Lord}.
\fn{Praise...: Heb. Hallelujah.}
\vs Psa 107:1 O give thanks unto the \textsc{Lord}, for \bibemph{he is} good: for his mercy \bibemph{endureth} for ever.
\vs Psa 107:2 Let the redeemed of the \textsc{Lord} say \bibemph{so}, whom he hath redeemed from the hand of the enemy;
\vs Psa 107:3 And gathered them out of the lands, from the east, and from the west, from the north, and from the south.
\fn{south: Heb. sea.}
\vs Psa 107:4 They wandered in the wilderness in a solitary way; they found no city to dwell in.
\vs Psa 107:5 Hungry and thirsty, their soul fainted in them.
\vs Psa 107:6 Then they cried unto the \textsc{Lord} in their trouble, \bibemph{and} he delivered them out of their distresses.
\vs Psa 107:7 And he led them forth by the right way, that they might go to a city of habitation.
\vs Psa 107:8 Oh that \bibemph{men} would praise the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{for} his goodness, and \bibemph{for} his wonderful works to the children of men!
\vs Psa 107:9 For he satisfieth the longing soul, and filleth the hungry soul with goodness.
\vs Psa 107:10 Such as sit in darkness and in the shadow of death, \bibemph{being} bound in affliction and iron;
\vs Psa 107:11 Because they rebelled against the words of God, and contemned the counsel of the most High:
\vs Psa 107:12 Therefore he brought down their heart with labour; they fell down, and \bibemph{there was} none to help.
\vs Psa 107:13 Then they cried unto the \textsc{Lord} in their trouble, \bibemph{and} he saved them out of their distresses.
\vs Psa 107:14 He brought them out of darkness and the shadow of death, and brake their bands in sunder.
\vs Psa 107:15 Oh that \bibemph{men} would praise the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{for} his goodness, and \bibemph{for} his wonderful works to the children of men!
\vs Psa 107:16 For he hath broken the gates of brass, and cut the bars of iron in sunder.
\vs Psa 107:17 Fools because of their transgression, and because of their iniquities, are afflicted.
\vs Psa 107:18 Their soul abhorreth all manner of meat; and they draw near unto the gates of death.
\vs Psa 107:19 Then they cry unto the \textsc{Lord} in their trouble, \bibemph{and} he saveth them out of their distresses.
\vs Psa 107:20 He sent his word, and healed them, and delivered \bibemph{them} from their destructions.
\vs Psa 107:21 Oh that \bibemph{men} would praise the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{for} his goodness, and \bibemph{for} his wonderful works to the children of men!
\vs Psa 107:22 And let them sacrifice the sacrifices of thanksgiving, and declare his works with rejoicing.
\fn{rejoicing: Heb. singing.}
\vs Psa 107:23 They that go down to the sea in ships, that do business in great waters;
\vs Psa 107:24 These see the works of the \textsc{Lord}, and his wonders in the deep.
\vs Psa 107:25 For he commandeth, and raiseth the stormy wind, which lifteth up the waves thereof.
\fn{raiseth: Heb. maketh to stand.}
\vs Psa 107:26 They mount up to the heaven, they go down again to the depths: their soul is melted because of trouble.
\vs Psa 107:27 They reel to and fro, and stagger like a drunken man, and are at their wits' end.
\fn{are...: Heb. all their wisdom is swallowed up.}
\vs Psa 107:28 Then they cry unto the \textsc{Lord} in their trouble, and he bringeth them out of their distresses.
\vs Psa 107:29 He maketh the storm a calm, so that the waves thereof are still.
\vs Psa 107:30 Then are they glad because they be quiet; so he bringeth them unto their desired haven.
\vs Psa 107:31 Oh that \bibemph{men} would praise the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{for} his goodness, and \bibemph{for} his wonderful works to the children of men!
\vs Psa 107:32 Let them exalt him also in the congregation of the people, and praise him in the assembly of the elders.
\vs Psa 107:33 He turneth rivers into a wilderness, and the watersprings into dry ground;
\vs Psa 107:34 A fruitful land into barrenness, for the wickedness of them that dwell therein.
\fn{barrenness: Heb. saltiness.}
\vs Psa 107:35 He turneth the wilderness into a standing water, and dry ground into watersprings.
\vs Psa 107:36 And there he maketh the hungry to dwell, that they may prepare a city for habitation;
\vs Psa 107:37 And sow the fields, and plant vineyards, which may yield fruits of increase.
\vs Psa 107:38 He blesseth them also, so that they are multiplied greatly; and suffereth not their cattle to decrease.
\vs Psa 107:39 Again, they are minished and brought low through oppression, affliction, and sorrow.
\vs Psa 107:40 He poureth contempt upon princes, and causeth them to wander in the wilderness, \bibemph{where there is} no way.
\fn{wilderness: or, void place.}
\vs Psa 107:41 Yet setteth he the poor on high from affliction, and maketh \bibemph{him} families like a flock.
\fn{from: or, after.}
\vs Psa 107:42 The righteous shall see \bibemph{it}, and rejoice: and all iniquity shall stop her mouth.
\vs Psa 107:43 Whoso \bibemph{is} wise, and will observe these \bibemph{things}, even they shall understand the lovingkindness of the \textsc{Lord}.
\vs Psa 108:1 A Song \bibemph{or} Psalm of David. O God, my heart is fixed; I will sing and give praise, even with my glory.
\vs Psa 108:2 Awake, psaltery and harp: I \bibemph{myself} will awake early.
\vs Psa 108:3 I will praise thee, O \textsc{Lord}, among the people: and I will sing praises unto thee among the nations.
\vs Psa 108:4 For thy mercy \bibemph{is} great above the heavens: and thy truth \bibemph{reacheth} unto the clouds.
\fn{clouds: or, skies.}
\vs Psa 108:5 Be thou exalted, O God, above the heavens: and thy glory above all the earth;
\vs Psa 108:6 That thy beloved may be delivered: save \bibemph{with} thy right hand, and answer me.
\vs Psa 108:7 God hath spoken in his holiness; I will rejoice, I will divide Shechem, and mete out the valley of Succoth.
\vs Psa 108:8 Gilead \bibemph{is} mine; Manasseh \bibemph{is} mine; Ephraim also \bibemph{is} the strength of mine head; Judah \bibemph{is} my lawgiver;
\vs Psa 108:9 Moab \bibemph{is} my washpot; over Edom will I cast out my shoe; over Philistia will I triumph.
\vs Psa 108:10 Who will bring me into the strong city? who will lead me into Edom?
\vs Psa 108:11 \bibemph{Wilt} not \bibemph{thou}, O God, \bibemph{who} hast cast us off? and wilt not thou, O God, go forth with our hosts?
\vs Psa 108:12 Give us help from trouble: for vain \bibemph{is} the help of man.
\vs Psa 108:13 Through God we shall do valiantly: for he \bibemph{it is that} shall tread down our enemies.
\vs Psa 109:1 To the chief Musician, A Psalm of David. Hold not thy peace, O God of my praise;
\vs Psa 109:2 For the mouth of the wicked and the mouth of the deceitful are opened against me: they have spoken against me with a lying tongue.
\fn{of the deceitful: Heb. of deceit. are opened: Heb. have opened themselves.}
\vs Psa 109:3 They compassed me about also with words of hatred; and fought against me without a cause.
\vs Psa 109:4 For my love they are my adversaries: but I \bibemph{give myself unto} prayer.
\vs Psa 109:5 And they have rewarded me evil for good, and hatred for my love.
\vs Psa 109:6 Set thou a wicked man over him: and let Satan stand at his right hand.
\fn{Satan: or, an adversary.}
\vs Psa 109:7 When he shall be judged, let him be condemned: and let his prayer become sin.
\fn{be condemned: Heb. go out guilty, or, wicked.}
\vs Psa 109:8 Let his days be few; \bibemph{and} let another take his office.
\fn{office: or, charge.}
\vs Psa 109:9 Let his children be fatherless, and his wife a widow.
\vs Psa 109:10 Let his children be continually vagabonds, and beg: let them seek \bibemph{their bread} also out of their desolate places.
\vs Psa 109:11 Let the extortioner catch all that he hath; and let the strangers spoil his labour.
\vs Psa 109:12 Let there be none to extend mercy unto him: neither let there be any to favour his fatherless children.
\vs Psa 109:13 Let his posterity be cut off; \bibemph{and} in the generation following let their name be blotted out.
\vs Psa 109:14 Let the iniquity of his fathers be remembered with the \textsc{Lord}; and let not the sin of his mother be blotted out.
\vs Psa 109:15 Let them be before the \textsc{Lord} continually, that he may cut off the memory of them from the earth.
\vs Psa 109:16 Because that he remembered not to shew mercy, but persecuted the poor and needy man, that he might even slay the broken in heart.
\vs Psa 109:17 As he loved cursing, so let it come unto him: as he delighted not in blessing, so let it be far from him.
\vs Psa 109:18 As he clothed himself with cursing like as with his garment, so let it come into his bowels like water, and like oil into his bones.
\fn{into his bowels: Heb. within him.}
\vs Psa 109:19 Let it be unto him as the garment \bibemph{which} covereth him, and for a girdle wherewith he is girded continually.
\vs Psa 109:20 \bibemph{Let} this \bibemph{be} the reward of mine adversaries from the \textsc{Lord}, and of them that speak evil against my soul.
\vs Psa 109:21 But do thou for me, O GOD the Lord, for thy name's sake: because thy mercy \bibemph{is} good, deliver thou me.
\vs Psa 109:22 For I \bibemph{am} poor and needy, and my heart is wounded within me.
\vs Psa 109:23 I am gone like the shadow when it declineth: I am tossed up and down as the locust.
\vs Psa 109:24 My knees are weak through fasting; and my flesh faileth of fatness.
\vs Psa 109:25 I became also a reproach unto them: \bibemph{when} they looked upon me they shaked their heads.
\vs Psa 109:26 Help me, O \textsc{Lord} my God: O save me according to thy mercy:
\vs Psa 109:27 That they may know that this \bibemph{is} thy hand; \bibemph{that} thou, \textsc{Lord}, hast done it.
\vs Psa 109:28 Let them curse, but bless thou: when they arise, let them be ashamed; but let thy servant rejoice.
\vs Psa 109:29 Let mine adversaries be clothed with shame, and let them cover themselves with their own confusion, as with a mantle.
\vs Psa 109:30 I will greatly praise the \textsc{Lord} with my mouth; yea, I will praise him among the multitude.
\vs Psa 109:31 For he shall stand at the right hand of the poor, to save \bibemph{him} from those that condemn his soul.
\fn{those...: Heb. the judges of.}
\vs Psa 110:1 A Psalm of David. The \textsc{Lord} said unto my Lord, Sit thou at my right hand, until I make thine enemies thy footstool.
\vs Psa 110:2 The \textsc{Lord} shall send the rod of thy strength out of Zion: rule thou in the midst of thine enemies.
\vs Psa 110:3 Thy people \bibemph{shall be} willing in the day of thy power, in the beauties of holiness from the womb of the morning: thou hast the dew of thy youth.
\fn{from...: or, more than the womb of the morning: thou shalt have, etc.}
\vs Psa 110:4 The \textsc{Lord} hath sworn, and will not repent, Thou \bibemph{art} a priest for ever after the order of Melchizedek.
\vs Psa 110:5 The Lord at thy right hand shall strike through kings in the day of his wrath.
\vs Psa 110:6 He shall judge among the heathen, he shall fill \bibemph{the places} with the dead bodies; he shall wound the heads over many countries.
\fn{many: or, great.}
\vs Psa 110:7 He shall drink of the brook in the way: therefore shall he lift up the head.

\fn{Praise ye...: Heb. Hallelujah.}
\vs Psa 111:2 The works of the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{are} great, sought out of all them that have pleasure therein.
\vs Psa 111:3 His work \bibemph{is} honourable and glorious: and his righteousness endureth for ever.
\vs Psa 111:4 He hath made his wonderful works to be remembered: the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} gracious and full of compassion.
\vs Psa 111:5 He hath given meat unto them that fear him: he will ever be mindful of his covenant.
\fn{meat: Heb. prey.}
\vs Psa 111:6 He hath shewed his people the power of his works, that he may give them the heritage of the heathen.
\vs Psa 111:7 The works of his hands \bibemph{are} verity and judgment; all his commandments \bibemph{are} sure.
\vs Psa 111:8 They stand fast for ever and ever, \bibemph{and are} done in truth and uprightness.
\fn{stand...: Heb. are established.}
\vs Psa 111:9 He sent redemption unto his people: he hath commanded his covenant for ever: holy and reverend \bibemph{is} his name.
\vs Psa 111:10 The fear of the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} the beginning of wisdom: a good understanding have all they that do \bibemph{his commandments}: his praise endureth for ever.
\fn{a good...: or, good success. his commandments: Heb. them.}
\vs Psa 112:1 Praise ye the \textsc{Lord}. Blessed \bibemph{is} the man \bibemph{that} feareth the \textsc{Lord}, \bibemph{that} delighteth greatly in his commandments.

\vs Psa 112:2 His seed shall be mighty upon earth: the generation of the upright shall be blessed.
\vs Psa 112:3 Wealth and riches \bibemph{shall be} in his house: and his righteousness endureth for ever.
\vs Psa 112:4 Unto the upright there ariseth light in the darkness: \bibemph{he is} gracious, and full of compassion, and righteous.
\vs Psa 112:5 A good man sheweth favour, and lendeth: he will guide his affairs with discretion.
\fn{discretion: Heb. judgment.}
\vs Psa 112:6 Surely he shall not be moved for ever: the righteous shall be in everlasting remembrance.
\vs Psa 112:7 He shall not be afraid of evil tidings: his heart is fixed, trusting in the \textsc{Lord}.
\vs Psa 112:8 His heart \bibemph{is} established, he shall not be afraid, until he see \bibemph{his desire} upon his enemies.
\vs Psa 112:9 He hath dispersed, he hath given to the poor; his righteousness endureth for ever; his horn shall be exalted with honour.
\vs Psa 112:10 The wicked shall see \bibemph{it}, and be grieved; he shall gnash with his teeth, and melt away: the desire of the wicked shall perish.

\vs Psa 113:4 The \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} high above all nations, \bibemph{and} his glory above the heavens.

\vs Psa 114:4 The mountains skipped like rams, \bibemph{and} the little hills like lambs.

\vs Psa 115:1 Not unto us, O \textsc{Lord}, not unto us, but unto thy name give glory, for thy mercy, \bibemph{and} for thy truth's sake.
\vs Psa 115:2 Wherefore should the heathen say, Where \bibemph{is} now their God?
\vs Psa 115:3 But our God \bibemph{is} in the heavens: he hath done whatsoever he hath pleased.
\vs Psa 115:4 Their idols \bibemph{are} silver and gold, the work of men's hands.
\vs Psa 115:5 They have mouths, but they speak not: eyes have they, but they see not:
\vs Psa 115:6 They have ears, but they hear not: noses have they, but they smell not:
\vs Psa 115:7 They have hands, but they handle not: feet have they, but they walk not: neither speak they through their throat.
\vs Psa 115:8 They that make them are like unto them; \bibemph{so is} every one that trusteth in them.
\vs Psa 115:9 O Israel, trust thou in the \textsc{Lord}: he \bibemph{is} their help and their shield.
\vs Psa 115:10 O house of Aaron, trust in the \textsc{Lord}: he \bibemph{is} their help and their shield.
\vs Psa 115:11 Ye that fear the \textsc{Lord}, trust in the \textsc{Lord}: he \bibemph{is} their help and their shield.
\vs Psa 115:12 The \textsc{Lord} hath been mindful of us: he will bless \bibemph{us}; he will bless the house of Israel; he will bless the house of Aaron.
\vs Psa 115:13 He will bless them that fear the \textsc{Lord}, \bibemph{both} small and great.
\fn{and: Heb. with.}
\vs Psa 115:14 The \textsc{Lord} shall increase you more and more, you and your children.
\vs Psa 115:15 Ye \bibemph{are} blessed of the \textsc{Lord} which made heaven and earth.
\vs Psa 115:16 The heaven, \bibemph{even} the heavens, \bibemph{are} the \textsc{Lord's}: but the earth hath he given to the children of men.
\vs Psa 115:17 The dead praise not the \textsc{Lord}, neither any that go down into silence.
\vs Psa 115:18 But we will bless the \textsc{Lord} from this time forth and for evermore. Praise the \textsc{Lord}.
\vs Psa 116:1 I love the \textsc{Lord}, because he hath heard my voice \bibemph{and} my supplications.

\fn{as long...: Heb. in my days.}
\vs Psa 116:3 The sorrows of death compassed me, and the pains of hell gat hold upon me: I found trouble and sorrow.

\vs Psa 116:4 Then called I upon the name of the \textsc{Lord}; O \textsc{Lord}, I beseech thee, deliver my soul.
\vs Psa 116:5 Gracious \bibemph{is} the \textsc{Lord}, and righteous; yea, our God \bibemph{is} merciful.
\vs Psa 116:6 The \textsc{Lord} preserveth the simple: I was brought low, and he helped me.

\vs Psa 116:8 For thou hast delivered my soul from death, mine eyes from tears, \bibemph{and} my feet from falling.
\vs Psa 116:9 I will walk before the \textsc{Lord} in the land of the living.

\vs Psa 118:3 Let the house of Aaron now say, that his mercy \bibemph{endureth} for ever.
\vs Psa 118:4 Let them now that fear the \textsc{Lord} say, that his mercy \bibemph{endureth} for ever.
\vs Psa 118:5 I called upon the \textsc{Lord} in distress: the \textsc{Lord} answered me, \bibemph{and set me} in a large place.
\fn{in distress: Heb. out of distress.}
\vs Psa 118:6 The \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} on my side; I will not fear: what can man do unto me?
\fn{on...: Heb. for me.}
\vs Psa 118:7 The \textsc{Lord} taketh my part with them that help me: therefore shall I see \bibemph{my desire} upon them that hate me.
\vs Psa 118:8 \bibemph{It is} better to trust in the \textsc{Lord} than to put confidence in man.
\vs Psa 118:9 \bibemph{It is} better to trust in the \textsc{Lord} than to put confidence in princes.
\vs Psa 118:10 All nations compassed me about: but in the name of the \textsc{Lord} will I destroy them.
\fn{destroy...: Heb. cut them off.}
\vs Psa 118:11 They compassed me about; yea, they compassed me about: but in the name of the \textsc{Lord} I will destroy them.
\vs Psa 118:12 They compassed me about like bees; they are quenched as the fire of thorns: for in the name of the \textsc{Lord} I will destroy them.
\fn{destroy: Heb. cut down.}
\vs Psa 118:13 Thou hast thrust sore at me that I might fall: but the \textsc{Lord} helped me.
\vs Psa 118:14 The \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} my strength and song, and is become my salvation.
\vs Psa 118:15 The voice of rejoicing and salvation \bibemph{is} in the tabernacles of the righteous: the right hand of the \textsc{Lord} doeth valiantly.
\vs Psa 118:16 The right hand of the \textsc{Lord} is exalted: the right hand of the \textsc{Lord} doeth valiantly.
\vs Psa 118:17 I shall not die, but live, and declare the works of the \textsc{Lord}.
\vs Psa 118:18 The \textsc{Lord} hath chastened me sore: but he hath not given me over unto death.
\vs Psa 118:19 Open to me the gates of righteousness: I will go into them, \bibemph{and} I will praise the \textsc{Lord}:
\vs Psa 118:20 This gate of the \textsc{Lord}, into which the righteous shall enter.
\vs Psa 118:21 I will praise thee: for thou hast heard me, and art become my salvation.
\vs Psa 118:22 The stone \bibemph{which} the builders refused is become the head \bibemph{stone} of the corner.
\vs Psa 118:23 This is the \textsc{Lord's} doing; it \bibemph{is} marvellous in our eyes.
\fn{the \textsc{Lord's}...: Heb. from the \textsc{Lord}.}
\vs Psa 118:24 This \bibemph{is} the day \bibemph{which} the \textsc{Lord} hath made; we will rejoice and be glad in it.
\vs Psa 118:25 Save now, I beseech thee, O \textsc{Lord}: O \textsc{Lord}, I beseech thee, send now prosperity.
\vs Psa 118:26 Blessed \bibemph{be} he that cometh in the name of the \textsc{Lord}: we have blessed you out of the house of the \textsc{Lord}.
\vs Psa 118:27 God \bibemph{is} the \textsc{Lord}, which hath shewed us light: bind the sacrifice with cords, \bibemph{even} unto the horns of the altar.
\vs Psa 118:28 Thou \bibemph{art} my God, and I will praise thee: \bibemph{thou art} my God, I will exalt thee.
\vs Psa 118:29 O give thanks unto the \textsc{Lord}; for \bibemph{he is} good: for his mercy \bibemph{endureth} for ever.
\vs Psa 119:1 ALEPH. Blessed \bibemph{are} the undefiled in the way, who walk in the law of the \textsc{Lord}.
\fn{undefiled: or, perfect, or, sincere.}
\vs Psa 119:2 Blessed \bibemph{are} they that keep his testimonies, \bibemph{and that} seek him with the whole heart.
\vs Psa 119:3 They also do no iniquity: they walk in his ways.
\vs Psa 119:4 Thou hast commanded \bibemph{us} to keep thy precepts diligently.
\vs Psa 119:5 O that my ways were directed to keep thy statutes!
\vs Psa 119:6 Then shall I not be ashamed, when I have respect unto all thy commandments.
\vs Psa 119:7 I will praise thee with uprightness of heart, when I shall have learned thy righteous judgments.
\fn{thy...: Heb. judgments of thy righteousness.}
\vs Psa 119:8 I will keep thy statutes: O forsake me not utterly.
\vs Psa 119:9 BETH. Wherewithal shall a young man cleanse his way? by taking heed \bibemph{thereto} according to thy word.
\vs Psa 119:10 With my whole heart have I sought thee: O let me not wander from thy commandments.
\vs Psa 119:11 Thy word have I hid in mine heart, that I might not sin against thee.
\vs Psa 119:12 Blessed \bibemph{art} thou, O \textsc{Lord}: teach me thy statutes.
\vs Psa 119:13 With my lips have I declared all the judgments of thy mouth.
\vs Psa 119:14 I have rejoiced in the way of thy testimonies, as \bibemph{much as} in all riches.
\vs Psa 119:15 I will meditate in thy precepts, and have respect unto thy ways.
\vs Psa 119:16 I will delight myself in thy statutes: I will not forget thy word.
\vs Psa 119:17 GIMEL. Deal bountifully with thy servant, \bibemph{that} I may live, and keep thy word.
\vs Psa 119:18 Open thou mine eyes, that I may behold wondrous things out of thy law.
\fn{Open: Heb. Reveal.}
\vs Psa 119:19 I \bibemph{am} a stranger in the earth: hide not thy commandments from me.
\vs Psa 119:20 My soul breaketh for the longing \bibemph{that it hath} unto thy judgments at all times.
\vs Psa 119:21 Thou hast rebuked the proud \bibemph{that are} cursed, which do err from thy commandments.
\vs Psa 119:22 Remove from me reproach and contempt; for I have kept thy testimonies.
\vs Psa 119:23 Princes also did sit \bibemph{and} speak against me: \bibemph{but} thy servant did meditate in thy statutes.
\vs Psa 119:24 Thy testimonies also \bibemph{are} my delight \bibemph{and} my counsellors.
\fn{my counsellors: Heb. men of my counsel.}
\vs Psa 119:25 DALETH. My soul cleaveth unto the dust: quicken thou me according to thy word.
\vs Psa 119:26 I have declared my ways, and thou heardest me: teach me thy statutes.
\vs Psa 119:27 Make me to understand the way of thy precepts: so shall I talk of thy wondrous works.
\vs Psa 119:28 My soul melteth for heaviness: strengthen thou me according unto thy word.
\fn{melteth: Heb. droppeth.}
\vs Psa 119:29 Remove from me the way of lying: and grant me thy law graciously.
\vs Psa 119:30 I have chosen the way of truth: thy judgments have I laid \bibemph{before me}.
\vs Psa 119:31 I have stuck unto thy testimonies: O \textsc{Lord}, put me not to shame.
\vs Psa 119:32 I will run the way of thy commandments, when thou shalt enlarge my heart.
\vs Psa 119:33 HE. Teach me, O \textsc{Lord}, the way of thy statutes; and I shall keep it \bibemph{unto} the end.
\vs Psa 119:34 Give me understanding, and I shall keep thy law; yea, I shall observe it with \bibemph{my} whole heart.
\vs Psa 119:35 Make me to go in the path of thy commandments; for therein do I delight.
\vs Psa 119:36 Incline my heart unto thy testimonies, and not to covetousness.
\vs Psa 119:37 Turn away mine eyes from beholding vanity; \bibemph{and} quicken thou me in thy way.
\fn{Turn...: Heb. Make to pass.}
\vs Psa 119:38 Stablish thy word unto thy servant, who \bibemph{is devoted} to thy fear.
\vs Psa 119:39 Turn away my reproach which I fear: for thy judgments \bibemph{are} good.
\vs Psa 119:40 Behold, I have longed after thy precepts: quicken me in thy righteousness.
\vs Psa 119:41 VAU. Let thy mercies come also unto me, O \textsc{Lord}, \bibemph{even} thy salvation, according to thy word.
\vs Psa 119:42 So shall I have wherewith to answer him that reproacheth me: for I trust in thy word.
\fn{So...: or, So shall I answer him that reproveth me in a thing.}
\vs Psa 119:43 And take not the word of truth utterly out of my mouth; for I have hoped in thy judgments.
\vs Psa 119:44 So shall I keep thy law continually for ever and ever.
\vs Psa 119:45 And I will walk at liberty: for I seek thy precepts.
\fn{at liberty: Heb. at large.}
\vs Psa 119:46 I will speak of thy testimonies also before kings, and will not be ashamed.
\vs Psa 119:47 And I will delight myself in thy commandments, which I have loved.
\vs Psa 119:48 My hands also will I lift up unto thy commandments, which I have loved; and I will meditate in thy statutes.
\vs Psa 119:49 ZAIN. Remember the word unto thy servant, upon which thou hast caused me to hope.
\vs Psa 119:50 This \bibemph{is} my comfort in my affliction: for thy word hath quickened me.
\vs Psa 119:51 The proud have had me greatly in derision: \bibemph{yet} have I not declined from thy law.
\vs Psa 119:52 I remembered thy judgments of old, O \textsc{Lord}; and have comforted myself.
\vs Psa 119:53 Horror hath taken hold upon me because of the wicked that forsake thy law.
\vs Psa 119:54 Thy statutes have been my songs in the house of my pilgrimage.
\vs Psa 119:55 I have remembered thy name, O \textsc{Lord}, in the night, and have kept thy law.
\vs Psa 119:56 This I had, because I kept thy precepts.
\vs Psa 119:57 CHETH. \bibemph{Thou art} my portion, O \textsc{Lord}: I have said that I would keep thy words.
\vs Psa 119:58 I intreated thy favour with \bibemph{my} whole heart: be merciful unto me according to thy word.
\fn{favour: Heb. face.}
\vs Psa 119:59 I thought on my ways, and turned my feet unto thy testimonies.
\vs Psa 119:60 I made haste, and delayed not to keep thy commandments.
\vs Psa 119:61 The bands of the wicked have robbed me: \bibemph{but} I have not forgotten thy law.
\fn{bands: or, companies.}
\vs Psa 119:62 At midnight I will rise to give thanks unto thee because of thy righteous judgments.
\vs Psa 119:63 I \bibemph{am} a companion of all \bibemph{them} that fear thee, and of them that keep thy precepts.
\vs Psa 119:64 The earth, O \textsc{Lord}, is full of thy mercy: teach me thy statutes.
\vs Psa 119:65 TETH. Thou hast dealt well with thy servant, O \textsc{Lord}, according unto thy word.
\vs Psa 119:66 Teach me good judgment and knowledge: for I have believed thy commandments.
\vs Psa 119:67 Before I was afflicted I went astray: but now have I kept thy word.
\vs Psa 119:68 Thou \bibemph{art} good, and doest good; teach me thy statutes.
\vs Psa 119:69 The proud have forged a lie against me: \bibemph{but} I will keep thy precepts with \bibemph{my} whole heart.
\vs Psa 119:70 Their heart is as fat as grease; \bibemph{but} I delight in thy law.
\vs Psa 119:71 \bibemph{It is} good for me that I have been afflicted; that I might learn thy statutes.
\vs Psa 119:72 The law of thy mouth \bibemph{is} better unto me than thousands of gold and silver.
\vs Psa 119:73 JOD. Thy hands have made me and fashioned me: give me understanding, that I may learn thy commandments.
\vs Psa 119:74 They that fear thee will be glad when they see me; because I have hoped in thy word.
\vs Psa 119:75 I know, O \textsc{Lord}, that thy judgments \bibemph{are} right, and \bibemph{that} thou in faithfulness hast afflicted me.
\fn{right: Heb. righteousness.}
\vs Psa 119:76 Let, I pray thee, thy merciful kindness be for my comfort, according to thy word unto thy servant.
\fn{for...: Heb. to comfort me.}
\vs Psa 119:77 Let thy tender mercies come unto me, that I may live: for thy law \bibemph{is} my delight.
\vs Psa 119:78 Let the proud be ashamed; for they dealt perversely with me without a cause: \bibemph{but} I will meditate in thy precepts.
\vs Psa 119:79 Let those that fear thee turn unto me, and those that have known thy testimonies.
\vs Psa 119:80 Let my heart be sound in thy statutes; that I be not ashamed.
\vs Psa 119:81 CAPH. My soul fainteth for thy salvation: \bibemph{but} I hope in thy word.
\vs Psa 119:82 Mine eyes fail for thy word, saying, When wilt thou comfort me?
\vs Psa 119:83 For I am become like a bottle in the smoke; \bibemph{yet} do I not forget thy statutes.
\vs Psa 119:84 How many \bibemph{are} the days of thy servant? when wilt thou execute judgment on them that persecute me?
\vs Psa 119:85 The proud have digged pits for me, which \bibemph{are} not after thy law.
\vs Psa 119:86 All thy commandments \bibemph{are} faithful: they persecute me wrongfully; help thou me.
\fn{faithful: Heb. faithfulness.}
\vs Psa 119:87 They had almost consumed me upon earth; but I forsook not thy precepts.
\vs Psa 119:88 Quicken me after thy lovingkindness; so shall I keep the testimony of thy mouth.
\vs Psa 119:89 LAMED. For ever, O \textsc{Lord}, thy word is settled in heaven.
\vs Psa 119:90 Thy faithfulness \bibemph{is} unto all generations: thou hast established the earth, and it abideth.
\fn{unto...: Heb. to generation and generation. abideth: Heb. standeth.}
\vs Psa 119:91 They continue this day according to thine ordinances: for all \bibemph{are} thy servants.
\vs Psa 119:92 Unless thy law \bibemph{had been} my delights, I should then have perished in mine affliction.
\vs Psa 119:93 I will never forget thy precepts: for with them thou hast quickened me.
\vs Psa 119:94 I \bibemph{am} thine, save me; for I have sought thy precepts.
\vs Psa 119:95 The wicked have waited for me to destroy me: \bibemph{but} I will consider thy testimonies.
\vs Psa 119:96 I have seen an end of all perfection: \bibemph{but} thy commandment \bibemph{is} exceeding broad.
\vs Psa 119:97 MEM. O how love I thy law! it \bibemph{is} my meditation all the day.
\vs Psa 119:98 Thou through thy commandments hast made me wiser than mine enemies: for they \bibemph{are} ever with me.
\fn{they...: Heb. it is ever with me.}
\vs Psa 119:99 I have more understanding than all my teachers: for thy testimonies \bibemph{are} my meditation.
\vs Psa 119:100 I understand more than the ancients, because I keep thy precepts.
\vs Psa 119:101 I have refrained my feet from every evil way, that I might keep thy word.
\vs Psa 119:102 I have not departed from thy judgments: for thou hast taught me.
\vs Psa 119:103 How sweet are thy words unto my taste! \bibemph{yea, sweeter} than honey to my mouth!
\fn{taste: Heb. palate.}
\vs Psa 119:104 Through thy precepts I get understanding: therefore I hate every false way.
\vs Psa 119:105 NUN. Thy word \bibemph{is} a lamp unto my feet, and a light unto my path.
\fn{lamp: or, candle.}
\vs Psa 119:106 I have sworn, and I will perform \bibemph{it}, that I will keep thy righteous judgments.
\vs Psa 119:107 I am afflicted very much: quicken me, O \textsc{Lord}, according unto thy word.
\vs Psa 119:108 Accept, I beseech thee, the freewill offerings of my mouth, O \textsc{Lord}, and teach me thy judgments.
\vs Psa 119:109 My soul \bibemph{is} continually in my hand: yet do I not forget thy law.
\vs Psa 119:110 The wicked have laid a snare for me: yet I erred not from thy precepts.
\vs Psa 119:111 Thy testimonies have I taken as an heritage for ever: for they \bibemph{are} the rejoicing of my heart.
\vs Psa 119:112 I have inclined mine heart to perform thy statutes alway, \bibemph{even unto} the end.
\fn{to perform: Heb. to do.}
\vs Psa 119:113 SAMECH. I hate \bibemph{vain} thoughts: but thy law do I love.
\vs Psa 119:114 Thou \bibemph{art} my hiding place and my shield: I hope in thy word.
\vs Psa 119:115 Depart from me, ye evildoers: for I will keep the commandments of my God.
\vs Psa 119:116 Uphold me according unto thy word, that I may live: and let me not be ashamed of my hope.
\vs Psa 119:117 Hold thou me up, and I shall be safe: and I will have respect unto thy statutes continually.
\vs Psa 119:118 Thou hast trodden down all them that err from thy statutes: for their deceit \bibemph{is} falsehood.
\vs Psa 119:119 Thou puttest away all the wicked of the earth \bibemph{like} dross: therefore I love thy testimonies.
\fn{puttest...: Heb. causest to cease.}
\vs Psa 119:120 My flesh trembleth for fear of thee; and I am afraid of thy judgments.
\vs Psa 119:121 AIN. I have done judgment and justice: leave me not to mine oppressors.
\vs Psa 119:122 Be surety for thy servant for good: let not the proud oppress me.
\vs Psa 119:123 Mine eyes fail for thy salvation, and for the word of thy righteousness.
\vs Psa 119:124 Deal with thy servant according unto thy mercy, and teach me thy statutes.
\vs Psa 119:125 I \bibemph{am} thy servant; give me understanding, that I may know thy testimonies.
\vs Psa 119:126 \bibemph{It is} time for \bibemph{thee}, \textsc{Lord}, to work: \bibemph{for} they have made void thy law.
\vs Psa 119:127 Therefore I love thy commandments above gold; yea, above fine gold.
\vs Psa 119:128 Therefore I esteem all \bibemph{thy} precepts \bibemph{concerning} all \bibemph{things to be} right; \bibemph{and} I hate every false way.
\vs Psa 119:129 PE. Thy testimonies \bibemph{are} wonderful: therefore doth my soul keep them.
\vs Psa 119:130 The entrance of thy words giveth light; it giveth understanding unto the simple.
\vs Psa 119:131 I opened my mouth, and panted: for I longed for thy commandments.
\vs Psa 119:132 Look thou upon me, and be merciful unto me, as thou usest to do unto those that love thy name.
\fn{as thou...: Heb. according to the custom toward those, etc.}
\vs Psa 119:133 Order my steps in thy word: and let not any iniquity have dominion over me.
\vs Psa 119:134 Deliver me from the oppression of man: so will I keep thy precepts.
\vs Psa 119:135 Make thy face to shine upon thy servant; and teach me thy statutes.
\vs Psa 119:136 Rivers of waters run down mine eyes, because they keep not thy law.
\vs Psa 119:137 TZADDI. Righteous \bibemph{art} thou, O \textsc{Lord}, and upright \bibemph{are} thy judgments.
\vs Psa 119:138 Thy testimonies \bibemph{that} thou hast commanded \bibemph{are} righteous and very faithful.
\fn{righteous: Heb. righteousness. faithful: Heb. faithfulness.}
\vs Psa 119:139 My zeal hath consumed me, because mine enemies have forgotten thy words.
\fn{consumed...: Heb. cut me off.}
\vs Psa 119:140 Thy word \bibemph{is} very pure: therefore thy servant loveth it.
\fn{pure: Heb. tried, or, refined.}
\vs Psa 119:141 I \bibemph{am} small and despised: \bibemph{yet} do not I forget thy precepts.
\vs Psa 119:142 Thy righteousness \bibemph{is} an everlasting righteousness, and thy law \bibemph{is} the truth.
\vs Psa 119:143 Trouble and anguish have taken hold on me: \bibemph{yet} thy commandments \bibemph{are} my delights.
\fn{taken...: Heb. found me.}
\vs Psa 119:144 The righteousness of thy testimonies \bibemph{is} everlasting: give me understanding, and I shall live.
\vs Psa 119:145 KOPH. I cried with \bibemph{my} whole heart; hear me, O \textsc{Lord}: I will keep thy statutes.
\vs Psa 119:146 I cried unto thee; save me, and I shall keep thy testimonies.
\fn{and I...: or, that I may keep.}
\vs Psa 119:147 I prevented the dawning of the morning, and cried: I hoped in thy word.
\vs Psa 119:148 Mine eyes prevent the \bibemph{night} watches, that I might meditate in thy word.
\vs Psa 119:149 Hear my voice according unto thy lovingkindness: O \textsc{Lord}, quicken me according to thy judgment.
\vs Psa 119:150 They draw nigh that follow after mischief: they are far from thy law.
\vs Psa 119:151 Thou \bibemph{art} near, O \textsc{Lord}; and all thy commandments \bibemph{are} truth.
\vs Psa 119:152 Concerning thy testimonies, I have known of old that thou hast founded them for ever.
\vs Psa 119:153 RESH. Consider mine affliction, and deliver me: for I do not forget thy law.
\vs Psa 119:154 Plead my cause, and deliver me: quicken me according to thy word.
\vs Psa 119:155 Salvation \bibemph{is} far from the wicked: for they seek not thy statutes.
\vs Psa 119:156 Great \bibemph{are} thy tender mercies, O \textsc{Lord}: quicken me according to thy judgments.
\fn{Great: or, Many.}
\vs Psa 119:157 Many \bibemph{are} my persecutors and mine enemies; \bibemph{yet} do I not decline from thy testimonies.
\vs Psa 119:158 I beheld the transgressors, and was grieved; because they kept not thy word.
\vs Psa 119:159 Consider how I love thy precepts: quicken me, O \textsc{Lord}, according to thy lovingkindness.
\vs Psa 119:160 Thy word \bibemph{is} true \bibemph{from} the beginning: and every one of thy righteous judgments \bibemph{endureth} for ever.
\fn{Thy word...: Heb. The beginning of thy word is true.}
\vs Psa 119:161 SCHIN. Princes have persecuted me without a cause: but my heart standeth in awe of thy word.
\vs Psa 119:162 I rejoice at thy word, as one that findeth great spoil.
\vs Psa 119:163 I hate and abhor lying: \bibemph{but} thy law do I love.
\vs Psa 119:164 Seven times a day do I praise thee because of thy righteous judgments.
\vs Psa 119:165 Great peace have they which love thy law: and nothing shall offend them.
\fn{nothing...: Heb. they shall have no stumblingblock.}
\vs Psa 119:166 \textsc{Lord}, I have hoped for thy salvation, and done thy commandments.
\vs Psa 119:167 My soul hath kept thy testimonies; and I love them exceedingly.
\vs Psa 119:168 I have kept thy precepts and thy testimonies: for all my ways \bibemph{are} before thee.
\vs Psa 119:169 TAU. Let my cry come near before thee, O \textsc{Lord}: give me understanding according to thy word.
\vs Psa 119:170 Let my supplication come before thee: deliver me according to thy word.
\vs Psa 119:171 My lips shall utter praise, when thou hast taught me thy statutes.
\vs Psa 119:172 My tongue shall speak of thy word: for all thy commandments \bibemph{are} righteousness.
\vs Psa 119:173 Let thine hand help me; for I have chosen thy precepts.
\vs Psa 119:174 I have longed for thy salvation, O \textsc{Lord}; and thy law \bibemph{is} my delight.
\vs Psa 119:175 Let my soul live, and it shall praise thee; and let thy judgments help me.
\vs Psa 119:176 I have gone astray like a lost sheep; seek thy servant; for I do not forget thy commandments.
\vs Psa 120:1 A Song of degrees. In my distress I cried unto the \textsc{Lord}, and he heard me.
\vs Psa 120:2 Deliver my soul, O \textsc{Lord}, from lying lips, \bibemph{and} from a deceitful tongue.
\vs Psa 120:3 What shall be given unto thee? or what shall be done unto thee, thou false tongue?
\fn{What shall be given...: or, What shall the deceitful tongue give unto thee? or, what shall is profit thee?. done: Heb. added.}
\vs Psa 120:4 Sharp arrows of the mighty, with coals of juniper.
\fn{Sharp...: or, It is as the sharp arrows of the mighty man, with coals of juniper.}
\vs Psa 120:5 Woe is me, that I sojourn in Mesech, \bibemph{that} I dwell in the tents of Kedar!
\vs Psa 120:6 My soul hath long dwelt with him that hateth peace.
\vs Psa 120:7 I \bibemph{am for} peace: but when I speak, they \bibemph{are} for war.
\fn{for peace: or, a man of peace.}
\vs Psa 121:1 A Song of degrees. I will lift up mine eyes unto the hills, from whence cometh my help.
\fn{I will...: or, Shall I lift up mine eyes to the hills? whence should my help come?.}
\vs Psa 121:2 My help \bibemph{cometh} from the \textsc{Lord}, which made heaven and earth.
\vs Psa 121:3 He will not suffer thy foot to be moved: he that keepeth thee will not slumber.
\vs Psa 121:4 Behold, he that keepeth Israel shall neither slumber nor sleep.
\vs Psa 121:5 The \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} thy keeper: the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} thy shade upon thy right hand.
\vs Psa 121:6 The sun shall not smite thee by day, nor the moon by night.
\vs Psa 121:7 The \textsc{Lord} shall preserve thee from all evil: he shall preserve thy soul.
\vs Psa 121:8 The \textsc{Lord} shall preserve thy going out and thy coming in from this time forth, and even for evermore.
\vs Psa 122:1 A Song of degrees of David. I was glad when they said unto me, Let us go into the house of the \textsc{Lord}.
\vs Psa 122:2 Our feet shall stand within thy gates, O Jerusalem.
\vs Psa 122:3 Jerusalem is builded as a city that is compact together:
\vs Psa 122:4 Whither the tribes go up, the tribes of the \textsc{Lord}, unto the testimony of Israel, to give thanks unto the name of the \textsc{Lord}.
\vs Psa 122:5 For there are set thrones of judgment, the thrones of the house of David.
\fn{are...: Heb. do sit.}
\vs Psa 122:6 Pray for the peace of Jerusalem: they shall prosper that love thee.
\vs Psa 122:7 Peace be within thy walls, \bibemph{and} prosperity within thy palaces.
\vs Psa 122:8 For my brethren and companions' sakes, I will now say, Peace \bibemph{be} within thee.
\vs Psa 122:9 Because of the house of the \textsc{Lord} our God I will seek thy good.
\vs Psa 123:1 A Song of degrees. Unto thee lift I up mine eyes, O thou that dwellest in the heavens.
\vs Psa 123:2 Behold, as the eyes of servants \bibemph{look} unto the hand of their masters, \bibemph{and} as the eyes of a maiden unto the hand of her mistress; so our eyes \bibemph{wait} upon the \textsc{Lord} our God, until that he have mercy upon us.
\vs Psa 123:3 Have mercy upon us, O \textsc{Lord}, have mercy upon us: for we are exceedingly filled with contempt.
\vs Psa 123:4 Our soul is exceedingly filled with the scorning of those that are at ease, \bibemph{and} with the contempt of the proud.
\vs Psa 124:1 A Song of degrees of David. If \bibemph{it had not been} the \textsc{Lord} who was on our side, now may Israel say;
\vs Psa 124:2 If \bibemph{it had not been} the \textsc{Lord} who was on our side, when men rose up against us:
\vs Psa 124:3 Then they had swallowed us up quick, when their wrath was kindled against us:
\vs Psa 124:4 Then the waters had overwhelmed us, the stream had gone over our soul:
\vs Psa 124:5 Then the proud waters had gone over our soul.
\vs Psa 124:6 Blessed \bibemph{be} the \textsc{Lord}, who hath not given us \bibemph{as} a prey to their teeth.
\vs Psa 124:7 Our soul is escaped as a bird out of the snare of the fowlers: the snare is broken, and we are escaped.
\vs Psa 124:8 Our help \bibemph{is} in the name of the \textsc{Lord}, who made heaven and earth.
\vs Psa 125:1 A Song of degrees. They that trust in the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{shall be} as mount Zion, \bibemph{which} cannot be removed, \bibemph{but} abideth for ever.
\vs Psa 125:2 As the mountains \bibemph{are} round about Jerusalem, so the \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} round about his people from henceforth even for ever.
\vs Psa 125:3 For the rod of the wicked shall not rest upon the lot of the righteous; lest the righteous put forth their hands unto iniquity.
\fn{the wicked: Heb. wickedness.}
\vs Psa 125:4 Do good, O \textsc{Lord}, unto \bibemph{those that be} good, and \bibemph{to them that are} upright in their hearts.
\vs Psa 125:5 As for such as turn aside unto their crooked ways, the \textsc{Lord} shall lead them forth with the workers of iniquity: \bibemph{but} peace \bibemph{shall be} upon Israel.
\vs Psa 126:1 A Song of degrees. When the \textsc{Lord} turned again the captivity of Zion, we were like them that dream.
\fn{turned...: Heb. returned the returning.}
\vs Psa 126:2 Then was our mouth filled with laughter, and our tongue with singing: then said they among the heathen, The \textsc{Lord} hath done great things for them.
\fn{hath...: Heb. hath magnified to do with them.}
\vs Psa 126:3 The \textsc{Lord} hath done great things for us; \bibemph{whereof} we are glad.
\vs Psa 126:4 Turn again our captivity, O \textsc{Lord}, as the streams in the south.
\vs Psa 126:5 They that sow in tears shall reap in joy.
\fn{joy: or, singing.}
\vs Psa 126:6 He that goeth forth and weepeth, bearing precious seed, shall doubtless come again with rejoicing, bringing his sheaves \bibemph{with him}.

\vs Psa 127:1 A Song of degrees for Solomon. Except the \textsc{Lord} build the house, they labour in vain that build it: except the \textsc{Lord} keep the city, the watchman waketh \bibemph{but} in vain.

\vs Psa 139:1 To the chief Musician, A Psalm of David. O \textsc{Lord}, thou hast searched me, and known \bibemph{me}.
\vs Psa 139:2 Thou knowest my downsitting and mine uprising, thou understandest my thought afar off.
\vs Psa 139:3 Thou compassest my path and my lying down, and art acquainted \bibemph{with} all my ways.
\fn{compassest: or, winnowest.}
\vs Psa 139:4 For \bibemph{there is} not a word in my tongue, \bibemph{but}, lo, O \textsc{Lord}, thou knowest it altogether.
\vs Psa 139:5 Thou hast beset me behind and before, and laid thine hand upon me.
\vs Psa 139:6 \bibemph{Such} knowledge \bibemph{is} too wonderful for me; it is high, I cannot \bibemph{attain} unto it.
\vs Psa 139:7 Whither shall I go from thy spirit? or whither shall I flee from thy presence?
\vs Psa 139:8 If I ascend up into heaven, thou \bibemph{art} there: if I make my bed in hell, behold, thou \bibemph{art there}.
\vs Psa 139:9 \bibemph{If} I take the wings of the morning, \bibemph{and} dwell in the uttermost parts of the sea;
\vs Psa 139:10 Even there shall thy hand lead me, and thy right hand shall hold me.
\vs Psa 139:11 If I say, Surely the darkness shall cover me; even the night shall be light about me.
\vs Psa 139:12 Yea, the darkness hideth not from thee; but the night shineth as the day: the darkness and the light \bibemph{are} both alike \bibemph{to thee}.
\fn{hideth...: Heb. darkeneth not. the darkness and...: Heb. as is the darkness, so is the light.}
\vs Psa 139:13 For thou hast possessed my reins: thou hast covered me in my mother's womb.
\vs Psa 139:14 I will praise thee; for I am fearfully \bibemph{and} wonderfully made: marvellous \bibemph{are} thy works; and \bibemph{that} my soul knoweth right well.
\fn{right...: Heb. greatly.}
\vs Psa 139:15 My substance was not hid from thee, when I was made in secret, \bibemph{and} curiously wrought in the lowest parts of the earth.
\fn{substance: or, strength, or, body.}
\vs Psa 139:16 Thine eyes did see my substance, yet being unperfect; and in thy book all \bibemph{my members} were written, \bibemph{which} in continuance were fashioned, when \bibemph{as yet there was} none of them.
\fn{all...: Heb. all of them. which...: or, what days they should be fashioned.}
\vs Psa 139:17 How precious also are thy thoughts unto me, O God! how great is the sum of them!
\vs Psa 139:18 \bibemph{If} I should count them, they are more in number than the sand: when I awake, I am still with thee.
\vs Psa 139:19 Surely thou wilt slay the wicked, O God: depart from me therefore, ye bloody men.
\vs Psa 139:20 For they speak against thee wickedly, \bibemph{and} thine enemies take \bibemph{thy name} in vain.
\vs Psa 139:21 Do not I hate them, O \textsc{Lord}, that hate thee? and am not I grieved with those that rise up against thee?
\vs Psa 139:22 I hate them with perfect hatred: I count them mine enemies.
\vs Psa 139:23 Search me, O God, and know my heart: try me, and know my thoughts:
\vs Psa 139:24 And see if \bibemph{there be any} wicked way in me, and lead me in the way everlasting.
\fn{wicked...: Heb. way of pain, or, grief.}

\vs Psa 140:2 Which imagine mischiefs in \bibemph{their} heart; continually are they gathered together \bibemph{for} war.
\vs Psa 140:3 They have sharpened their tongues like a serpent; adders' poison \bibemph{is} under their lips. Selah.
\vs Psa 140:4 Keep me, O \textsc{Lord}, from the hands of the wicked; preserve me from the violent man; who have purposed to overthrow my goings.
\vs Psa 140:5 The proud have hid a snare for me, and cords; they have spread a net by the wayside; they have set gins for me. Selah.

\vs Psa 143:2 And enter not into judgment with thy servant: for in thy sight shall no man living be justified.
\vs Psa 143:3 For the enemy hath persecuted my soul; he hath smitten my life down to the ground; he hath made me to dwell in darkness, as those that have been long dead.
\vs Psa 143:4 Therefore is my spirit overwhelmed within me; my heart within me is desolate.
\vs Psa 143:5 I remember the days of old; I meditate on all thy works; I muse on the work of thy hands.

\vs Psa 143:12 And of thy mercy cut off mine enemies, and destroy all them that afflict my soul: for I \bibemph{am} thy servant.

\vs Psa 144:4 Man is like to vanity: his days \bibemph{are} as a shadow that passeth away.
\vs Psa 144:5 Bow thy heavens, O \textsc{Lord}, and come down: touch the mountains, and they shall smoke.

\vs Psa 144:11 Rid me, and deliver me from the hand of strange children, whose mouth speaketh vanity, and their right hand \bibemph{is} a right hand of falsehood:
\vs Psa 144:12 That our sons \bibemph{may be} as plants grown up in their youth; \bibemph{that} our daughters \bibemph{may be} as corner stones, polished \bibemph{after} the similitude of a palace:
\fn{polished: Heb. cut.}
\vs Psa 144:13 \bibemph{That} our garners \bibemph{may be} full, affording all manner of store: \bibemph{that} our sheep may bring forth thousands and ten thousands in our streets:
\fn{all...: Heb. from kind to kind.}
\vs Psa 144:14 \bibemph{That} our oxen \bibemph{may be} strong to labour; \bibemph{that there be} no breaking in, nor going out; that \bibemph{there be} no complaining in our streets.
\fn{strong...: Heb. able to bear burdens, or, loaden with flesh.}
\vs Psa 144:15 Happy \bibemph{is that} people, that is in such a case: \bibemph{yea}, happy \bibemph{is that} people, whose God \bibemph{is} the \textsc{Lord}.
\vs Psa 145:1 David's \bibemph{Psalm} of praise. I will extol thee, my God, O king; and I will bless thy name for ever and ever.
\vs Psa 145:2 Every day will I bless thee; and I will praise thy name for ever and ever.
\vs Psa 145:3 Great \bibemph{is} the \textsc{Lord}, and greatly to be praised; and his greatness \bibemph{is} unsearchable.
\fn{and his...: Heb. and of his greatness there is no search.}
\vs Psa 145:4 One generation shall praise thy works to another, and shall declare thy mighty acts.
\vs Psa 145:5 I will speak of the glorious honour of thy majesty, and of thy wondrous works.
\fn{works: Heb. things, or, words.}
\vs Psa 145:6 And \bibemph{men} shall speak of the might of thy terrible acts: and I will declare thy greatness.
\fn{declare: Heb. declare it.}
\vs Psa 145:7 They shall abundantly utter the memory of thy great goodness, and shall sing of thy righteousness.
\vs Psa 145:8 The \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} gracious, and full of compassion; slow to anger, and of great mercy.
\fn{of great...: Heb. great in mercy.}
\vs Psa 145:9 The \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} good to all: and his tender mercies \bibemph{are} over all his works.
\vs Psa 145:10 All thy works shall praise thee, O \textsc{Lord}; and thy saints shall bless thee.
\vs Psa 145:11 They shall speak of the glory of thy kingdom, and talk of thy power;
\vs Psa 145:12 To make known to the sons of men his mighty acts, and the glorious majesty of his kingdom.
\vs Psa 145:13 Thy kingdom \bibemph{is} an everlasting kingdom, and thy dominion \bibemph{endureth} throughout all generations.
\fn{an...: Heb. a kingdom of all ages.}
\vs Psa 145:14 The \textsc{Lord} upholdeth all that fall, and raiseth up all \bibemph{those that be} bowed down.
\vs Psa 145:15 The eyes of all wait upon thee; and thou givest them their meat in due season.
\fn{wait...: or, look unto.}
\vs Psa 145:16 Thou openest thine hand, and satisfiest the desire of every living thing.
\vs Psa 145:17 The \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} righteous in all his ways, and holy in all his works.
\fn{holy: or, merciful, or, bountiful.}
\vs Psa 145:18 The \textsc{Lord} \bibemph{is} nigh unto all them that call upon him, to all that call upon him in truth.
\vs Psa 145:19 He will fulfil the desire of them that fear him: he also will hear their cry, and will save them.
\vs Psa 145:20 The \textsc{Lord} preserveth all them that love him: but all the wicked will he destroy.
\vs Psa 145:21 My mouth shall speak the praise of the \textsc{Lord}: and let all flesh bless his holy name for ever and ever.
\vs Psa 146:1 Praise ye the \textsc{Lord}. Praise the \textsc{Lord}, O my soul.
\fn{Praise ye...: Heb. Hallelujah.}
\vs Psa 146:2 While I live will I praise the \textsc{Lord}: I will sing praises unto my God while I have any being.
\vs Psa 146:3 Put not your trust in princes, \bibemph{nor} in the son of man, in whom \bibemph{there is} no help.
\fn{help: or, salvation.}
\vs Psa 146:4 His breath goeth forth, he returneth to his earth; in that very day his thoughts perish.
\vs Psa 146:5 Happy \bibemph{is he} that \bibemph{hath} the God of Jacob for his help, whose hope \bibemph{is} in the \textsc{Lord} his God:
\vs Psa 146:6 Which made heaven, and earth, the sea, and all that therein \bibemph{is}: which keepeth truth for ever:
\vs Psa 146:7 Which executeth judgment for the oppressed: which giveth food to the hungry. The \textsc{Lord} looseth the prisoners:
\vs Psa 146:8 The \textsc{Lord} openeth \bibemph{the eyes of} the blind: the \textsc{Lord} raiseth them that are bowed down: the \textsc{Lord} loveth the righteous:
\vs Psa 146:9 The \textsc{Lord} preserveth the strangers; he relieveth the fatherless and widow: but the way of the wicked he turneth upside down.
\vs Psa 146:10 The \textsc{Lord} shall reign for ever, \bibemph{even} thy God, O Zion, unto all generations. Praise ye the \textsc{Lord}.
\vs Psa 147:1 Praise ye the \textsc{Lord}: for \bibemph{it is} good to sing praises unto our God; for \bibemph{it is} pleasant; \bibemph{and} praise is comely.
\vs Psa 147:2 The \textsc{Lord} doth build up Jerusalem: he gathereth together the outcasts of Israel.
\vs Psa 147:3 He healeth the broken in heart, and bindeth up their wounds.
\fn{wounds: Heb. griefs.}
\vs Psa 147:4 He telleth the number of the stars; he calleth them all by \bibemph{their} names.
\vs Psa 147:5 Great \bibemph{is} our Lord, and of great power: his understanding \bibemph{is} infinite.
\fn{his...: Heb. of his understanding there is no number.}
\vs Psa 147:6 The \textsc{Lord} lifteth up the meek: he casteth the wicked down to the ground.
\vs Psa 147:7 Sing unto the \textsc{Lord} with thanksgiving; sing praise upon the harp unto our God:
\vs Psa 147:8 Who covereth the heaven with clouds, who prepareth rain for the earth, who maketh grass to grow upon the mountains.
\vs Psa 147:9 He giveth to the beast his food, \bibemph{and} to the young ravens which cry.
\vs Psa 147:10 He delighteth not in the strength of the horse: he taketh not pleasure in the legs of a man.
\vs Psa 147:11 The \textsc{Lord} taketh pleasure in them that fear him, in those that hope in his mercy.
\vs Psa 147:12 Praise the \textsc{Lord}, O Jerusalem; praise thy God, O Zion.
\vs Psa 147:13 For he hath strengthened the bars of thy gates; he hath blessed thy children within thee.
\vs Psa 147:14 He maketh peace \bibemph{in} thy borders, \bibemph{and} filleth thee with the finest of the wheat.
\fn{He...: Heb. Who maketh thy border peace. finest...: Heb. fat of wheat.}
\vs Psa 147:15 He sendeth forth his commandment \bibemph{upon} earth: his word runneth very swiftly.
\vs Psa 147:16 He giveth snow like wool: he scattereth the hoarfrost like ashes.
\vs Psa 147:17 He casteth forth his ice like morsels: who can stand before his cold?
\vs Psa 147:18 He sendeth out his word, and melteth them: he causeth his wind to blow, \bibemph{and} the waters flow.
\vs Psa 147:19 He sheweth his word unto Jacob, his statutes and his judgments unto Israel.
\fn{his word: Heb. his words.}
\vs Psa 147:20 He hath not dealt so with any nation: and \bibemph{as for his} judgments, they have not known them. Praise ye the \textsc{Lord}.
\vs Psa 148:1 Praise ye the \textsc{Lord}. Praise ye the \textsc{Lord} from the heavens: praise him in the heights.
\fn{Praise ye the \textsc{Lord}. Praise: Heb. Hallelujah, etc.}
\vs Psa 148:2 Praise ye him, all his angels: praise ye him, all his hosts.
\vs Psa 148:3 Praise ye him, sun and moon: praise him, all ye stars of light.
\vs Psa 148:4 Praise him, ye heavens of heavens, and ye waters that \bibemph{be} above the heavens.
\vs Psa 148:5 Let them praise the name of the \textsc{Lord}: for he commanded, and they were created.
\vs Psa 148:6 He hath also stablished them for ever and ever: he hath made a decree which shall not pass.
\vs Psa 148:7 Praise the \textsc{Lord} from the earth, ye dragons, and all deeps:
\vs Psa 148:8 Fire, and hail; snow, and vapour; stormy wind fulfilling his word:
\vs Psa 148:9 Mountains, and all hills; fruitful trees, and all cedars:
\vs Psa 148:10 Beasts, and all cattle; creeping things, and flying fowl:
\fn{flying...: Heb. birds of wing.}
\vs Psa 148:11 Kings of the earth, and all people; princes, and all judges of the earth:
\vs Psa 148:12 Both young men, and maidens; old men, and children:
\vs Psa 148:13 Let them praise the name of the \textsc{Lord}: for his name alone is excellent; his glory \bibemph{is} above the earth and heaven.
\fn{excellent: Heb. exalted.}
\vs Psa 148:14 He also exalteth the horn of his people, the praise of all his saints; \bibemph{even} of the children of Israel, a people near unto him. Praise ye the \textsc{Lord}.
\vs Psa 149:1 Praise ye the \textsc{Lord}. Sing unto the \textsc{Lord} a new song, \bibemph{and} his praise in the congregation of saints.
\fn{Praise...: Heb. Hallelujah.}
\vs Psa 149:2 Let Israel rejoice in him that made him: let the children of Zion be joyful in their King.
\vs Psa 149:3 Let them praise his name in the dance: let them sing praises unto him with the timbrel and harp.
\fn{in...: or, with the pipe.}
\vs Psa 149:4 For the \textsc{Lord} taketh pleasure in his people: he will beautify the meek with salvation.
\vs Psa 149:5 Let the saints be joyful in glory: let them sing aloud upon their beds.
\vs Psa 149:6 \bibemph{Let} the high \bibemph{praises} of God \bibemph{be} in their mouth, and a twoedged sword in their hand;
\fn{mouth: Heb. throat.}
\vs Psa 149:7 To execute vengeance upon the heathen, \bibemph{and} punishments upon the people;
\vs Psa 149:8 To bind their kings with chains, and their nobles with fetters of iron;
\vs Psa 149:9 To execute upon them the judgment written: this honour have all his saints. Praise ye the \textsc{Lord}.
\vs Psa 150:1 Praise ye the \textsc{Lord}. Praise God in his sanctuary: praise him in the firmament of his power.
\fn{Praise ye...: Heb. Hallelujah.}
\vs Psa 150:2 Praise him for his mighty acts: praise him according to his excellent greatness.
\vs Psa 150:3 Praise him with the sound of the trumpet: praise him with the psaltery and harp.
\fn{trumpet: or, cornet.}
\vs Psa 150:4 Praise him with the timbrel and dance: praise him with stringed instruments and organs.
\fn{dance: or, pipe.}
\vs Psa 150:5 Praise him upon the loud cymbals: praise him upon the high sounding cymbals.
\vs Psa 150:6 Let every thing that hath breath praise the \textsc{Lord}. Praise ye the \textsc{Lord}.
